Bhāskara Bhagavadāśayānusaraṇabhāsya

bhāskara bhagavadāśayānusaraṇabhāsya

bhāskarabhāṣyasya prathamapṛṣṭhasya dve vākye ānandajayatīrthakṛtagītāṭīkāyā uddhṛte । tayoḥ sāhāyyena bhāskarakṛtagītābhāṣyasya luptaprathamapṛṣṭhasya viṣayonumātuṃ śakyate । te vākye śāstraprayojanābhidhāne prastute avatāraprayojanābhidhānam asaṃgatam । jñānakarmasamuccayasādhyatvān mokṣasya tatpratipādanāya gītārambhe na dharmādipratipādanārtham । tadarthānāṃ manvādidharmaśāstrāṇāṃ sanakādiyogaśāstrāṇāṃ ca pratikālaṃ vidyamānatvāt । jayatīrthaṭīkāyām yad āha bhāskara iti vākyād anantaram upalabhete ime vākye । tatra prathamaṃ vākyaṃ ṣaṣṭhe pṛṣṭhe dvitīyaṃ vākyaṃ navame pṛṣṭhe ।

śrībhagavadgītāyā bhagavadbhāskarakṛtabhagavadāśayānusaraṇābhidhānabhāṣyam ।

idaṃ hi triṣu lokeṣu mahajjñānaṃ pratiṣṭitam ।
vistaraiś ca samāsaiś ca dhāryate yad dvijātibhiḥ ।।

yodhīte bhārata puṇyaṃ brāhmaṇo niyatavrataḥ ।
śrāvayec ca mahāpuṇyaṃ tasya dharmaḥ sanātanaḥ ।।

taponiyamam āsthāya kṛtam etan maharṣiṇā ।
tasmān niyamasaṃyuktair adhyeyaṃ brāhmaṇair idam ।
kṛṣṇaproktam imāṃ puṇyāṃ bhāratīm uttamāṃ kathām ।
śrāvayiṣyanti ye viprā ye ca śroṣyanti mānavāḥ ।।

ityevamādau śrāvayiṣyanti ityatra vipragrahaṇād dvijātīnām evādhyayane śravaṇe cādhikāro darśitaḥ । itareṣāṃ tu ye tu śrośyanti mānavā iti mānavagrahaṇāc chravaṇa evādhikāraḥ śāstravirodhāc cādhyayane nādhikāraḥ ।

tathā coktaṃ śukotpattau

sarvas taratu durgāṇi sarvo bhadrāṇi paśyatu ।
śrāvayec caturo varṇān kṛtvā brāhmaṇam agrataḥ ।।

iti cāturvarṇyamadhyapātinaḥ śūdrasya śravaṇamātraṃ vidhīyate । rāmāyaṇe hy ayam evārtho viśeṣeṇa pratipāditaḥ

paṭhaṃ dvijo vāgṛṣabhatvam īyāt
syāt kṣatriyo bhūmipatitvam amīyāt ।
vaiśyas tathā sarvadhanatvam īyāc
chṛṇvan hi śūdropi mahattvam īyāt ।।

ity atretihāsaśravaṇamātram eva śūdrāder nirṇītam । tatrāpi cākhyāyikāmātraśravaṇe na tu rahasyavedāntārthapratipādanapradeśeṣu sanatsujātīyagītāmokṣadharmādiṣu tasya vedādhyayanaśravaṇatadarthaparijñānatadanuṣṭānānāṃ pratiṣedhasmaraṇāt । tathā ca manusmṛtau

na śūdrāya matiṃ dadyān nocciṣṭaṃ na haviṣkṛtam ।
na cāsyopadiśed dharmaṃ na cāsya vratam ādiśet ।।

iti cādṛṣṭārthamatidānadharmopadeśādiniṣedhāt । na ca svamanīṣikayā brāhmaṇopadeśam anapekṣya pustakādes tadvivaraṇād vā tadartham adhigamya karmānutiṣṭhataḥ phalāya tad bhavati pratyuta śāstraniṣiddhenānupanītena gṛhītaṃ śāstrajñānam anarthotpādakam । yato nyāyasmṛtyācārāvirodhī yaḥ padārthaḥ sa śāstrārthaḥ । tatra nyāyaḥ yathotkṛṣṭanikṛṣṭavarṇayor na karma tulyatā tathā na sadṛśadharmatā yuktā । tad uktam

apavarge adhikāras tu strīśūdrāṇāṃ bhaved yadi । jātyutkarṣo dvijātīnām anarthāya tato bhavet ।। iti ।

smṛtir api

viduṣā brāhmaṇenedam adhyetavyaṃ prayatnataḥ । śiṣyebhyaś ca pravaktavyaṃ samyaṅ nānyena kenacit ।। iti ।

ācāraś cāryyadeśe jñānaśāstraśravaṇe tasyāpravṛttyaivāveditaḥ yaḥ śāstravidhim utsṛjya ityādinā cehāpi pratyayasya pratipādayiṣyamāṇatvāt । ata evoktam

adhikāraṃ vinā yas tu gṛḥṇāti śāstram anyathā ।
tat tyaktvā pāvanaṃ kṛtvā svadharmaṃ punar āśrayet ।।

pāvanaṃ prāyaścittam । manunā cādhyayanaśravaṇatadarthānuṣṭhānayuktasyaiva dvijāter jñānedhikāro darśitaḥ

adhītya vidhivad vedān putrān utpādya dharmataḥ ।
iṣṭvā ca śaktito yajñair mano mokṣe niveśayet ।।

tadrahitasya dvijāter api mokṣedhikāro noktaḥ

anadhītya dvijo vedam anutpādya tathā prajām ।
aniṣṭvā caiva yajñaiś ca mokṣam icchan vrajaty adhaḥ ।।

śūdrasya ca vasiṣṭamunināpy upanayanādibhir asaṃskāryatvaṃ pratipāditam ।

tathā ca tatroktam gāyatryā brāhmaṇam asṛjata triṣṭubhā rājanyaṃ jagatyā vaiśyaṃ na kenacic chandasā śūdram ity asaṃskāryo vijñāyata iti । kiṃ ca bhagavatā sākṣād dharmeṇāpi śāpavaśād vidurākhyaśūdrajanmanātmajñānaviṣaye dhṛtarāṣṭrapṛṣṭena śūdrayonisthatvād anadhikāritvaṃ manyamānena vedārthopadeśārthaṃ sanatsujātam ānayatā tatrānadhikāro darśitaḥ । tathā ca tenaiva tatroktam

śūdrayonāv ahaṃāto nāto anyad vaktum utsahe ।
brāhmīṃ hi yonim āpannaḥ suguhyam api yo vadet ।।

na tena garhyo devānāṃ tasmād etad bravīmi te ।।

evaṃ ca brāhmaṇayonivyatiriktānyayonijo yadi guhyaṃ vedārthaṃ vadati tadā devādibhir asau garhyate niṣiddhasevanena pāpayogān narakādau prakṣipyata ity arthaḥ ।

kumārasya tu yā buddhir veda tāṃ śāśvatīm aham ।

kumārasyānujjhitabrahmacaryasya sanatsujātasya yā buddhir yaj jñānam bodhanaṃ buddhiḥ tām ahaṃ veda । niratiśayajñānayukto asāv iti jātis maratvāj jānāmi । kiṃ tu nikṛṣṭajātisthatvenānadhikārād vaktuṃ na śaknomi ।

yas te guhyān prakāśāṃś ca sarvān hṛdayasaṃśrayān ।
pravakṣyati mahārāja sarvabuddhimatāṃ varaḥ ।।

kiṃ bahunā sāṅkhyādiśāstreṣv api brāhmaṇānām evāsuriprabhṛtīnāṃ bhagavadbhiḥ kapilamunipramukhair mahātmabhir jñānopadeśaḥ kṛto nānyasya । ity ato api na śūdrāder jñāne adhikāro asti । tasmāt sakaletihāsapurāṇadharmaśāstrādipaurvāparyaparyālocanenāyam eva vākyārtha iti sthitam । śāstraikasamadhigamyā kilādhikāravyavasthā dharmādharmavyavasthāvan na pramāṇāntaragamyā । ko hi nāma bhagavato dharmasya hetuto niścayam avadhārituṃ śaktaḥ । hetutaś ca dharmavyavasthāyāṃ kariṣyamāṇāyāṃ hetvanavasthānād dharmānavasthānam api prasajyeteti । ataś ca

striyo vaiśyās tathā śūdrās te api yānti parāṃ gatim ।

itīdam api liṅgam ।

kiṃ punar brāhmaṇāḥ puṇyā bhaktā rājarṣayas tathā ।

ity api kṛtabrāhmaṇarājarṣiviṣayakapravartakavidhiprarocanārthavādatvena draṣṭavyam na tu svārthapratipādanaparam । liṃ gaṃ hi pramāṇāntarataḥ prāptasyaivārthasya dyotakaṃ bhavati nāprāptasyāprāpakam te api yānti ity abhidhāyakavartamānakālavācipratyayāntaśabdanirdeśāt pūrvoktavidhisāpekṣatvena sākāṅkṣatvāc ca । vāstavena rūpeṇānyaparaṃ yadvākyaṃ śabdena cānyārthapratipādakaṃ talliṃ gam ।

vidhiniṣedhaśeṣatayā tv arthavādānāṃ pravṛttiḥ na tu svārthapratipādakatayā viṣabhakṣaṇādivākyavad arthavādavākyānāṃ parārthatvāt svārthe tātparyābhāvād anyaparatvād vidhivihitārthastāvakatayā niṣiddhārthaninditṛtayā ca pravṛtter iti । etac ca nipuṇataram atraiva navame adhyāye vakṣyāmaḥ । anyac ca

jñānaṃ vijñānam āstikyaṃ brāhmaṃ karma svabhāvajam ।

iti brāhmaṇasyaiva bhagavān dharmaḥ śreyaḥsādhanam iti darśayiṣyati । yato adikṛtānām āryyāṇāṃ dvijātīnām eva śrutivihitanityanaimittikakarmakṣapitakalmaṣamohabhayāyāsānām upāsyamāna eṣa paramātmātigrahanaḥ saṃsāropaplavarahito ananto akṣayo anādir ajo amanomayo nirvikalpo apāpaḥ sarvalokeśa eka eva sarvaśarīrāvasthitaḥ sarvapadārthāvasthitaḥ satatāsāditavimalabhāvaḥ sarvaśaktiḥ svaśaktivibhavajanitasakalādvaitasadrūpaḥ pratyakṣo bhavati । sādhanavīryāt teṣām eva hi śrutismṛtyuktapraśastayamaniyamapramukhayogāṅgādisambhavād upāsakatvena ca teṣām eva niyamāt ta eva ca tam ātmānaṃ paśyanti । tathā cānukramaṇyādāv api bhagavatā vyāsenoktam

yat tad yativarā muktā dhyānayogabalānvitāḥ ।
pratibimbam ivādarśe paśyanty ātmany avasthitam ।।

yad akṣaraṃ vedavido vadanti viśanti yad yataro vītarāgāḥ ।

ityādinā viśiṣṭajātīyāśramiviṣaye dhānenātmopalambhanam upapannaṃ bhavatīti pradarśitam ।

nāhaṃ prakāśaḥ sarvasya yogam āyāsam āvṛtaḥ ।

iti bhagavān eva śūdrāder ātmadarśanābhāvaṃ pratipādayiṣyati । dvaipāyano api

śāntātmāno dvijaśreṣṭhāḥ prāpnuvanti tadakṣaram iti ।

ataḥ śūdrader dhyānādinā kriyamāṇenāpi na tatprāptir bhavati niyamavidher bhaṃ gabhayād akhilavidyāyā adhikṛtānuṣṭhitāyā eva phaladātṛtvāvagamāt । avihitena tūtkṛṣṭajātīyakarmaṇā yogena jñānena ca śūdrādir utkarṣa netuṃ na śakyate । na hi kārṣṇāyasaṃ bhūyo apy analasantāpanena suvarṇatvam āpādayituṃ śakyam । kriyā hi dravyaṃ vilāpayati nādravyam । vedasmṛtiliṃ gebhyaḥ kila brāhmaṇasyaiva mukhyayā vṛttyā mokṣādhikāro avagamyate na kṣatriyavaiśyayoḥ yogābhyāsādhikāre saty api । tad uktam

bandhamokṣavyavasthityāṃ pramāṇaṃ codanā svataḥ ।
vedasyānatiśaṅkyatvād anapekṣatayā tathā ।।

vidhir niyuṅkte adhikṛtam uttamaṃ śreyase sadā ।
aśāstrīyāt phalāsaṃ gāt svayaṃ kāmī hi badhyate ।।

apunarjanmasambandho yasmāc chabdaikagocaraḥ ।। iti ।

yat tu rājarṣīṇāṃ janakaśvapatipravāhaṇaprabhṛtīnāṃ mahābhāratādau mokṣaśravaṇaṃ tat kasyāñcid viśiṣṭāyām avasthāyāṃ pravṛttayāgatvena yajamānānāṃ tu mantrāptasambodhāvirbhāve sati na sarvadā । yāgasthānāṃ hi teṣāṃ brāhmaṇatvaṃ śrūyate । tathā ca śatapathaśrutiḥ

sā yāṃ kāñcana yajate brahmaiva bhūtvā yajata iti ।

tadvadhe ca smṛtau brahmahatyāprāyaścittam āmnātam

yāgasthakṣatriyaṃ hantā cared brahmahaṇivratam iti ।

evaṃ ca kṣatriyavaiśyayor api na tathā brāhmaṇena tulyatayā mokṣe adhikāraḥ tasmād dvijātīnām eva । yogābhyāsena tu prayatamānānām apy anadhikṛtānāṃ śūdrādīnāṃ vidyamāne hṛdayapuṇḍarīke api nādhikāraḥ tiraścām iveti । kiṃ ca yathā saura āloko divācarāṇāṃ eva bhūtānām ākṣaṃ janayati na tu rātricaraṇāṃ kauśikādīnāṃ tulye api prakāśadātṛtve tadvat ।

yad ayaṃ samudāyārthaḥ garbhādhānādisaṃskārasaṃskṛto yo yathāvidhyupanīto yathāśakticīrṇavedavratādiko arthāvabodhaparyantavedādhyayanasaṃskṛto gṛhād vanaṃ vanān maunam āśramāṇāṃ samuccayam aṅgīkṛtya vikalpe vā brahmacaryād yathāruci śānto

dāntaḥ śraddadhānaḥ so apavarge adhikārabhāk yataḥ sūtrakāraḥ svadharmāṇāṃ vidhyarthatvaṃ na manyate

karmaṇāṃ sahakāritvaṃ sahaiveti śruter matam ।
na hy anāśramiṇo vedo yogyatvam iha manyate ।।

devopakāraḥ kartavyo devān bhāvayateti ha ।

ataḥ
yāvajjīvaṃ prakurvīta svakarmāṇi yathāvidhi ।
saṃskurvīta svadharmaiś ca smṛtito avagataṃ tathā ।।

mahāyajñaiś ca yajñaiś ca aṣṭāv ātmaguṇā iti catvāriṃśat saṃskārā iti ca । api ca saṃyatānām eva yajñādayaś ca śrūyate । tattvaprakaraṇe kila

vidyayāśramiṇo yogo nānyasyeti śruter matam ।।

karmaṇā tasya vijñānaṃ tadbhāvam upanīyate । paścād āpannatadbhāvo deham etaṃ vimuñcati ।। iti ।

tathā cātra vājasaneyināṃ yajñasūtrakāraḥ kātyāyano adhikāravivekam uktavān athāto adhikāraḥ iti । athaśabda ānantaryārthaḥ । ataḥśabdo hetvarthaḥ । yato vedādhyayanaṃ pūrvavṛttam atas tadarthajñānāvasare prathamam adhikāro nirūpyate kasyātrādhikāra iti । adhikāraśabdasyaiva tāvat

ko arthaḥ ayam ucyate

abhyupagatāgamaprāmāṇyānāṃ puruṣāṇāṃ śāstreṇa yady asya kartavyatayā vidhīyate tatra tasyāgamapāratantryeṇānuṣṭhānāṅgīkaraṇam । tathā yac chāstreṇa niṣidhyate na kalañjaṃ bhakṣayet ityādi tatra pratiṣidhyamānakriyasya mukhyasyādhikāriṇo jighatsāprayuktarāganibandhanaḥ kalañjabhakṣaṇapravṛttiniṣedhārthaḥ śāstrapāratantryeṇaiva । akāraṇasaṅkalpa audāsīnyāśrayaṇaṃ cādhikāraḥ । tad uktaṃ bhaṭṭena

vidhinā yujyate yatra na hanyān na pibed iti ।
tatraudāsīnyavastv eva pratipattāvalambane ।।

audāsīnyaṃ pravṛttyuparamo vyāpārābhāvaḥ svāmitvena yo vyāpārasyādhikāras tasyābhāva ity uktaḥ । tenaitad uktaṃ bhavati idam agnihotrādi karma matsambandhitayā vihitam ato mama kartavyam । idaṃ ca parahiṃsādi tathaiva niṣiddham ato na kartavyam iti brāhmaṇādir avagacchati । eṣa adhikāraśabdārtha iti । tad uktam 

yatra yasyādhikāro asti nitye naimittike ca saḥ । badhyate na hi sarvo hi śāstrātikramabandhanaiḥ ।। iti ।

śāstradṛṣṭyādhikāro nirūpyata ity atra niyojyatvaṃ tāvad āha brāhmaṇarājanyavaiśyānāṃ śrutiḥ । tathā ca 

vasante brāhmaṇenādhyeyo grīṣmo rājanyena śaradi vaiśyena iti śrutiḥ । kiṃ ca aṅgahīnāśrotriyaṣaṇḍapatitaśūdravarjam ity aṅgahīnānām andhamūkapaṅgvādīnām ājyāvekṣaṇopasthānavacanaviṣṇukramaṇādiṣv asāmarthyāt karmaṇi nādhikāraḥ । aśrotriyasya sāṅgavedādhyayanavijñānarahitasya yathāvac chāstrānavabodhe mantrāṇāṃ devatādisatattvānagamād anadhikāraḥ । uktaṃ ca 

vaidhe kṛtārthakaṃ śāstram avaidhaṃ nānuśāsti hi । iti । ṣaṇḍasya klībasya pūrvajanmārjitaduṣṭakarmasūcakatvena duṣkṛtitvād anadhikāro dāyādivibhāgapratiṣedhāt tasya karmaṇāṃ ca dravyādisādhyatvād vibhavayuktasya putriṇa ādhānādisaṃyogāt klībasyāputriṇo nādhikāraḥ । tathā coktam

patitavyādhiśūdrāṇāṃ yāvad vacanam iṣyate । adhikāro na sarvasmin namuceḥ ṣaṇḍakasya ca ।। iti ।

patito brahmahādiḥ । tasyānadhikāro mahāpātakitvāt । śūdrasya cānadhikāraḥ । kuto athātaḥśabdābhyāṃ vedādhyayanānantaryadyotakābhyāṃ yasya vedādhyayanaṃ tasya karmaṇy adhikāra iti jñāpitatvāt । karmādhikṛtasya ca jñāne adhikāro jñānena karmaṇaḥ samuccayanāt । tathā coktam 

niḥśreyasāyādhikṛtān vidyā karma vyabodhayat ।
karmaśrutir evānuśāsti tān ।। iti

tasmāc chūdro yajñe anavakḷpta iti tasya karmaparyudāsād mūrkhatvāc ca । mūrkhatvaṃ ca tasyopanayanavedādhyayanatadarthādhigamapratiṣedhāt । tathā ca gautamaḥ

śūdraś caturtho varṇa ekajātir na ca saṃskāram arhati । iti

tathā athāsya vedam upaśṛṇvatas trapujatubhyāṃ śrotrapratipūraṇam udāharaṇe jihvocchedo dhāraṇe hi śarīrabheda iti ।

vaśiṣṭo apy āha

padyur vā eṣa śmaśānaṃ yac chūdras tasmāc chūdrasamīpe nādhyetavyam iti ।

na cānadhikṛtena kṛtaṃ karma śāstrapratyayaṃ phalaṃ sampādayitum arhati śāstralakṣaṇatvāt phalasambandhasyotkarṣāpakarṣayoś ca । uktaṃ ca

avaidhatvād anagnitvān nādhikāro asti karmasu ।
śrauteṣv avaidhatāpy asya vedādhyayanavarjanāt ।।

yaḥ svādhyāyam adhīyīta kuryāt karma sa eva tat ।
avaiduṣyād ataḥ śūdraḥ karmaṇaḥ paryudasyate ।।

kiṃ sarvebhyaḥ na ।

smārtaṃ ca pitṛyajñādiṃ śūdraḥ kuryād yathāśrutam ।
tad vidvattām avāptyaiva kathañcid dvijasaṃśrayāt ।।

śrautād adhikṛtānāṃ tu yāvadvihitasevanāt ।
niṣiddhavarjanāc cāpi pāramparyeṇa sadgatiḥ ।।

hīnād dhīnāc chubhaṃ janma pāramparyeṇa yad abhavet ।
anugrahaḥ sa eṣo asya puṃsaḥ śrutikṛto mataḥ ।।

tasmāc chūdrādīnāṃ karmaṇy anadhikārād asmin śāstre etatpratipādite ca yogābhyāse nāsty adhikāra iti । kiṃ ca

ātmābhyāso api nāsyāsti vipraseveti hi smṛteḥ ।
teṣām evānukampeti dvijāter adhikāritā ।।

teṣām evetiśabdena brāhmaṇasya stutiḥ kṛtā ।
śūdrayonāv ahaṃāta ityādi bahu dṛśyate ।।

evamādi bahuvākyajātaṃ bhārate tatra tatra dṛśyate granthagauravabhayāt tu na likhyata iti । uktaṃ ca

adhikāry eva śāstrārthaṃ śaktaḥ sādhayituṃ yataḥ । tatsiddhāv aprabhutvaṃ hi jñātātrānadhikāritā ।। iti ।

itthaṃ śūdrāder mokṣābhāvād dharmārthakāmalakṣaṇe trivarge ca puruṣārthe sati hīnādhikārād gītāśāstrādes tenādhyayanādi na kartavyam । yasmād yo yatrānadhikṛtaḥ sa tadiṣṭabuddhyāpi anutiṣṭhan na kevalaṃ tatphalaṃ na prāpnoti yāvad apareṇa pratyavāyenāpi yujyate । yathā rājādinā yaḥ kutracid apy aniyuktaḥ puruṣaḥ sa tadīyagrāmādau svātantryeṇa grāmavyāpārādi kurvaṃs tasmād rājādeḥ śarīradhanadaṇḍādilakṣaṇaṃ pratyavāyaṃ prāpnoti tathā śāstre api yo yatrānadhikṛtas tadiṣṭārtham api kurvan pratyavaiti । yathā ca ślaiṣmikahitam auṣadhaṃ bhakṣayann ārogyārthaṃ paittiko nairujyaṃ na labhate pratyuta rogaprakopeṇa pīḍyate evam ihāpi boddhavyam । uktaṃ ca

paryudasto hi yo yasmāc chāstrīyād api karmaṇaḥ ।
sa tatrānadhikārī syād dānādau dīkṣito yathā ।।

evaṃ cādhikṛtenānuṣṭhitaṃ karma phalasādhakaṃ na svabuddhyaivānadhikṛteneti śāstraniyamaḥ । etac ca bhagavān eva vakṣyati

yaḥ śāstravidhim utsṛjya vartate kāmakārataḥ ।
na sa siddhim avāpnoti na sukhaṃ na parāṃ gatim ।।

^kṣāvaddharmārthakāmā^ ^hānadhikārādrotāsāstrāde^ ^ssatadaṣṭavuḍryāpi puruṣassa tadīpagrāmodakhātantryeṇa rājñādeḥ ghanadañjādi^ pratyavāyuṃ kṛtastadṛṣṭārthamapi ślauṃ jikahitamauṣadhaṃ yaitikaṃ auṣadhavupi bhakṣayan pratyuta prakopena pīḍryata yavamihāpi vobhdavyam tatrānadhikārī ^dvānādaukṣito ^nuṣṭitaṃ ^sādhakalasvavuḍrauvā^ matsṛjya parā^

yataḥ

pratiṣedham atikramya pratyaveyāt kṛtān naraḥ tasmāt tasyānatikrāntau nityaṃ yuktataro bhavet ।। iti ।

yataḥ kila sarveṇa puruṣeṇāvihitānuṣṭhānapratiṣiddhasevananimittajanitapāpahetukavividhanarakarauravāsipatravanakrakacacchedanaśvaśṛgālādikṛmikīṭabhakṣaṇavedanāpūyaśoṇitakardamamajjanādiyāmyayātanāśatādyanarthasaṅkaṭādisantrāsāc charaṇaiṣiṇā sthāvarakīṭapataṅgādiyonisahasrāvartabhramaṇasadyomaraṇajarāvyādhikṣutpipāsābandhanāṅgacchedādiduḥkhabhayocchedakāri śāstrīyaṃ karmānuṣṭhīyate । tat punar utkṛṣṭaṃ karma niṣiddhatvād viruddhaṃ sadgatānugatikatvenādṛṣṭabuddhyānuṣṭhīyamānam apy avihitatvenāśāstrīyatvān na kevalaṃ niṣphalaṃ bhavati yāvat pratyutānadhikṛtatvena pratyavāyakaratvāt paraloke bahuvidhanarakapātādyupadravavṛndotpādakam iti jñātvā śūdrādinā naivātra nityam ātmā kṣapaṇīyaḥ । tathā cehaiva vakṣyati

varaṃ svadharmo viguṇaḥ paradharmāt svanuṣṭhitāt ।
svadharme nidhanaṃ śreyaḥ paradharmo bhyāvahaḥ ।।

varaṃ śreyan । darśayati ca manur api

paradharmeṇa jīvan hi sadyaḥ patati jātitaḥ ।

śūdrajātito api bhraṣṭas tiryagādijātiṃ prāpnotīti vākyārthaḥ ।

vede mantreṣu gṛhyeṣu śrutismṛtiniṣedhataḥ ।
nādhikāro asti śūdrasya purāṇādiṣu bhārata ।।

brāhmaṇaṃ tu puraskṛtya śṛṇvataḥ phalam īritam । striyo vaiśyās tathā śūdrāḥ śuddhāḥ sukham avapnuyuḥ ।। iti ।

yataḥ

tiryagbhyaḥ puruṣāḥ śreṣṭhāḥ kāryākāryavivekataḥ ।
tantrādhikārāt tebhyo api dvijā vedādhikārataḥ ।।

adhikārāt pravacane tebhyaḥ śreṣṭhā dvijottamāḥ । śrutyā smṛtyādhikārārthaṃ śraiṣṭyam eṣāṃ prakāśate ।। iti ।

tathā ca manuḥ

brāhmaṇo jāyamāno hi pṛthivyām adhijāyate ।
īśvaraḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ dharmakośasya guptaye ।।

tad evam uktasambandhābhidheyaprayojanaṃ pratipāditādhikāraviśeṣam etacchāstraṃ vyākhyātuṃ śrotuṃ ca yogyam iti । ato asya vyākhyānam ārabhyate ।

anekaiś ca vyākhyātṛbhiḥ svapakṣanikṣiptadṛṣṭibhir itas tataḥ kṛṣyamāṇam anavasthām āpadyamānaṃ gītāśāstram apavargaprāptyupadeśamahāprayojanam । ataḥ bhagavato abhiprete sanmārge sthāpayitum ayaṃ yatnaḥ kriyate ।

nanv itihāsapurāṇānāṃ pauruṣeyatvād apavargaprāptilakṣaṇe atīndriyārthe na svataḥ prāmāṇyaṃ sambhavati । satyam etat । kiṃ tu mantrārthavādās teṣāṃ mūlam iti nyāyavidbhiḥ sthāpitam । atas tetra mūlaṃ syuḥ

dharmāṇāṃ viprakīrṇānāṃ vedajñātṛprayatnataḥ ।
kṛtaṃ saṃharaṇaṃ sākṣād dharmāvagatihetukam ।।

vaidikānāṃ hi śabdānāṃ prasthānāt tu vilakṣaṇam ।
smṛtīnāṃ racaneyaṃ hi puṃpraṇītā vilakṣaṇā ।।

bhagavadvyāsādismaraṇaṃ ca svataḥ prāmaṇam eva । te hi sākṣātkṛtadharmatvāt karatalagatāmalakavat sakalaṃ vedārthaṃ pratyakṣeṇaiva paśyanti । tad uktam sākṣātkṛtadharmāṇa ṛṣayo babhūvur iti । na hy asmadādivad vyāsādayo atīndriyam arthaṃ na paśyantīti vaktuṃ śakyam । vidhūtakalmaṣatvād īśvarānugrahād vedārthasya vopanibandhanāc ca sambhavaty evatīndriyārthadarśanaṃ teṣām ity adoṣaḥ ।

itthaṃ sthite arjunasya jñānakarmopadeśaprasaṅgam avatārayituṃ prastutakathāsamāptau kāryāntaraṃ jijñāsur dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ punaḥ sañjayaṃ pṛcchaṃs tāvad āha

dharmakṣetre kurukṣetre sarvakṣtrasamāgame ।
māmakāḥ pāṇḍavāś caiva kim akurvata sañjaya ।।

he sañjaya kurukṣetrākhye deśe dharmaprasavahetutvād dharmasya

kṣetre sthāne sarvakṣatrasamāgame sannidhāne sati matsanbandhinas tanayāḥ pāṇḍuputrāś ca kim akurvata kim anuṣṭhitavanta iti । pūrvaṃ rājaṛṣiṇā tapasyatā tatra dharmaḥ kilopta iti kurukṣetrasya dharmakṣetratvam । atra kurutāto dharmaṃ kṣipraṃ trāṇo bhaviṣyatīti kurukṣetrasya kurukṣetratvam ity āhuḥ paurāṇikāḥ ।।

evaṃ pṛṣṭaḥ sañjaya uvāca

dṛṣṭvā tu pāṇḍavānīkaṃ vyūḍhaṃ duryodhanas tadā ।
ācāryam upasaṅgamya rājā vacanam abravīt ।।

pāṇḍavasainyaṃ vyūḍhaṃ śāstradṛṣṭyā kṛtavinyāsaviśeṣaṃ dṛṣṭvaiva tasmiṃ kāle duryodhano droṇam upasaṅgamya gauravāt 
tatsamīpaṃ prāpya vakṣyamāṇaṃ
viśiṣṭapadakriyāparikalpitarūpaṃ
vākyam uktavān ।।

tadāha

paśyaitāṃ pāṇḍuputrāṇām ācārya mahatīṃ camūm ।
vyūḍhāṃ drapadaputreṇa tava śiṣyeṇa dhīmatā ।।

he ācārya pāṇḍuputrasambandhinīṃ camūṃ mahatīṃ senām aṅgabāhulyād vistīrṇāṃ dhṛṣṭadyumnena vyūhavidhānakuśalena ca vyūḍhāṃ kṛtacaranāviśeṣāṃ paśya । yo hi bhavacchiṣyo buddhimāṃś ca so avaśyam

apratimāṃ vyūharacanāṃ karoti ।
ataḥ pratividhānaparo bhavetyāśayaḥ ।।

kiṃ ca

atra śūrā maheṣvāsā bhīmārjunasamā yudhi ।
yuyudhāno virāṭaś ca drupadaś ca mahārathaḥ ।।

atra asyāṃ senāyām amī śūrā bhayaviṣādān abhijāḥ । tathā maheṣvāsāḥ । iṣavaḥ śarā asyante kṣipyante yais ta iṣvāsāḥ koḍaṇḍāḥ mahānto bṛhantaḥ sudṛḍhāḥ parair abhedyā iṣvāsā dhanūṃṣi yeṣāṃ te maheṣvāsāḥ । atha vā yuddha iṣūn asyantītīṣvāsā dhānuṣkāḥ yuddhakarmaparāḥ । ta eva ca divyāḥ prabhāvattvād dhanur vedakṛtābhiyogatvād anekasaṅgrāmalabdhavijayatvāc ca । mahānta uttamāḥ praśastāḥ । 
tathā yudhi yuddhe bhīmārjunābhyāṃ yoddhṛtvena samās tulyāḥ ।
ke ta ity āha yuyudhānaḥ sātyakiḥ virāṭo drupadaś ca mahārathaḥ ।
mahān preraṇāvaraṇayuddhāpasāraṇāvakāśādidharmayogāt
praśasto ratho yasyāsau mahārathaḥ ।।

kiṃ ca

dhṛṣṭaketuś cekitānaḥ kāśirājaś ca vīryavān ।
purujit kuntibhojaś ca śaibyaś ca narapuṅgavaḥ ।।

^vicāna^ mahārarthaḥ senāyāsamī^ mayaviṣāda^ maheṣāsāḥ arayante kṣipyate ṣaiste draghāsāḥ kodaṃḍāḥ mahānto vṛhantaḥ sudavāḥ paraisamedhā^ dhanuṣi te tathā yuddhādraṣṭūnasyantītīṣvāsā dhānukāḥ karmaraparā prabhāvatvā dekasaṃ^ yoddhatvena yuyudhānastātyakirvirāṭo^ mahānpraraṇāvaraṇā yuddhāpasārāvakāśādidharmayogāt cekitān kuntibhojaiśca

iha sañjñāmātrapradhānā amī śabdā nigadavyākhyātāḥ । tāḥ ato na vyākhyāyogyāḥ । yeṣāṃ tv arthānugame viśeṣa upalabhyate te leśato vyākhyāyante । kāśīnāṃ rājā vīryavān utsāhaśaktyupetaḥ । puru bahu jayatīti purujit । kuntayo janapadāḥ teṣāṃ vāsī kuntibhojaḥ । śivayo janapadās teṣāṃ rājā śaibyaḥ । sa ca śauryādyuttamaguṇayogān narapuṅgavaḥ puruṣaśreṣṭhaḥ ।।

tathā

yudhāmanyuś ca vikrānta uttamaujāś ca vīryavān ।
saubhadro draupadeyāś ca sarva eva mahārathāḥ ।।

vikrānto vīryavān subhadrāsūnur abhimanyuḥ ।।

evaṃ pāṇḍavānīke pradhānanāyakanirddeśaṃ kṛtvā svānīke pradhānanāyakān darśayann āha

asmākaṃ tu viśiṣṭā ye tān nibodha dvijottama ।
nāyakān mama sainyasya sañjñāarthaṃ tān bravīmi te ।।

asmākaṃ ye viśiṣṭāḥ kulaśauryādibhiḥ pradhānās tān sañjñārthaṃ bravīmi । sañjñānaṃ sañjñā । tuśabdaḥ pūrvebhyo 
viśeṣāvadyotanaḥ ।
yuyudhānādayo varākā yuṣmākaṃ purato akiñcitkarā ity arthaḥ ।। 
।।

tāś ca parigaṇayann āha

bhavān bhīṣmaś ca karṇaś ca kṛpaḥ śalyo jayadrathaḥ ।
aśvatthāmā vikarṇaś ca saumadattiś ca vīryavān ।।

na kevalam ete yāvat

anye api bahavaḥ śūrā madarthe tyaktajīvitāḥ ।
nānāśastrapraharaṇā nānāyuddhaviśāradāḥ ।।

nānāprakārāṇi cakrāsimuśalagadāprabhṛtīni śastrāṇi praharaṇāni yeṣāṃ te tathā । nānāvidhagajarathāśvādiyuddhakriyāsu paṇḍitā matkārye ca tyaktajīvitā santy evānye ।।

evam ubhayasainyanāyakanirdeśaṃ kṛtvā sārāsāratāṃ nirūpayann āha

aparyāptaṃ tad asmākaṃ balaṃ bhīmābhirakṣitam ।
paryāptaṃ tv idam eteṣāṃ balaṃ bhīṣmābhirakṣitam ।।

asmākaṃ yathānirdiṣṭasaṃhatānāṃ tatpāṇḍavabalam aparyāptam asamartham abhibhavitum yato bhīmābhirakṣitam bhīmasenena pradhānabhūtena guptam । sa ca bhīmo bhīṣmāpekṣayā kiñcin nyūnatara ity abhiprāyaḥ । idaṃ tv asmākaṃ balam eteṣāṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ paryāptam abhibhavāya vināśane samartham ity arthaḥ yato bhīṣmābhirakṣitam । bhīṣmas tv anekaśastrāstrapārago nirjitānekamahāsamara ityāśayaḥ ।।

।।

mavān kaṇaśca jayadrathaḥ aśvasyāmā saumardanniśca śūrādarthe tyaktā jīvitāḥ viśāradāḥ aṅkoyam nirūpayannāha asmāt parosti valaṃ ^sahitānāṃ kiñcintyūnatara iti ābhiprāyaḥ pāṇḍavāmāṃ paryāsamābhibhavāya vināśane sarmarthamity arthaḥ ^rakṣitaṃ bhīṣmosvanekaśāstrāśsrapāragonekanirjitamahāsamara ityāśayaḥ aṅkoyam āha asmāt parosti

pradhānanirdeśaparyojanam āha

anyeṣu tu sarveṣu yathābhāgam avasthitāḥ ।
bhīṣmam evābhirakṣantu bhavantaḥ sarva eva hi ।।

hi yasmād evambhūtena bhīṣmeṇābhirakṣitam asmākaṃ balaṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ parābhave paryāptam । tato ayaneṣu sarveṣu rathamārgarathyāsu sarvāsu yathābhāgam । yo yo bhāgo yathābhāgam । yo yasyātmīyo bhago aṃśaḥ sa tena rakṣyaḥ । tatra avasthitāḥ santo bhavanto bhīṣmam evābhirakṣantv iti tasmin nāyake sarvato gupte balaṃ parabalapraṇāśane kṣamaṃ bhavatītyāśayaḥ । yady asminn iti ? ayanaṃ kakṣyādi ।।

idānīṃ kāryāntaram upakṣipati sañjayaḥ

tasya sañjanayan harṣaṃ kuruvṛddhaḥ pitāmahaḥ ।
siṃhanādaṃ vinadyoccaiḥ śaṅkhaṃ dadhmau pratāpavān ।।

tasya prakrāntasya balasya duryodhanasya vā harṣam utpādayan bhīṣmaḥ kurūṇāṃ tatkālajānāṃ pūrvavayāḥ siṃhanādam ucchair vinadya tataḥ śaṅkhaṃ dadhmau । siṃhasya iva nādaḥ siṃhanādaḥ taṃ vinadya । sāmānyanader viśeṣanadiḥ karma । siṃhanādaṃ kṛtvety arthaḥ ।।

tataḥ śaṅkhāś ca bheryaś ca paṇavānakagomukhāḥ ।
sahasaivābhyahanyanta sa śabdas tumulo abhavat ।।

anantaraṃ śaṅkhādayaḥ sahasaivāvicāritaniyantraṇam eva abhyahanyanta tāḍitāḥ । sa ca vāditrasaṅghātajaḥ śabdas tumulo mahān

avibhāvyamānāvayavavivekaḥ śrotṛhṛdayadāraṇo abhavat । bheryaḥ kātvāḥ ? ānakastamisvā ? gomukho analambakaḥ ? ।।

tataḥ śvetair hayair yukte mahati syandane sthitau ।
mādhavaḥ pāṇḍavaś caiva divyau śaṅkhau pradadhmatuḥ ।।

mādhavapāṇdavau divyaikarathārūḍhāvacintyaprabhāvau śaṅkhāvatyarthaṃ dhmātavantau ।।

atha pradhānaśaṅkhanāmanirddeśam āha

pāñcajanyaṃ hṛṣīkeśo devadattaṃ dhanañjayaḥ ।
pauṇḍraṃ dadhmau mahāśaṅkhaṃ bhīmakarmā vṛkodaraḥ ।।

anantavijayaṃ rājā kuntīputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ ।
nakulaḥ sahadevaś ca sughoṣamaṇipuṣpakau ।।

pauṇḍraṃ puṇḍradeśajaṃ vipulaṃ vṛkodaro dīptāgnyudaro bhīmakarmā bakahiḍimbādirākṣasavidāraṇādīni bhīṣaṇāni karmāṇi yasya saḥ । kuntīputragrahaṇaṃ praśaṃsārtham । 
pitur asaṃvijñāne mātrā vyavadeśo yady api kutsā rādhāsutasyeva
tasya punaḥ saṃvijñāne praśaṃsaiva dharmaputratvād
yudhiṣṭhirasya ।।

kiṃ ca tathā

kāśyaś ca parameṣvāsaḥ śikhaṇḍī ca mahārathaḥ ।
dhṛṣṭadyumno virāṭaś ca sātyakiś cāparājitaḥ ।।

mahānavibhāvyamāmāvayavavivekaḥ śrottrtṛdayāruṇobhavat gomukhonalavaṅkaḥ śveteha^ pāṃḍavāścaiva diyyaikaratharuṭāvacintyaprabhāvau śaṃvyau^ ^nāmunirdeśa^ karmārvṛkodaraḥ kutīputra dīptāgyadaraḥ yatyukutsā savijñāne praśaṃseva dharmaputrātvāghradhiṣṭirasya

pāñcālaś ca maheṣvāso draupadeyāś ca pañca ye । saubhadraś ca mahābāhuḥ śaṅkhān dadhmuḥ pṛthak pṛthak ।।
sātyakiś cāparājito yuddheṣv iti vijñeyam ।।
kiṃ ca

sa ghoṣo dhārtarāṣṭrāṇāṃ hṛdayāni vyadārayat ।
nabhaś ca pṛthivīṃ caiva tumulo vyanunādayat ।।

yathoktaśaṅkhaghoṣas tumulo duryodhanādīnāṃ hṛdayāny abhinad bhinnavān । yato nabhaś ca pṛthivīṃ caiva sakalam iva vyanunādayat pratiśabddayuktam akārayat vyanunadanaṃ prayuktavān । vyanunādayad ity atra vyatyaye anāḍabhāvaḥ । ihasthānam apadānāṃ nirvacanaṃ granthagauravabhayān na kṛtam । yeṣāṃ ca śabdānām iha lakṣaṇānugamo na dṛśyate teṣāṃ virodho nodbhāvanīyaḥ । yataḥ paramarṣiṇā dvaipāyanenaivoktam alaṅkṛtaṃ śubhaiḥ śabdair iti । atas tad āgamād evāvagamyate śubhaśabdatve vyākaraṇānāṃ bahutve ca kathaṃ pāṇinīyena kevalena virodha udbhāvayituṃ yuktaḥ । itihāsādīnāṃ vaidikārthapratipādanāc chandastulyatvam । tathā cānenaivoktam idaṃ hi devasammitam pavitram idam uttamam iti kārṣṇavedam idaṃ puṇyam iti । tathā anyatrāpi coktam

vedābhedaṃ bhāratasyāvalokya
vyāso vākyair aśvinoḥ stotram ādau ।
samyakkṛtvā vaidikair lakṣaṇoktīr
bhūyo bhūyas tāḥ kariṣyaty atra śeṣāḥ ।।

anyad api kāryāntaram upakṣipann āha

atha vyavasthitān dṛṣṭvā dhārtarāṣṭrān kapidhvajaḥ ।
pravṛtte śastrasampāte dhanur udyamya pāṇḍavaḥ ।।

hṛṣīkeśaṃ tadā vākyam idam āha mahīpate ।

atha śaṅkhaghoṣād anantaram arjuno duryodhanādīn vyavasthitān vividhenākāreṇa yathāvibhavam avasthitān dṛṣṭvā śastrāṇāṃ sampāte pravṛtte dhanur utkṣipya sāvadhāno hṛṣīkeśam idaṃ vakṣyamāṇaṃ vākyam āha । hṛṣīkam itīndriyagrāmākhyā tadīśaṃ hṛṣīkeśam iti । he mahīpata iti dhṛtarāṣṭrodbodhanaṃ sañjayena ।।

kiṃ tad vākyam ity āha
ubhayoḥ senayor madhye rathaṃ sthāpaya me acyuta ।।
yāvad etān nirīkṣe ahaṃ yoddhukāmān avasthitān । kair mayā saha yoddhavyam asmin raṇasamudyame ।।

madhye rathasthāpanād yuyutsāsaṃśayo anumīyate pārthasya । taṃ ca prakaṭayiṣyati । kimarthaṃ senayor madhye rathasthāpanam iti ced ata āha yāvad iti । yāvad ity anena kāryaśeṣaṃ sūcayati

raṇasamudyame yuddhodyoge kaiḥ saha mayā yoddhavyam iti
yoddhukāmān avasthitān dṛṣṭvā tato yathābhipretam
ācariṣyāmītyāśayaḥ ।।

sañjaya uvāca

evam ukto hṛṣīkeśo guḍākeśena bhārata ।
ubhayoḥ senayor madhye sthāpayitvā rathottaram ।।

bhīṣmadroṇapramukhataḥ sarveṣāṃ ca mahīkṣitām । uvāca pārtha paśyaitān samavetān kurūn iti ।।

guḍākā nidrā tadīśena jitanidreṇārjunenaivam ukto bhagavān ubhayoḥ senayor madhye rathaṃ sthāpayitvovāca । kathaṃ sthāpayitvety āha bhīṣmadroṇapramukhataḥ tayoḥ sammukham । ādyāditvāt sārvavibhaktikaḥ tasiḥ । sarveṣāṃ ca rājñāṃ sammukham । kim uvācety āha he pārtha । paśyaitān ekatra samavāyaṃ gatān kurūn iti । 
bhīṣmadroṇābhimukhe rathasthāpanābhiprāyaṃ bhagavān āha
yata pitāmahagurūn prati kadācid asyāyuyutsā syāt tad enaṃ
jñānopadeśena pravartayiṣyāmīti ।।

tatrāpaśyat sthitān pārthaḥ pitṝn atha pitāmahān ।
ācāryān mātulān bhrātṝn putrān pautrān sakhīṃs tathā ।।

śvaśurān suhṛdaś caiva senayor ubhayor api ।

tatra ubhayoḥ senayor madhye pārthaḥ pitrādīn apaśyat । pitṝn pāṇḍudhṛtarāṣṭrabhrātṝn kenāpi vānyena sambandhena tatsthānīyān pitāmahān bhīṣmabāhulīkasomadattaprabhṛtīṃs 
tatsthānīyān vā mātulān śalyaśakunyādīṃś ca
tathaivobhayoḥ senayor anyān svajanān bhrātṝṃ tattulyān sutān
pautrān apaśyat ।।

tān samīkṣya sa kaunteyaḥ sarvān bandhūn avasthitān ।।
kṛpayā parayāviṣṭaḥ sīdamānābravīd idam ।

tān sarvān bandhūn iti samīkṣya na kaścid atra paraḥ sarva eva svajanā ity evaṃ vicārya katham ete mārayituṃ yuvatā iti prakṛṣṭayā karuṇayā vaśīkṛtaḥ । tata eva sīdamāno avasādaṃ gacchan yuddhodyamaṃ jahad idam abravīd iti । vyatyayenātrātmanepadam ।।

kiṃ tad ity āha

dṛṣṭvemān svajananān kṛṣṇa yuyutsūn samavasthitān ।।

sīdanti mama gātrāṇi mukhaṃ ca pariśuṣyati ।
vepathuś ca śarīraṃ me romaharṣaś ca jāyate ।।

saṃsate gāṇḍivaṃ hastāt tvak caiva paridahyate । na ca śaknomy avasthātuṃ bhramatīva ca me manaḥ ।।

he kṛṣṇa imān svān janān yuyutsūn samavāyenāvasthitān dṛṣṭvā me aṅgāni yoddhuṃ necchanti । vepathuḥ kampo

romaharṣaś ca ūrddhvaromatā gāṇḍīvaṃ saṃsate adhaḥpatati । tvak śarīraṃ carma śokāgninā dahyate । mumūrṣūṃ dṛṣṭvā kṛpayā tathābhūtaḥ san iti । atra ca bhinnakartṛkatā pūrvoktanyāyān na codanīyā । yad vā darśanakriyāyā arjunaḥ kartā gātrādisādanādau ca vāstavena dharmeṇārjuna eva । na hy arjunavyatirekeṇānyad gātrādy asti । ivaśabdas tūpamārtho bhedabuddhiṃ janayatīti । api ca kṛpāvaśāt prayatnaśaithilye saty avaṣṭambhaṃ dhārayituṃ na śaknomi । duḥkhaprakarṣāc ca cakrārūḍham iva me mano bhramaty anavasthitatvād bhramatīvety uktam ।।

kiṃ ca

nimittāni ca paśyāmi viparītāni keśava ।
na ca śreyo anupaśyāmi hatvā svajanam āhave ।।

nimittāni yāni jayasūcakāni utsāhādīnīṣyante । tāni viparītāni anukūlāni paśyāmi । yad vā gātrāvasādādīni nimittāni paśyāmi । na cāhave bandhuvargaṃ hatvopakāram anupaśyāmi ।।

tatraitat syāt yady uddhyatāṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ vijaye sati rājyādilābhalakṣaṇasya śreyasaḥ sambhāvanāstīti tad āha 

na kāṅkṣe vijayaṃ kṛṣṇa na ca rājyaṃ sukhāni ca ।
kin no rājyena govinda kiṃ bhogair jīvitena vā ।।

sāmpratam eva mriyate bandhuvargas tato jayam api na kāṅkṣe nābhilaṣāmi । athocyate jaye sati rājyaṃ labhyata iti cet tan na । na ca rājyaṃ kāṅkṣe । rājye hi sati sukhāni bhavantīti cet tan na । na ca sukhāni kāṅkṣe । kasmād ity āha he govinda rājyena bhogaiḥ sukhādibhir vā kiṃ naḥ kṛtyam । sarvaṃ vā rājyabhogādikaṃ yaj jīvitopakaraṇaṃ tenāpi kiṃ prayojanam iti ।।

na tv eṣa puruṣārthāṃ yad ātmambharitvam । kiṃ tarhi । sarvaṃ hi jīvitaṃ rājyādi vā gurupitrādyartham iṣyata ity āha 

yeṣāṃ arthe kāṅkṣitaṃ no rājyaṃ bhogāḥ sukhāni ca ।
ta eveme sthitā yoddhuṃ prāṇāṃs tyaktvā sudustyajān ।।

yeṣāṃ gurvādīnāṃ kṛte rājyādy asmābhiḥ kāṅkṣitaṃ ta eva me gurvādayaḥ sudustyajān prāṇāṃs tyaktvā no asmākaṃ purato yoddhuṃ sthitāḥ । tat ko nāma buddhipūrvakārī niṣprayojanaṃ rājyādi priyaṃ kuryān na gurvādīn ।।

tān eva darśayati

ācāryāḥ pitaraḥ putrās tathaiva ca pitāmahāḥ ।
bhātulāḥ śvaśurāḥ pautrāḥ śyālāḥ sambandhinas tathā ।।

śyālāḥ śvāśuryāḥ । sambandhino jāmātrādayaḥ ।।

idānīṃ karuṇāviṣṭa āha 

etān na hantum icchāmi ghnato api madhusūdana ।
api trailokyarājyasya hetoḥ kin nu mahīkṛte ।।

etān ācāryādīn ghnato api jighāṃsato api hiṃsituṃ necchāmi । ghnato hy avaśyaṃ hanyate lābhārthaṃ yadi te hanyeran । tatra trailokyarājyasyāpi hetor na hantum icchāmi kiṃ punaḥ pṛthivyā arthe ।।

pāpaśaṅkāyām āha 

nihatya dhārtarāṣṭrān naḥ kā prītiḥ syāj janārdana ।
pāpam evāśrayed asmān hatvaitān ātatāyinaḥ ।।

he janārdana etān hatvā asmākaṃ ko abhyudayo bhavet । kasya hi bandhumaraṇāt prītir utpadyate । prītir iti yady api kṛdabhihito bhāvo dravyavad bhavati tathāpi bhāvarūpatāṃ na jahāti nāsti bhinnakartṛkatā । hananaprītyor hy ekakartṛkatā । yata ātatāyinaḥ kilaite kathan naḥ prītiḥ syād ity āha pāpam eveti । etān hatvā pratyuta pāpam eva asmān āśrayet । yata ātatāyitve api bhrātrādayaḥ sambhajanīyā vardhanīyā lāḍanoyā na tu

hantavyā iti । kathaṃ hi bhrātrādivadhād evādharmo asmān na
bhajata iti hatvā pāpam āśrayed iti । atrāpiśabdena nyāye 
bhinnakartṛkatā vāstavena tu nāsti ।
pāpaṃ hi hiṃsādikaṃ kriyātmakam eva ।
tataś ca eva hanti tenaiva kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ syād ity ekaḥ kartā ।।

evaṃ bhrātrādivadhāśaṅkāviklavam abhidhāya tadabhiprāyāviṣkaraṇāyāha 

tasmān nārhā vayaṃ hantuṃ dhārtarāṣṭrān svabandhavān ।
svajanaṃ hi kathaṃ hatvā sukhinaḥ syāma mādhava ।।

yasmād dhārtarāṣṭrahananāt prītir nāsti pratyutādharmaḥ
tasmāt tān svajanavargān hantuṃ vayaṃ nārhāḥ ।
svajanaṃ hi hatvā kathaṃ sukhino bhavema ।
dharmabahiṣkṛtānām etadācāraṇam ityabhyiprāyaḥ ।।

kiṃ ca 

yady apy ete na paśyanti lobhopahatacetasaḥ ।
kulakṣayakṛtaṃ doṣaṃ mitradrohe ca pātakam ।।

kathaṃ na jñeyam asmābhiḥ pāpād asmān nivartitum । kulakṣayakṛtaṃ doṣaṃ prapaśyadbhir janārdana ।।

kulakṣayas tāvad dhruvaḥ pratyupasthitaḥ । tatkṛtaś ca doṣo vakṣyamāṇaḥ sarva eva । amī ca droṇādayo asmāsu maitryāṃ vartamānatvān mitrāṇi । teṣāṃ drohe jighāṃsāyāṃ yat pātakaṃ yad vā mitrāṇi druhyatīti mitradhruk tasmin mitradruhi puruṣe yat pātakam

iti sambandhaḥ । tad etad ubhayam ete dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ pṛthivīlābhopahatacetasaḥ santo yady api na paśyanti na cetayante । tat katham asmād uktarūpāt pāpān nivartitum asmābhir na jñeyam avaśyaṃ jñeyam ity arthaḥ । kimbhūtair asmābhiḥ । kulakṣayakṛtadoṣam anvagacchadbhiḥ ।।

tam eva doṣaṃ darśayati

kulakṣaye praṇaśyanti kuladharmāḥ sanātanāḥ ।
dharme naṣṭe kulaṃ kṛtsnam adharmo abhibhavaty uta ।।

kulakṣaye sati ye dharmā nityanaimittikā yāgādayo gotrasamācārāḥ srtīrakṣaṇādayaś cānādikālīnās te puruṣāṇām anuṣṭhātṝṇām abhāvāt praṇaśyanti । yatra ca dharmasya hānis tatrāvaśyam adharmaḥ prabhavati parasparaṃ pratyanīkatvāt tayoḥ । tadabhibhūtaś ca prāṇino akāryeṣu 
pravartanta ity āha dharme naṣṭe kulaṃ kṛtsnam iti ।
ubhayalokahitavan nistryādikam adharma ākramya tiṣṭhatīty arthaḥ ।
utāvaśyam iti ।।

kiṃ ca

adharmābhibhavāt kṛṣṇā praduṣyanti kulastriyaḥ ।
strīṣu duṣṭāsu vārṣṇeya jāyate varṇasaṅkaraḥ ।।

adharmābhibhavād hetoḥ kulastriyaḥ caritrahīnā bhavanti । tāsu duṣṭāsu varṇeya jāyate varṇasaṅkaraḥ । varṇaś cāsau saṅkaraś ceti । aśuddho varṇa ity arthaḥ ।।

saṅkaro narakāyaiva kuladhnānāṃ kulasya ca ।
patanti pitaro hy eṣāṃ luptapiṇḍodakakriyāḥ ।।

sa varṇasaṅkaraḥ kulasya narakapatanāya kalpate । yataḥ santatiḥ śuddhavaṃśyā tu patareha ca śarmaṇe । viparītā tu narakāya ity āgamaḥ । kuladhnānāṃ ca narakāya । yato varṇasaṅkarotpattau kuladhnāḥ kāraṇabhāvaṃ pratipadyante । kasmāt saṅkaro narakāya । yasmād eṣām ubhayasainyāśritakulānāṃ pitaraḥ dharmyasantānābhāval luptapiṇḍodakakriyā bhavanti । piṇḍaś ca udakaṃ ca piṇḍodake tayoḥ kriyāḥ tā luptā yeṣāṃ te śrāddhādivicchede sati patanti ।।

।।

punar api śokasaṃvignatvāt saṅkṣepeṇa tad evālocayann āha 

doṣair etaiḥ kuladhnānāṃ varṇasaṅkarakārakaiḥ ।
utsādyate jātir dharmaḥ kuladharmaś ca śāśvataḥ ।।

kuladhnānāṃ sambandhibhiḥ etaiḥ yathoktaiḥ kuladharmanāśādharmābhibhavakulastrīdūṣaṇair varṇasaṅkarakārakair hetubhiḥ doṣaiḥ kulābhāvād jātidharmo anādikālīnaḥ 
kṣātraḥ
kuladharmaś cādhyayanaśraddhodakadānādiḥ utsādyate mūlata eva
vilopyata ity arthaḥ ।।

tataś ca 

utasannakuladharmāṇāṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ janārdana ।
narake niyataṃ vāso bhavatīty anuśuśruma ।।

utsanne kuladharme tv ayam anyo doṣo yat kuladharmaiḥ

parasvargādyabhyudayena yogāt pretānāṃ santativicchedān na bhavati svargaprāptiḥ । pratyuta śrāddhātithyādikuladharmābhāvān narakapatanaṃ teṣāṃ bhavaty eveti vedavādibhyaḥ anuśuśruma śrutavanto vayam iti ।।

evaṃ saṃśayāviṣṭacetā narakapratyavāyadarśanāt sañjātasaṃvega āha 

aho bata mahatpāpaṃ kartuṃ vyavasitā vayam ।
yad rājyasukhalobhena hantuṃ svajanam udyatāḥ ।।

aho vismaye । bata viṣāde । yad rājyasukhalobhena vismayakāriṇā sārabhūtaṃ durlabhaṃ svajanaṃ hantuṃ vayam udyatāḥ tat mahatpāpaṃ kartuṃ vyavasitā ity ato asya viṣādaḥ । tathā rājyasukhaṃ nāma paśya kīdṛśaṃ yena vayam adya pāpāḥ sambhāvyamānasvajanavadhāya pravartāmaha iti vismayaḥ । yad vā aho dainye । bata khedānukampayoḥ । rājyena yat sukhaṃ tallobhāt svajanavadhapāpavyavasāye pravartāmahe । trayo apy ete kleśā rājyārtham asya prādur abhavann iti kṛtvā nivartitum icchatīti ।।

saṃvegākulaḥ punar api pralapann āha 

yadi mām apratīkāram aśastraṃ śastraprāṇayaḥ ।
dhārtarāṣṭrā raṇe hanyus tan me kṣemataraṃ bhavet ।।

yadi dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ śastrapāṇayaḥ santaḥ mām aśastram anudyatāyudham apratīkāram akṛtapratividhānam udāsīnāvasthaṃ hanyus tan me

kṣemataraṃ yuktataraṃ syāt ।
paro manorathaḥ siddhaḥ syāt pāpākaraṇād ity arthaḥ ।
saśastraṃ sapratīkāraṃ māṃ hantuṃ na kecana kṣamāḥ syur
ity ubhayor upādānam ।।

idānīṃ sañjayo dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ praty arjunakathāprastāvaṃ samāpayann idam āha 

evam uktvārjunaḥ saṅkhye rathopastha upāviśat ।
utsṛjya saśaraṃ cāpaṃ śokasaṃvignamānasaḥ ।।

tān samīkṣya sīdamāno abravīd idam ity ataḥ prabhṛti evaṃ yathoktam uktvā arjunaḥ saṅkhye yuddhabhūmau dhanur utsṛjya rathasyopary upāviśat । kiṃ kāraṇam । yataḥ svajanahananajanitaśokākula iti ।।

atra saṅgrahaślokāḥ 

śūrasaṅkhyā paravyūhe svabale śūrasaṅgrahaḥ ।
tadviveko bhīṣmarakṣā śaṅkhavāditraniḥsvanāḥ ।।

didṛkṣā sainyayor jñātigurumitrānudarśanam ।
tajjānukampā pārthasya paridevaparibhramau ।।

yuddhatyāgaś ca śokaś ca padārthāḥ sārasaṅgrahaḥ ।।

iti śrīmadbhagavadgītāsu bhagavadbhāskarakṛte
bhagavadāśayānusaraṇābhidhāne bhāṣye arjunaviṣādo nāma
prathamo adhyāyaḥ ।।

atha dvitīyo adhyāyaḥ

ittham antakavaktrakuharābhimukhaṃ janaṃ mitrabandhuvargaṃ prati jātaghṛṇaṃ arjunaṃ pṛthivībhārāvataraṇasampipādayiṣayā bhagavān svadharmasahitasamyagdarśanopadeśena yuyodhayiṣatīti pratipādayituṃ dvitīyādhyāyagranthārambhaḥ । taṃ sañjayo dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ prati vivṛṇvann āha 

taṃ tathā kṛpayāviṣṭam aśrupūrṇākulekṣaṇam ।
sīdamānam idaṃ vākyam uvāca madhusūdanaḥ ।।

tam arjunaṃ tena prakāreṇa prathamādhyāyoktena gātrāvasādamukhaśoṣaromaharṣādilakṣaṇam avasīdantaṃ kāruṇyaparavaśam ata evāśrupūravyākulatvāl lohitekṣaṇam 
avasīdantaṃ vyuparatayuddhodyamaṃ bhagavān vakṣyamāṇaṃ
vākyam uvāca ।
taṃ vākyam uvāceti dvikarmakatā ।।

kutas tvā kaśmalam idaṃ viṣame samupasthitam ।
anāryajuṣṭam asvargyam akīrtikaram arjuna ।।

kuta iti saṃśayānaḥ pṛcchati । kasmād idaṃ mohalakṣaṇaṃ pāpaṃ kartṛ tvām upagatam āgatam । asmin viṣame saṅkaṭe trailokyasambhāvitapauruṣaṃ tvām asambhāvyamāno mohaḥ kutaḥ samprāpta iti mahān saṃśayaḥ । kīdṛśaṃ kaśmalam । kulaśīlavidyārahitaiḥ sevitam ataś cākīrtikaraṃ tata eva cāsvargya narakādiprāpakaṃ tasmāt ।।

mā klaivyaṃ gaccha kaunteya naitat tvayy upapadyate ।
kṣudraṃ hṛdayadaurbalyaṃ tyaktvottiṣṭha parantapa ।।

klaibyam amanuṣyatvaṃ dīnabhāvaṃ mohān mā gaccha mā āśraya yatas tvayi khāṇḍavānalatarpaṇena saṅgrāmārādhitatryambakatayā nivātakavacavadhaparitoṣitapurandaratvādibhir upādānair deveṣv api prakhyātapauruṣe naitad upapadyate na sambhāvyate । 
atas tvaṃ hṛdayasyālpasāratvaṃ kṣudram alpavastubhūtaṃ
nyūnahṛdayatvaṃ kāpuruṣasevitaṃ tyaktvā rathopasthād uttiṣṭha ।
utthāya ca yuddhāya sajjo bhavety āśayaḥ ।
parantapety anenārjunaṃ protsāhayati ।।

evaṃ bhagavatokte arjuna uvāca 

kathaṃ bhīṣmam ahaṃ saṅkhye droṇaṃ ca madhusūdana ।
iṣubhiḥ pratiyotsyāmi pūjārhāv arisūdana ।।

kathaṃ kena prakāreṇa kayā yuktyā bhīṣmādīn mānanīyān ahaṃ pratiyotsyāmi । madhusūdanārisūdaneti bhaktaḥ punaḥ punar āsthāṃ karoti samakrameṇa ।।

kim iti na ca pratiyotsyāmīty āha 

gurūn ahatvā hi mahānubhāvān śreyaś cartuṃ bhaiṣkyam apīha loke ।
na tv arthakāmas tu gurūn nihatya bhuñjīya bhogān rudhir apradigdhān ।।

hi yataḥ kāraṇāt । yasmād iha loke deśe gurūn bhīṣmādīn prati yuddhavarjanena ahatvā rakṣitvā bhaikṣyam api cartuṃ śreyaḥ । na tu dhanābhilāṣī san gurūn nihatya bhogān rājyādīn śoṇitalepabahulān bhuñjīyeti kutsā । naiva bhuñjīyety arthaḥ । iha loka iha kṣaṇike jīvaloka ity arthaḥ । tuśabdo guruhananavyāvṛttisūcanārthaḥ । punas tugrahaṇād bhaikṣyam api praśasyataram । na tv evaṃvidho viṣayopabhoga iti ।।

etaddaśāyām idam iva tāvad vicāryatām 

na caitad vidmaḥ kataran no garīyo yad vā jayema yadi vā no jayeyuḥ ।
yān eva hatvā na jijīviṣāmas tena sthitāḥ pramukhe dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ ।।

caśabdaḥ pūrvāpekṣayādhikābhyudayayuktidyotanārthaḥ । etad iti vakṣyamāṇāvamarśinā sarvanāmnā yad vā jayema yadi vā no jayeyuḥ ity etadvakṣyamāṇavākyadvayābhidheyo arthaḥ pratyavamṛśyate । na ty ātmīyaparavargāv ekīkṛtya nirdeśaḥ । sa dhārtarāṣṭrāṇām asmākam ity artho vivakṣitaḥ । katarad ity anena sāmānyavādinā tadvākyadvayābhidheyayor balayor ekataraṃ garīyastvena vikalpato nirṇīyate ।

yadyadiśabdau vitarke vikalpe vā । tad ayaṃ vākyārthaḥ na caitad vayaṃ jayaparājayayor aniyamāj jānīmaḥ katarad balam asmākaṃ dhārtarāṣṭrāṇāṃ madhyād garīyo gurutaraṃ balavattaram iti । yad vā vayaṃ tān jayemābhibhavema yadi vā te no asmān jayeyur abhibhaveyur iti । kiṃ ca yān eva dhārtarāṣṭrān hatvā jīvituṃ 
necchāmaḥ kṛpālutayā ta evāsmākaṃ pramukhe sammukhe sthitā iti ।
etac cārjunasya sambhramaparidevanaṃ hastādyabhinayena ।।

evaṃ sakāraṇaṃ svaparidevanaṃ punar api bhagavantam arjuna āha 

kārpaṇyadoṣopahatasvabhāvaḥ pṛcchāmi tvāṃ dharmasammūḍhacetāḥ ।
yac chreyaḥ syān niścitaṃ brūhi tan me śiṣyas te ahaṃ śādhi māṃ tvāṃ prapannam ।।

evam ahaṃ gurubandhumitrasvajanān mṛtyunā dhṛtān dṛṣṭvā kārpaṇyadoṣopahatasvabhāvaḥ kārpaṇyam aucityapratipakṣabhūtaṃ dainyam tad eva doṣas tenopahato dūṣitaḥ sattvadhairyātmakaḥ svabhāvo yasya sa tathoktaḥ । tathā dharme sammūḍham apratipattiṃ gataṃ ceto yasya so ahaṃ pṛcchāmi tvāṃ parameśvaram । yan me śreyaḥ syāt tan me niścitam asandigdhaṃ brūhīti । dharmaviṣayadainyadoṣopahatacitto aham ity arthaḥ ।

śāstravihito anuṣṭheyaḥ kriyāmārgo dharmaḥ । tatraitat syāt nāśiṣyāyopadeśo deyaḥ iti । tan na । śiṣyas te ahaṃ niveditātmā tvāṃ prapannaḥ śaraṇāgataś ca । ato anuśāsanenānugṛhāṇeti ।।

kasmāt tvattaḥ śreyo anuśāsanaṃ prārthyata iti cet tad āha 

na hi prapaśyāmi mamāpanudyād yac chokam ucchoṣaṇam indriyāṇām ।
avāpya bhūmāv asapatnam ṛddhaṃ rājyaṃ surāṇām api cādhipatyam ।।

hi yataḥ kāraṇād deśe । yasmād bhūmau niṣkaṇṭakaṃ sphītaṃ rājyaṃ tato api cādhikaṃ surāṇāṃ svāmitvaṃ prāpya ahan na tat tathābhūtaṃ prapaśyāmi buddhyā nirīkṣye yo mamaivambhūtasya sarvādhipateḥ sambhāvyamānahitopadeśasahāyakasyāpi mumūrṣor glānisamutthaṃ śokaṃ sarvendriyāṇām indriyavṛttīnām 
ucchoṣaṇaṃ
saṅkocakaram apanudyāt nirasyet tvāṃ vinety atas tvāṃ
pṛcchāmīti ।।

adhunā sañjayaḥ pārthapratijñātām uktim samāpayaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭram āha 

evam uktvā hṛṣīkeśaṃ guḍākeśaḥ parantapa ।
na yotsyāmīti govindam uktvā tūṣṇīṃ babhūva ha ।।

he parantapa । kathaṃ bhīṣmam ahaṃ ity ataḥ prabhṛti 
bhagavantam uktvā tato atiśokākulamanāḥ punar api govindam āha 
na yotsyāmi iti ।
evaṃ paricchedam utsādya tūṣṇīṃ babhūvety arthaḥ ।
haḥ pādapūraṇe ।।

idānīṃ bhagavatprayuktiṃ varṇayann āha 

tam uvāca hṛṣīkeśaḥ prahasann iva bhārata ।
senayor ubhayor madhye sīdamānam idaṃ vacaḥ ।।

tam arjunaṃ senayor madhye yathoktena prakāreṇa sīdamānaṃ yuddhaṃ 
prati tyktotsāhaṃ hṛṣīkeśo hasann idaṃ vakṣyamāṇaṃ vākyam
āha ।
mahātmānaḥ kila smitapūrvābhibhāṣiṇo bhavantīti ।।

tatra na yotsyāmi ity ātmaviṣayamithyājñānavaśān niścitasaṅkalpam arjunam ātmajñānopadeśam antareṇa tannivṛtter asambhavāt tadupadeśāya prasaṅgam avatārayituṃ bhagavān uvāca 

tvaṃ mānuṣeṇopahatāntarātmā viṣādamohābhibhavād visañjñaḥ ।
kṛpāgṛhītaḥ samavekṣya bandhūn abhiprapannān mukham antakasya ।।

tvaṃ mānuṣeṇa māṇuṣajātisulabhenānuśayena malinīkṛtamanāḥ । ata eva mṛtyor āsyam ābhimukhyenāgantum ārabhamāṇān bandhūn avekṣya dayābhibhūto mānuṣajātisulabhābhyāṃ śokamohābhyāṃ grahaṇād dhetor visañjño vyavahitadivyajñānaḥ saṃvṛtta iti । itaś copahāsakāraṇam । sañjñānaṃ sañjñā viśiṣṭā buddhiḥ । 
vigatā vyavahitā vā sañjñā asyeti visañjñaḥ ।
upahatāntarātmā ।
vṛttyaprasaṅgāt samāso mānuṣeṇety anena sāpekṣatve api
gamakatvād yujyata eveti ।।

kasmād visañjño asīty āha 

aśocyān anvaśocas tvaṃ prajñāvādāṃś ca bhāṣase ।
gatāsūnagatāsūṃś ca nānuśocanti paṇḍitāḥ ।।

aśocyān aśocanīyān bhīṣmādīn anuśocitavān asi । teṣāṃ hi svadharmānuṣṭhānapravṛttatvena trivargāsiddher bhāvino arthasya ca nityatvād aśocyatvam । api ca prajñāvādāṃś ca bhāṣase 

pāpam evāśrayed asmān śreyaś cartuṃ bhaikṣyam apīha loke iti । tad etad ubhayaṃ tava na śobhate । yasmād gataprāṇānagataprāṇāmś ca nānuśocanti paṇḍitāḥ । pariniṣṭhitatattvajñānāḥ paṇḍitāḥ । pariniṣṭhitatattvajñānāḥ paṇḍitā ucyante । atra punar ātmayāthātmyavādino abhipreyante । teṣāṃ tāvad ātmano avināśitvadarśanād aśokaḥ । tadvad avināsitvaṃ saṃpadya mohaśokau tyaktum arhasīti tātparyārthaḥ ।

na punar asyāyam arthaḥ paṇḍitā na śocanti tvaṃ tu mūḍho asīti । nehātivinītasya maurkhyaṃ sampādyaṃ tadapanayārthatvāt pravṛtteḥ ।।

kathaṃ punar asyāvināśitvam ity utsāhayitum āha 

na tv evāhaṃ jātu nāsaṃ na tvaṃ neme janādhipāḥ ।
na caiva na bhaviṣyāmaḥ sarve vayam ataḥ param ।।

catuśabdau kadācid ity asminn arthe varttete । nāhaṃ kadācin nāsam api tv āsam eva । na tvaṃ nāsīr asīr evety arthaḥ । neme bhīṣmādayo nāsaṃ kiṃ tv āsann eva । na ca na bhaviṣyāmaḥ । asmāc charīrāt paraṃ śarīrāntare bhaviṣyāma eva । anena triṣv api kāleṣu sattākhyāyate । pratiśarīraṃ kṣetrajñānāṃ bhedāt tadbhedavyapadeśaḥ । ke punar amī kṣetrajñā nāma । paramātmano aṃśāḥ । tathā ca vakṣyati mamaivāṃśo jīvaloke jīvabhūtaḥ sanātana iti । agnivisphuliṅgavan mahākāśaghaṭākāśavaj jīvaparayor bhedābhedau । tatra svābhāviko abheda aupādhikas tu bheda iti sthitiḥ । evam uttaratra kvacid abhedena vyapadeśaḥ kvacid bhedena ca bhaviṣyati । anādisiddhāś ca jīvāḥ sanātanā iti vacanān na teṣāṃ sargādāv utpādaḥ pralayo vānte । tathā ca yājñavalkyaḥ 

ahaṅkāreṇa manasā gatyā karmaphalena ca । śarīreṇa ca nātmāyaṃ muktapūrvaḥ kadācana ।। iti ।

evaṃ cānāditve pūrvakṛtakarmāpekṣayā sargādau suranaratiryagbhedena sṛṣṭivaicitryopapattiḥ । dharmādharmavyavasthā bandhamokṣavyavasthā cāsmin pakṣe avakalpate ।

yeṣāṃ punaḥ paramātmaiva sākṣād anupraviṣṭaḥ śarīreṣu tadaṃśo jīvo nāma nāstīti matam teṣām ekasmin mukte sarvamuktiprasaṅgo baddhe caikasmin sarvasyāpi muktyabhāvād iti vyāsasūnoḥ śukasyāpi muktyabhāvaḥ syāt । na ca paramātmanaḥ saṃsāritvaṃ yujyate । tasya ca vidyāyogāt vijñānam ānandaṃ brahma iti ca nityākāśānandasvarūpatvāt । tasmād īśvarāṃśāḥ pratiśarīraṃ parasparaṃ bhinnā jīvā abhyupagantavyāḥ । evaṃ ca ghaṭadhūmadṛṣṭānto api yujyate 

yathaikasmin ghaṭākāśe rajodhūmādibhir vṛte । na sarve saṃprayujyante tadvaj jīvāḥ sukhādibhiḥ ।। iti ।

yeṣām ayam īśvaro atyantabhinno jīvātmānaś ca bahavas te ca sarve sarvagatā iti teṣām api sāṅkaryaprasaṅgaḥ । ekenāgnihotre kṛte sarveṣāṃ tatkṛtaṃ syād ekena ca madyapāne kṛte sarvaiḥ kṛtaṃ syāt । atha yasya taccharīraṃ tasyaiva tad iti cet

kasya tac charīram । sarveṣāṃ tat sambandhāviśeṣād abhisandhyādivaśāt syād vyavastheti cet abhisandhyādiṣu caikatulyatvād ekasmin manasi sarveṣāṃ samavāyāḥ saṅkalpādayaḥ samānās tatpūrvakaṃ karma tannimittaṃ ca śarīram iti sarvasādhāraṇyān na kadācid asādhāraṇyahetuḥ śakyate kenacid darśayitum । anāditvasyāsmatpakṣe apy aviśeṣād aṇuparimāṇāś ca jīvā iṣyante । kasmāt । utkrāntigatyāgatiśruteḥ । 
liṅgaśarīrasya ca saṅkocavikāsadharmiṇor aṇurūpatvād
aupādhikam aṇutvaṃ jīvasya gīyate ।
paramātmarūpeṇa tu sarvagatatvaṃ jīvasyeti
sthitam ।।

tasya nityatve lokasiddhaṃ dṛṣṭāntam ācaṣṭe

dehino asmin yathā deho kaumāraṃ yauvanaṃ jarā ।
tathā dehāntaraprāptir dhīras tatra na muhyati ।।

yathā bālyayauvanasthāvireṣu so aham asmīti pratyabhijñānān nityatvam ātmanaḥ pratyakṣapramāṇasiddham । dehasyaivāvasthāntarāpattir nātmana iti tathā nityasyaiva tatrāvasthitasya ātmanaḥ dehāntaraprāptiḥ । tatra dhīro dhīmān na muhyati । yadi tarhy avināśitvam ātmanas tad idānīṃ vṛthā te śokaḥ samupasthitaḥ katham ।।

śītoṣṇādikṛtaiḥ sukhaduḥkhaiḥ saṃyogāt tadanuparama iti । tac ca 

mātrāsparśās tu kaunteya śrītoṣṇasukhaduḥkhadāḥ ।
āgamāpayino anityās tāṃs titikṣasva bhārata ।।

mīyante viṣayā ābhir iti mātrā indriyavṛttayaḥ । tāsāṃ sparśā viṣayaiḥ saṃyogāḥ śītoṣṇanimittasukhaduḥkhahetavaḥ । te cānityāḥ । kasmāt । āgamāpāyitvāt । āgacchanti apagacchanti ca na ca nityasamavetāḥ pāvakauṣṇyavat । śītoṣṇagrahaṇaṃ pradarśanārtham । ādhyātmikam ādhidaivikam ādhibhautikaṃ trividhaṃ duḥkham tat ca trividham eveti । yasmād anityās teṣām upāyenoparamaḥ śakyaḥ kartum । ko asāv upāyaḥ । jñānapūrvikā titikṣā । tad āha tāṃs titikṣasva iti sahasvety arthaḥ ।।

kathaṃ tatsahanaṃ taduparamahetur ity āha 

yaṃ hi na vyathayanty ete puruṣaṃ puruṣarṣabha ।
samaduḥkhasukhaṃ dhīraṃ so amṛtatvāya kalpate ।।

na vyathayanti na cālayanti svasmād ātmasvarūpāt । same duḥkhasukhe yasya । yaṃ samaduḥkhasukhaṃ na cālayanti so amṛtatvāya mokṣāya kalpate samartho yogyo bhavatītyathaḥ ।।

nanu cāmṛtatvaṃ na sambhāvayituṃ śakyate sukhaduḥkhalakṣaṇasya vikārasya mukte apy ātmani sambhavād ātmano vā kadācid vināśopapattir ity āśaṅkya āha 

nāsato vidyate bhāvo nābhāvo vidyate sataḥ ।
ubhayor api dṛṣṭo antas tv anayos tattvadarśibhiḥ ।।

ātmany avidyamānasya sukhaduḥkhalakṣaṇasya dharmasya na kadācid vidyate bhāvaḥ । bhavanaṃ bhūtir utpattir ity arthaḥ । sikatāsv iva tailasya । utpadyamānasyaiva hi mānasaḥ sukhaduḥkhalakṣaṇo vikāraḥ śītoṣṇādinibandhano jāyata ity anantaram uktam । nanv acetanatvād antaḥkaraṇasya saṃvedanaṃ nopapadyate । cetanatvāt kṣetrajñasamavetasyaivāyaṃ vikāraḥ ।

yathā vaiśeṣikāḥ prāhuḥ naitad evam antaḥkaraṇastho apy asau jīvātmā saṃvedyate । yathā ca rūpādayo ghaṭādisthāḥ iti । nāyaṃ kṣetrajñadharma iti ca vakṣyati icchā dveṣaḥ sukhaṃ duḥkham iti । yady api kṣetrajñasamavāyitvaṃ sukhaduḥkhayos tathāpi tatsvarūpasya na vikriyā maṇisvarūpavat । nīlapītādīnām eva maṇisamavāyināṃ parasparavirodhād vikriyā । vikriyā hi nāma vināśa upamardaḥ । tathātmana iti । nābhāvo vināśo vidyate । sata ātmanaḥ so aham iti pratyabhijñānān nityatvopapatter anityahetoś cābhāvāt । avināśī vā are ayam ātmā iti śruteḥ । ubhayoḥ sadasator dṛṣṭo nirṇīto anto maryādā antyāvastheti yāvat । antaśabdo maryādāvacano atra grāmānta iti yathā । yat sat

tat sad eva । yad asat tad asad eveti ।
kair ayaṃ niścayaḥ kṛta ity āha tattvadarśibhiḥ । tadbhāvas tattvam । tad iti sarvanāmnā padārthamātraṃ vyapadiśyate । vastuyāthātmyavedibhir ity arthaḥ । apare tu māyāvādino anyathāvatārya varṇayanti । itaś ca śokamohāv akṛtvā śītoṣṇāder vidyate bhāvaḥ । bhavanam astitā । kutaḥ । vikāratvāt । vikāraś ca pratyakṣādibhiḥ pramāṇair nirūpyamāṇo nāstitāṃ pratipadyate । yathā ghaṭādiḥ svakāraṇavyatirekeṇānupalabdher asan evaṃ sarvo vikāra iti । nanv evaṃ sarvābhāve śūnyavādaḥ prasajyeta । nāyaṃ doṣaḥ । dve buddhī sarvaprāṇiprasiddhe bhavataḥ viśeṣyabuddhir viśeṣaṇabuddhiś ca । san ghaṭaḥ san pataḥ iti । tatra viśeṣyaviṣayā buddhir ghaṭādiviṣayā satpaṭādau vyabhicārān mithyābuddhiḥ । yā punar viśeṣaṇaviṣayā sadbuddhiḥ sā sarvatra vṛtter amithyā । tasmāt saiva pāramārthiko । sarvo hi ghaṭādiḥ śarīrādiś ca prapañco māyāmātram asad iti manyante ।

etad anye pramāṇakuśalāḥ pratyācakṣate । yat tāvad uktam pratyakṣādibhiḥ pramāṇair vikāro ghaṭādir nirūpyamāṇaḥ svarūpaṃ jahātīti tad asat । ālokendriyamanaḥsaṃskāre sati ghaṭo ayaṃ paṭo ayam iti pratyakṣā buddhir utpadyate । yayā buddhyā yo artho pratīyate tayaiva tadabhāvaḥ pratīyate

iti ko vaded yo na tārkikaḥ । pañcabhiḥ pramāṇaiḥ pratyakṣānumānopamānārthāpattyāgamair vastusvarūpaṃ paricchidyate । yatra pañcāpi nivṛttāni tatra pramāṇanivṛttyā prameyābhāvo niścīyate । yathā nātra ghaṭa iti । na ca vyabhicārād evāvastutvaṃ bhavati । yathaiva ghaṭabuddheḥ paṭādau vyabhicārād avastutvaṃ tathā sadbuddher api śaśaviṣāṇādāv api vyabhicārād avastutvaṃ prasajyate । bhāvabuddhir abhāvān nivartate bhāvābhāvayoḥ parasparavirodhāt । atha yathā sadbuddhiḥ sattāṃ jñāpayati tathā ghaṭādibuddhir apīndriyajanyatvāviśeṣād anuvṛttivyāvṛttipratyayagrāhyatvāc ca । avāntarasāmānyam api ghaṭatvagotvādi sarvam abhyupagantavyam । tathā ca vyaktiḥ sāmānyasya taddharmatvāt । param aparaṃ ca dvividhaṃ sāmānyam । paraṃ sattālakṣaṇam । aparaṃ gotvādilakṣaṇam । na hy āśrayasya dharmiṇo bhāvas tadāśritasya sāmānyasya vastutvam avakalpate । sato hi bhāvaḥ sattā । na hi sā nirduṣṭā svatantrā nāma kenacid iha ghaṭādyāśrayanirapekṣā cakṣuṣā gṛhyate । satsu dravyeṣu pṛthivyādiṣu gṛhyamāṇeṣu tatsamavetā tadavyatiriktā sattāpi gṛhyate । ata eva sattā dravyadharmatvād ātmā na bhavati । tatra sattaivātmā iti yat kaiścid uktam tad apāstaṃ bhavati । ata eva yad uktaṃ kenāpi cāturvidhyāc ca pratyakṣaṃ na nigrāhyaṃ vipaścitā iti sattāyā eva grāhakaṃ pratyakṣam ity abhipretya tasya tad apy apākṛtaṃ

bhavati । satāṃ hi bhāvaḥ sattā iti pāratantryavapadeśāt ।
na ca ghaṭādibuddhīnāṃ ghaṭatvādāv avāntarasāmānye tadyuktau vā vyabhicāraḥ । kasyāṃcid vyaktau vinaṣṭau vinaṣṭāyāṃ vyaktyantarāṇām ānantyād yugapad ucchedanānupapatteḥ ।

svaviṣayavabhicāro hi buddhīnāṃ doṣo viṣaye tu paṭādau notpadyata iti kim atrāścaryam । na hi viṣayendriyālokasaṃskārasāmarthyatāyāṃ satyāṃ ghaṭabuddhiḥ kadācit kasyacin notpadyate । kiṃ ca kāryatvād ghaṭatvabuddhiḥ kāraṇam apekṣate । ghaṭajñānasya ghaṭaḥ kāraṇaṃ nānyad iti । yathā bījāṅkuraḥ kāraṇaṃ bījam apekṣate dhūmaś cāgnim evam anyatrāpīti । tasmān na vyabhicāro mithyāhetur iti durupadeśo ayam । kas tarhi mithyāhetuḥ kāraṇadoṣo abādhakapratyayo vā । tathā coktam 

yasya ca duṣṭaṃ karaṇaṃ yatra ca mithyeti pratyayaḥ । sa evāsamīcīnaḥ pratyayo nānyaḥ iti ।

tad evam anuvṛttipratyayāt sāmānyaṃ siddhaṃ vyāvṛttipratyayād viśeṣa iti । sāmānyaviśeṣātmakaṃ vastu bhinnābhinnarūpam iti sthitam । kiṃ ca san ghaṭa iti ghaṭatvavastutve sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ buddhau nāvakalpate । nanu tac cedam udakam iti mṛgatṛṣṇikāyāṃ sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ dṛśyate । tatrāpi vidyamānā abhimānina

eva sāmānādhikaraṇyabuddhir utpadyate । yadā tu bādhakapratyayo jāyate mṛgatṛṣṇikeyam atra nodakam astīti tadā sāmānādhikaraṇyabuddhir apaiti । 
na cātra bādhakapratyayo astīti
dṛṣṭāntavaiṣamyam ।
ato apavyākhyānam etad iti sthitam ।।

sato bhāvo nāstīti sāmānyenoktaṃ tad idānīṃ viśeṣalakṣaṇena nivārayitum āha 

avināśi tu tad viddhi yena sarvam idaṃ tatam ।
vināśam avyayasyāsya na kaścid kartum arhati ।।

tuśabdo avadhāraṇārthaḥ । avināśi tat । na vinaṣṭuṃ śīlam asyety avināśi । kiṃ tat । yena sarvam idaṃ tataṃ vyāptam । svābhāvikena paramātmarūpeṇa kṣetrajño vyapadiśyata iti । kasmād evaṃ vyākhyāyate । tadvināśāśaṅkāanirākaraṇaparatvād asya prakaraṇasya । na hy atra brahmopāsanam akasmāt pratipādyate । jñānasvarūpasyopāsanaṃ ṣaṣṭe adhyāye vidhāpayiṣyata iti jīvasvarūpam evedānīṃ vaktavyam । kasmād avināśīty āha vināśam avyayasyāsya iti । vyayo vināśaḥ । niravayavatvān nāsya vināśam īśvaro api kartum arhatīti ।।

yadi tarhy ayam avināśī tat kathaṃ kṛto vyapadeśaḥ vinaṣṭaḥ puruṣa iti । ata āha 

antavanta ime dehā nityasyoktāḥ śarīriṇaḥ ।
vināśino aprameyasya tasmād yuddhasva bhārata ।।

nityasya śarīriṇo aprameyasyāntavanto vināśino dehā uktā nityānityavibhāgavidbhiḥ । antavanto vināśina iti na punaruktam । antavanta ity asyārthaṃ svayam eva bhagavān vyācaṣṭe vināśina ity eke varṇayanti ।

anye tu vadanti kasyacid antavattvaṃ na bhavati । yathā pṛthivyā gandhas tirobhūto nātyantaṃ vinaṣṭo vṛṣṭisaṃyogād abhivyajyate tathā dehasyānto bhaved nātyantaṃ vināśa iti । tan mā bhūd iti viśinaṣṭi vināśina iti । asminn api vyākhyāne antavadgrahaṇam atiriktam । tad akṛtvā vināśina ity eva vaktavyam abhipretāvināśasiddheḥ ।

apare tu pāṭhāntaraṃ kurvanti avināśino aprameyasya iti । teṣām api nityasyāvināśina iti punaruktam । na tu pṛthivyādivad āpekṣikaṃ nityatvaṃ gauṇaṃ gṛhyate । atyantanityasya mukhyasya nityaśabdārthasyāsambhavād avināśina ity ukte apy āpekṣikaṃ kin na gṛhyate । tasya vyākhyāntarakaraṇaṃ vyartham । kā tarhi gatiḥ । vināśino dehā iti pratijñātam । tatrāntavanta iti hetvabhidhānārtham antavadgrahaṇaṃ deśataḥ kālataś ca paricchinnatvāt kūṭādivad iti vyatirekād dhetuvacanam aprameyasyeti । kasmād ātmā nityaḥ । aprameyatvād deśataḥ kālataś ceti sa svadharme pravartate iti bhagavān āha ।

nanu śokamohādisaṃsārakāraṇanivṛttyarthaṃ gītāśāstraṃ na pravartakam । atrocyate na sādhu tātparyaṃ bhavatā parāmṛṣṭam । yuddhaṃ prakramya śokamohāpanayasyedam eva prayojanam kathaṃ nāma yuddhe pravarteteti । itarathā dvārikāyāṃ sthitvā gītāśāstraṃ 
praṇayet svadharmaparityāgena jñānamātrād
yadi mokṣo abhipreto abhaviṣyat ।
idānīṃ praṇayanasyedam eva prayojanam arjunasyānyeṣāṃ ca
jñānasahitāt svadharmānuṣṭhānān niḥśreyasam upadekṣyāmīti ।। 
।।

evaṃ tāvad avināśitvam ātmanaḥ pratipādya svayaṃ ca manyase hantāham eṣām ime mayā hanyanta iti tac ca mṛṣā । katham 

ya enaṃ vetti hantāraṃ yaś cainaṃ manyate hatam ।
ubhau tau na vijānīto nāyaṃ hanti na hanyate ।।

nabhasa ivāsya hananakriyayā vināśaḥ kartuṃ na śakyate niravayavatvāt । 
sāvayavasyāvayavaviśleṣādinā śakyate vināśaḥ
sambhāvayitum ।
tasmād ubhāv apy etāv ajñau hantāham iti yo manyate
yaś ca hato aham iti manyate ca ।।

idaṃ pratijñāmātreṇoktam । hetvapekṣāyāṃ ṣaṇṇām api bhāvavikārāṇām ātmany abhāvād iti hetum ācaṣṭe 

na jāyate mriyate vā kadācin nāyaṃ bhūtvā bhavitā vā na bhūyaḥ ।
ajo nityaḥ śāśvato ayaṃ purāṇo na hanyate hanyamāne śarīre ।।

na jāyata iti janmalakṣaṇo bhāvavikāraḥ pratiṣidhyate । vāśabdaś cārthe । na cāyaṃ mriyata iti vināśalakṣaṇo bhāvavikāraḥ pratiṣidhyate । katham etat । bhūtvā nāyaṃ na bhavitā । bhūyaḥ punaḥ । kiṃ tarhi । bhavitaiva । bhāviny api kāle sattāṃ na hāsyatīty arthaḥ । vāśabdād abhūtvā bhāvaḥ pratiṣiddhyate । nāyam abhūtvā bhavati । kiṃ tarhi । bhūtvaiva bhavitā । bhūtakāle api sattāṃ na babhārety arthaḥ । yas tv abhūtvā bhavati bhūtvā ca na bhavati sa janmavināśābhyāṃ yujyate yathā ghaṭādir iti । sattāpi janmapūrvikā ghaṭasyevāsya neṣyate । niravadhikaivāsya satteti ghaṭādibhyo asya vailakṣaṇyam । upasaṃharati ajo nitya iti । janmavināśapratiṣedhenaiva madhyavarttino bhāvavikārāḥ pratiṣiddhā bhavanti । tathāpi mandabuddhyanugrahārthaṃ svaśabdena pratiṣedhati । śāśvata ity apakṣayo niṣidhyate । svāṅgāpacayaḥ sādhanāpacayo vāsya nāstīti । yathā kṛṣṇo rājā hastyaśvādibhir vā hīna iti । purāṇa iti vṛddhilakṣaṇo bhāvavikāraḥ pratiṣidhyate । nāyaṃ śaśivat kalābhir upavipacīyate । na hanyate hanyamāne śarīra iti vipariṇāmo niṣidhyate । vipariṇāmo avasthāntarāpattiḥ yathā śaśasya māṃsāvasthā ।

anye punar apy anyathā varṇayanti nāyaṃ bhūto bhavitā vā na bhūya iti pāṭhāntaraṃ kṛtvā parabrahmopāsanam anayā gītayā lakṣyate ।

nāyaṃ bhūta iti ca mṛtpiṇḍavat kāraṇatvaṃ niṣidhyate । bhavitā vā iti ghaṭādivad utpādyatvaṃ niṣiddhyate । kāryakāraṇabhāvo brahmaṇy aupādhiko na pāramārthika ity uktaṃ bhavatīti । tad idaṃ śradhāmātreṇa brahmopāsanam utprekṣitaṃ na śrutiliṅgaprakaraṇagamyam । prakaraṇaṃ hi yac coktam ucchoṣaṇam indriyāṇām iti paṭhanāt tadapanodaparam । ṣaḍbhāvavikāranivṛttiparāṇi na jāyata ityādīny akṣarāṇi । liṅgaṃ sāmarthyam ucyate । tac ca śabdānāṃ tāvanmātre paryavasyati । tan nopāsanam ākṣipati ।

ajñānam eva tāvad idānīṃ nirasanīyam । kim atitvarayā brahmopāsanaṃ kalpyate । pāṭhāntarakaraṇaṃ cāhopuruṣikāmātram । brahmaṇo hi jagatkāraṇatvaṃ śrutisiddham sad eva somyedam iti । kāryatvaṃ punar na jāyata ity anenaiva niṣidhyate । tasmād yatkiñcid etad evaṃ tu pāṭhāntaraṃ 
kurvanto arthāntaraṃ svamatiparikalpitaṃ
varṇayanto bahavo vyākhyātāro abhiyuktāś cocyate ।
uktaṃ ca 
śīladoṣād agṛhṇantaṃ lokam ākulīkurvantīti vā ।।

pratijñātam artham avikriyātvādibhiḥ pratyākhyāyopasaṃharati 

vedāvināśinaṃ nityaṃ ya enam ajam avyayam ।
kathaṃ sa puruṣaḥ pārtha kaṃ ghātayati hanti kam ।।

veda jānāti । ya enam uktaprakārakam ātmānam avināśinam । kathaṃ kena prakāreṇa । sa puruṣaḥ । taṃ kṣetrajñaṃ kaṃ ghātayati । upāyaviśeṣo hetuḥ kartṛtvaṃ ca niṣiddhyate । kathaṃ vā hantīti svayaṃ kartṛtvamapi paścān niṣidhyate । na hy avināśī ca yo bhāvo avyabhicārādinā sa svayam udyamena parakartṛkanipātanena vā vināśayituṃ śakyo gaganavad iti ।

atra kleśabhīravaḥ kecit svamataṃ bhagavatyāropya varṇayanti viduṣaḥ sarvakarmapratiṣedha eva prakaraṇārtho abhipreto bhagavataḥ iti । hantigrahaṇam udāharaṇārtham । yāni karmāṇi śāstre vidhīyante tāny aviduṣo vihitānīti bhagavato niścayo niścaya ity atrābhidhīyate ।

na hīdaṃ pūrvapadānusandhānarahitam abhiprāyavarṇanaṃ lakṣyate । kathaṃ yuddhe pravṛttyartham ātmanaḥ sattvopavarṇanam atra kriyate । tasmād yuddhasva bhārata iti tam abhidhāya tatsiddhyartham eva jāyata iti । ārambhād yadi ca sarvakarmatyāga evābhipretaḥ syād ayaṃ śloko arjunāya na vaktavyaḥ syāt । bhagavatoktaś ca ṣaḍbhāvavikārarahita ātmā । yadi viduṣaḥ karmāsambhavaṃ ced astu । tasyāpi tatsamānam ity apravṛttir eva syāt । uttarāś ca gītāḥ sarvā na saṅgaccheran । ato neyaṃ mṛṣāśā kartavyā ।

svadharmatyāgenākṛṣṭacetasaḥ sukham āsīnā mokṣaṃ lobhemahīti ।
uttaratra ca jñānakarmasamuccayaṃ nyāyato nipuṇataram
upapādayiṣyāmaḥ ।।

hananāsambhavād avināśitvam uktaṃ tat katham ivety āha 

vāsāṃsi jīrṇāni yathā vihāya navāni gṛḥṇāti naroparāṇi ।
tathā śarīrāṇi vihāya jīrṇāny anyāni saṃyāti navāni dehī ।।

yathā jīrṇānāṃ kāryākṣamāṇāṃ vastrāṇāṃ parityāgas tathā śarīrāṇām । abhinavānāṃ copādānam । anyan navataraṃ kalyāṇataraṃ rūpaṃ kurute iti ca brāhmaṇam ।।

yāni ca vināśakāraṇāni śastrādīni prasiddhāni tāny apy enaṃ na vināśayantīty āha 

nainaṃ chindanti śastrāṇi nainaṃ dahati pāvakaḥ ।
na cainaṃ kledayanty āpo na śopayati mārutaḥ ।।

nainaṃ chindanti śāstrāṇi asiprabhṛtīni niravayavatvād ākāśavat । nainam agnir bhasmīkaroti । 
nainam āpo avayavaviśleṣaṇāya
kledayanti carmavat ।
nainaṃ mārutaḥ śoṣayati svedāpanayena ।।

tad asyāḥ pratijñāyā hetur ucyate । yasmād ayaṃ chedanādyarho na bhavati । katham 

acchedyo ayam adohyo ayam akledyo aśoṣya eva ca ।
nityaḥ sarvagataḥ sthāṇur acalo ayaṃ sanātanaḥ ।।

nityatvāt sarvagataḥ sarvagatatvāt sthāṇuḥ sthāṇutvād acala ity akṣarayojanā । sanātanaś cirantanaḥ । kutaś cit kāraṇān nāyaṃ

niṣpanno abhinava ity arthaḥ । nātra punaruktadoṣaś codanīyaḥ । durbodhatvād ātmavastunaḥ paryāyaśabdaiḥ punaḥ puas tad evocyate sukhapratipattaye ।।

kiṃ ca 

avyakto ayam acintyo ayam avikāryo ayam ucyate ।
tasmād evaṃ viditvainaṃ nānuśocitum arhasi ।।

indriyāgocaratvād avyakto ata evācintyaḥ । ya indriyagocaro gavādiḥ sa vyaktaś cintanīyaḥ । yo hi vyaktaḥ sa vikāryaḥ । ayaṃ tv avikāryaḥ । tasmād iti nigamanam । svarūpatas tāvad ātmano avināśitvaṃ tathoktam ।।

atha śarīrendriyopādhivināśād vināśaṃ tadutpattyā cotpattim ātmano manyase tathāpi śoko na yuktaḥ kartum ity āha 

atha cainaṃ nityajātaṃ nityaṃ vā manyase mṛtam ।
tathāpi tvaṃ mahāvāho nānuśocitum arhasi ।।
kasmāt । aupādhikayor janmanāśayor aparihāryatvāt tad āha 
jātasya hi dhruvo mṛtyur dhruvaṃ janma mṛtasya ca ।
tasmād aparihārye arthe na tvaṃ śocitum arhasi ।।

yena karmaṇā janmārambhas tasya karmaṇaḥ kṣaye dhruvo bhāvī mṛtyuḥ । mṛtasya cāvaśyambhāviśarīragrahaṇam । śarīrāntarārambhakāraṇānām anyeṣāṃ vidyamānatvāt punaḥ śarīraṃ punaḥ karmeti

saṃsāracakrasyānāditvāt । evaṃ vyākhyāyamāne dhruvaṃ janma mṛtasya ca iti ślokārtho avakalpate । 
nairātmyavādidarśanābhyupagamena vyākhyāne mṛtasya
punarjanmābhāvād
anupapattiḥ syāt ।।

itaś ca śokakaraṇam ayuktam 

avyaktādīni bhūtāni vyaktamadhyāni bhārata ।
avyaktanidhānāny eva tatra kā paridevanā ।।

avyaktaṃ pañcabhūtānāṃ sūkṣmāvasthā prakṛtiḥ tadādir yeṣāṃ bhūtānāṃ tānīmāni avyaktādīni । vyaktaṃ madhyaṃ yeṣāṃ tāni vyaktamadhyāni । vyaktaṃ sthūlāvasthocyate । kāraṇe pracaratvāt । avyakte nidhanaṃ vināśaḥ pralayo yeṣāṃ tāny avyaktanidhanāni svakāreṇa pralīnāni kāryakāraṇasaṅghātātmakāni । tatra kā paridevanā । śokanimittaḥ pralāpaḥ paridevanocyate ।

satkāryavādināṃ tv aupaniṣadānāṃ sāṅkhyānāṃ ca triṣv api kāleṣu sarve bhāvāḥ santi āvirbhāvatirobhāvamātratvād utpattivināśayoḥ । yathā ghaṭaś cūrṇarūpeṇa svakāreṇa vidyamānaḥ kumbhakāravyāpāreṇāvirbhavati mudgatādiyogena tirobhūtaḥ śaktyātmanā punar api kāraṇaṃ praviśati ।

apare ty āhuḥ avyaktam adarśanam । tadādir yeṣāṃ tāny avyaktādīni iti । atrocyate yadi svadarśanābhāvo adarśanaṃ tasyādyantatā nopapadyate abhāvasya bhāvotpattihetutvanirākaraṇāt । katham

saṃsāranakrusyānādi^ ślokārdho^ nairātmyavādi bhāvādamupapatti syāt yuktaṃ ṣyaktamadhyāni bhārana avyaktanidhanāneva tānīmānyavyaktādāni sthulāvasthocyate nidhānaṃvināśa paridevatā śokaniminnaḥ svaupaniṣadānāṃ saṃsyānāṃ bhāvassantyāvivetirobhāva^ svakāreṇa mudarādiyogena tirobhūtaḥ tasyādityantā bhāvokṣatti hetu^

asataḥ saj jāyata iti । tirohitaṃ hi dravyaṃ dravyāntarasyotpādakam । mṛtsuvarṇādau atiprasiddham etalloke । athādarśanam 
indriyāgocaratvād avyaktam abhipretaṃ
tato nāsti visaṃvāda iti ।
evaṃ tāvad ātmanaḥ svarūpāvināśatvān na yuktaḥ śokaḥ
kartum ity uktam ।।

durvijñeyaś cāyam ātmā yasmād bhūtasaṅghāte saty upalabhyate ta tasmād eva bahavo momuhyante । kecid bhūtacaitanyaṃ pratijānate vyatiriktam ātmānaṃ paśyanti apare vijñānasantānaṃ kṣaṇikam icchantīti । tad etad atra 

āścaryavat paśyati kaścid enam āścaryavad vadati tathaivam anyaḥ ।
āścaryavac cainam anyaḥ śṛṇoti śrutvāpy enaṃ veda na caiva kaścit ।।

yathāścaryam adbhutaṃ kaścit kadācit paśyati tadvad enam ātmānaṃ tathāścaryam iva paśyati kaścit । yadainaṃ kaścid vadati rūpādirahitam amūrtaṃ svasaṃvedyaṃ cetanasvabhāvam āścaryam iva kaścid enaṃ śṛṇoti । ātmaśravaṇaparāṅmukha eva hi prāyeṇa jantuḥ । śrutvāpy enaṃ na ca veda kaścit । tad apy āścaryam eveti । tasmād ātmatattvamuktalakṣaṇaṃ samyagavadhāryaṃ tan na vismaraṇīyam ityabhiprāyaḥ ।

kecid asya ślokasyārthaṃ svamatikalpanayā varṇayanti 

ātmā vā are draṣṭavyaḥ śrotavya ity asyāḥ śruter arthaḥ pratinirdiśyata iti । tad etad vyākhyānaṃ śrotriyeṣv eva śobhate । na hi tadarthapratyabhijñānam iha vidyate । vidhipratyayas tatra śrūyate । vartamāno apadeśaś cāyam । na ca tatrāścaryavad draṣṭavya ity artho abhidhīyate । na cākṣaramātrasādṛśyāt pradeśāntaragato arthaḥ śakyaḥ kalpayitum । na ca prakṛtārthopayogitvam asyāḥ kalpanāyāḥ । kiṃ ca 

śravaṇāyāpi bahubhir yo na labhyaḥ
śṛṇvanto api bahavo yaṃ na vidyuḥ ।
āścaryo vaktā kuśalo asya labdhā
āścaryo dhyātā kuśalo anuśiṣṭaḥ ।।
ity asya mantrasya yo arthaḥ so atra kathyate ।। 
durlabho ayam ātmopadeśa iti varṇayitum athedānīṃ prakaraṇārthopasaṃhāraḥ kriyate 

dehī nityam avadhyo ayaṃ dehe sarvasya bhārata ।
tasmāt sarvāṇi bhūtāni nānuśocitum arhasi ।।

yata evaṃ tasmād bhīṣmādīn anucintya na tvaṃ śocitum arhasi ।।

ātmaviṣayam anātmadharmaparikalpitam apanīya aśocyān 

ityādi yad uktaṃ tad upasaṃhṛtam । adhunā dharmaviṣayam adharmādhyāropaṇam । tannirāsāya prajñāvādāṃś ca ity uktaṃ yat tat prastūyate 

svadharmam api cāvekṣya na vikampitum arhasi ।
dharmyād dhi yuddhāc chreyo anyat kṣatriyasya na vidyate ।।

dharmād anapetaṃ dharmyaṃ yuddham । tato anyan na vidyate śreyaskaram । kṣatriyagrahaṇaṃ pradarśanārtham । anyeṣām api svadharmānuṣṭhānaṃ śreyaskaram । tad anena prakāreṇa śreyaskare jñānaṃ karma ca samuccinoti ।।

itaś ca yuddhaṃ kartavyam 

yadṛcchayā copapannaṃ svargadvāram apāvṛtam ।
sukhinaḥ kṣatriyāḥ pārtha labhante yuddham īdṛśam ।।

ayatnopanītaṃ svargasya dvāram apāvṛtam udghāṭitam ।
sukhinaḥ sukhabhāgino hi labhante yuddham īdṛśaṃ netare ।
atha vā kiṃ sukhinaḥ kleśabhīravo labhante ।
mandabhāgyā ityabhiprāyaḥ ।।

yadi cetthaṃ kartavyaṃ prāptam 

atha cet tvam imaṃ dharmyaṃ saṅgrāmaṃ na kariṣyasi ।
tataḥ svadharmaṃ kīrtiṃ ca hitvā pāpam avāpsyasi ।।

tataḥ svadharmaṃ kīrtiṃ ca mahādevādiyuddhanimittāṃ hitvā pāpaṃ pratipadyase ।।

na kevalam etāvad eveti śeṣaḥ 

akīrtiṃ cāpi bhūtāni kathayiṣyanti te avyayām ।
sambhāvitasya cākīrtir maraṇād atiricyate ।।

avyayāṃ santatāṃ dīrghakālām ity arthaḥ । śauryādibhiś ca 
guṇaiḥ sambhāvitasyākīrtir maraṇād atiricyate ।
tato maraṇaṃ varam ity arthaḥ ।।

kiṃ ca 

bhayād raṇād uparataṃ maṃsyante tvāṃ mahārathāḥ ।
yeṣāṃ ca tvaṃ bahumato bhūtvā yāsyasi lāghavam ।।

karṇādibhyo bhayād uparataṃ maṃsyante tvām aśvatthāmaprabhṛtayo mahārathāḥ । 
bahubhir guṇaiḥ dharmāśayas tvam añjasā
śūra ityādibhiḥ guṇaiḥ bahumato yāsyasi laghubhāvam ।
tad api kaṣṭataram ।।

kiṃ ca 

avācyavādāṃś ca bahūn vadiṣyanti tavāhitāḥ ।
nindantas tava sāmarthyaṃ tato duḥkhataraṃ nu kim ।।

ahitāḥ śatravaḥ । tato duḥkhataraṃ nu kim । nv iti vitarke । tato nānyad duḥkhataram astīty arthaḥ ।।

yuddhe tu kriyamāṇe guṇā evobhayatrety āha 

hato vā prāpsyasi svargaṃ jitvā vā bhokṣyase mahīm ।
tasmād uttiṣṭha kaunteya yuddhāya kṛtaniścayaḥ ।।

mohaṃ tyaktvottiṣṭha । yad vā mayāvaśyaṃ kartavyaṃ hi yuddham ity evaṃ kṛtaniścayaḥ ।।

tatra ca yuddhapravṛttasya buddhisāmyam upadeṣṭum āha 

sukhaduḥkhe same kṛtvā lābhālābhau jayājayau ।
tato yuddhāya yujyasva naivaṃ pāpam avāpsyasi ।।

sukhe harṣo duḥkhe viṣādaḥ । tāv akṛtvā । tayoḥ kinnimittam ity āha lābhālābhau samau kṛtvā lābhe sukham alābhe duḥkham utpadyate । tayoḥ punaḥ ko hetur ity āha jayājayau । jaye lābho viparyaye alābha iti । idam uktaṃ kurvan na pāpaṃ pratyavāyam avāpsyasīsi । tad evopasaṃhṛtam । anyathā papaśaṅkānupapatter iha svadharmaṃ kurvato yat pāpaṃ bhavati tan niṣidhyate । atha vā pāpam iti saṃsāravyasanam । tan naivam avāpsyasi । jñānakarmasamuccayānuṣṭhānam evam iti vyapadiśyate sāmyaparyantam ।।

idānīṃ jñānaprakaraṇam upasaṃharati karmaṇy upāyaviśeṣo vaktavya iti vibhāgajñāpanāya 

eṣā te abhihitā sāṅkhye buddhir yoge tv imāṃ śṛṇu ।
buddhyā yukto yayā pārtha karmabandhaṃ prahāsyasi ।।

yady api sāṅkhyaśabdaḥ kāpilatantre rūḍhaḥ guṇapuruṣavivekajñānaṃ yatropadiśyate tathāpi tad iha na gṛhyate । na tatsādṛśyād ātmayāthātmyavivekaḥ sāṅkhyaśabdenātra vyapadiśyate । tadviṣayā buddhir uktety arthaḥ । yogaḥ karmānuṣṭhānopāyaḥ । phalasaṅkalparahitatvaṃ samatvam । kṛtasya kriyamāṇasya vā karmaṇaḥ īśvarārpaṇam iti । tvam imāṃ buddhiṃ śṛṇu । tāṃ viśinaṣṭi śrotuś cittasamādhānāya ।

yayā buddhyā yuktaḥ karmabandhaṃ karmaiva bandhaḥ karmānekajanmasañcitaṃ prahāsyasi tyakṣyasi ।

kecid atra sāṅkhyaśabdenodgīthādyupāsanānām atimokṣasya sampadaś ca vidhāyakaṃ śāstram etat sarvaṃ vyapadiśyata iti bruvate ।

atrocyate । tad etad aprastutam anupayogyam ākasmikam upanyastam iti naḥ pratibhāti । kutaḥ । puruṣaviśeṣaviṣayās tūpāsanāsampado atimokṣaś ca । na ca tā ātmopāsanāḥ । atra ca śokamohākulitacetasas tadapanayanāyātmayāthātmyavarṇanārthaṃ prakaraṇam । evaṃ ca kvodgīthādayaḥ kvedaṃ prakaraṇam । na ca sāṅkhyaśabdaḥ paribhāṣayā vinātimokṣādiṣu varteta । tasmāt paurvāparyaparyālocanayā sambandhyamāno yo arthaḥ sa sāṅkhyaśabdayogyo vyākhyeyaḥ । sa cāsmābhir ukta iti ।

yogaśabdo apy atra samatvaṃ yoga ucyate 
ity upasaṃhāravacanād
anuṣḥānopāyavacano nānyatra yojanīya iti ।।

buddhiyuktasya karmaṇo guṇāntaram ucyate 

nehātikramanāśo asti pratyavāyo na vidyate ।
svalpam apy asya dharmasya trāyate mahato bhayāt ।।

atikrāmati saṃsāraduḥkhaṃ yena buddhiyuktena karmaṇā so atikramaḥ । abhikrama iti kecit paṭhanti । arthas tu sa eva ।

nāśo niṣphalatvam । iha mokṣamārge avasthāya kriyamāṇasya
karmaṇo niṣphalatvaṃ nāsti yathā kṛṣṇāder anekāntikaphalatvaṃ nāpi cikitsakakṛtadharmavat pratyavāyo vidyate । pratyuta svalpam api 
yathāśaktyanuṣṭhitasya dharmasya sambandhi
trāyate rakṣaty anuṣṭhātāraṃ
mahataḥ saṃsārabhayāt ।।

ātmaviṣayā karmaviṣayā buddhir ekaivaikaphalatvād iti darśayitum āha 

vyavasāyātmikā buddhir ekaiva kurunandana ।
bahuśākhā hy anantāś ca buddhayo avyavasāyinām ।।

samuccitābhyāṃ jñānakarmabhyām apavargo avāpyate yathāgneyādibhir itaretaraṃ yuktair yāgaiḥ svargaḥ । sā ceyaṃ vyavasāyātmikā buddhir ekā । avyavasāyināṃ tu kevalakarmiṇāṃ kevalajñānavādināṃ 
ca karmākaraṇe prayatamānānāṃ bahuśākhā
bahuprabhedā asaṅkhyeyāś
ca buddhayo bhavanti ।।

tatra kevalakarmiṇo adhikṛtyāha 

yām imāṃ puṣpitāṃ vācaṃ pravadanty avipaścitaḥ ।
vedavādaratāḥ pārtha nānyad astīti vādinaḥ ।।

yām imāṃ vakṣyamāṇāṃ puṣpitāṃ phalaprasavitrīṃ vākyalakṣaṇāṃ vācam anātmavido vipaścito vedavākyeṣu agnihotraṃ juhuyāt svargakāmaḥ ityādiṣu ratāḥ karmaṇā niratiśayasukhaṃ

svargaśabdavācyaṃ prāpyate । 
tato anyad apavargākhyaṃ sukhaṃ nāstīti
vādino vadanaśīlāś
ca pravadanti ।।

itaḥ 

kāmātmānaḥ svargaparā janmakarmaphalapradām ।
kriyāviśeṣabahulāṃ bhogaiśvaryagatiṃ prati ।।

aprāptasya prāptīcchā kāmaḥ । tadanuraktacetasa ity arthaḥ । svargaḥ paraḥ puruṣārtho yeṣāṃ te svargaparāḥ svargapradhānāḥ । janmakarmaphalapradām । karmaṇaḥ phalaṃ karmaphalaṃ । janmayuktaṃ karmaphalaṃ pradadātīti janmakarmaphalapradām । vācam ity adhikriyate । punar api kiṃviśiṣṭām । kriyāviśeṣabahulām । kriyāṇāṃ viśeṣā atibahulā bahuprakārā yasyāṃ vāci tām । kiṃ prati pravṛttām ity āha bhogaiśvaryagatiṃ prati । bhogaś caiśvaryaṃ ca tayor gatiḥ prāptis tām uddiśya । bhogaḥ sukhavedanā । aham eṣāṃ patiḥ svāmīti yatrābhimāno jāyate tadāiśvaryam । athavā gater evobhayaṃ viśeṣaṇam । 
kīdṛśagatiṃ prati ।
janmakarmaphalapradāṃ kriyāviśeṣabahulāṃ prati ।
puṣpitāṃ vācaṃ pratīty arthaḥ ।।

teṣāṃ caivaṃ vadatām 

bhogaiśvaryaprasaktānāṃ tayāpahṛtacetasām ।
vyavasāyātmikā buddhiḥ samādhau na vidhīyate ।।

tayā pūrvoktayā vācāpahṛtavivekajñānānāṃ jñānakarmasamuccayalakṣaṇā vyavasāyātmikā buddhiḥ samādhau । samādhīyate asmin

cittam iti samādhir ātmā । tasminn ātmani na vidhīyate na sambhavatīty arthaḥ । athavā samādhānaṃ samādhis tadviṣayā buddhiḥ । apare punar yuktaṃ vyākhyānam ananusarantas tatpratimānaṃ kalpayanto vadanti । sarveṣāṃ kila karmakāṇḍagatānāṃ vākyānāṃ hi dvividhaṃ phalam anvayanibandhanaṃ tātparyasamadhigamyaṃ ca । tatrānvayikaṃ svargabrahmavarcasādiphalam anvayanibandhanam । śamadamādihetutayānuṣṭhātṝṇāṃ vyavasāyātmikāyāṃ buddhau yogyatāpādanaṃ tatrānvayaphalam eva svargādi ye vadanty avipaścitas te tātparyaphalam ajānanta iti yojayanti ।

atrābhidhīyate । tad etacchabdapramāṇabāhyaṃ puruṣabuddhiprabhavaṃ nyāyavidbhyo nātirocate । na hi svargakāmo yajeta ity asya vākyasya dvāv arthau tatra yāgena svargaṃ prāpnuyād ity ayam evaiko artho vidhīyate । padārthasaṃsargo hi vākyārthaḥ । na punar yāgānuṣṭhānena jñānayogyatāṃ kuryād iti kasyacit padasya tātparyo dṛśyate । padārthapūrvakaś ca vākyārtho jñāne nimittam iti sthitiḥ । na ca puruṣecchāvaśād vākyasya nārthāntaram ākṣipati । ye hi śrūyamāṇam artham anādṛtya vākyasyārthāntaraṃ kalpayanti ta eva sutarām avipaścito na mīmāṃsakā ye śabdapramāṇavṛttaṃ bruvate śamadamādayo yāgānuṣṭhānasādhyā iti । kiṃ tarhi । śānto dānta uparataḥ

ityādivacanagamyāḥ saṃsāradoṣadarśanena cittavṛttinirodhāt sādhanāgranthagauravabhayād uparamyate । pratiślokaṃ caivam anye cānye vyākhyātāro pūrvam artham utprekṣamāṇā āhopuruṣikāṃ loke prathayanti । tatra yat prāmāṇyavṛttam uktaṃ tad atra bhavanto vidāṃ kurvantu ।

ātmajñānena tu nityakarmaṇāṃ samuccayo vacanāntareṇa tam evaṃ vedānuvacanena 
iti niyatasya tu sannyāsaḥ karmaṇo
nopapadyate iti ca tyāgapratiṣedhāt teṣām
evātmanām ।।

traiguṇyaviṣayā vedā nistraiguṇyo bhavārjuna ।
nirdvandvo nityasattvastho niryogakṣema ātmavān ।।

trayāṇāṃ sattvarajastamasāṃ guṇānāṃ karma tat traiguṇyam । sa viṣayaḥ prakāśayitavyo yeṣāṃ vedānāṃ te traiguṇyaviṣayāḥ । guṇānāṃ ca saṃsārapravartanaṃ karma । tadviṣayā vedāḥ । tatra sattvam upasarjanam । rajastamasī tūtkaṭe । tābhyāṃ vaśīkṛtaḥ puruṣaḥ ihāmutraphaleṣu karmasu pravartamānaḥ saṃsāracakraṃ nātivartata iti tātparyārthaḥ । tvaṃ tu nistraiguṇyo bhava । traiguṇyam ativartasva । katham । nirdvandvaḥ nityasattvasthaḥ । kāmakrodhau rāgadveṣau sukhaduḥkhe śītoṣṇe iti dvandvāni tāni sahasvety arthaḥ । sattvaguṇastho bhūtvā dhairyam avalambya । niryogakṣemaś ca । aprāptasya svīkaraṇaṃ yogaḥ prāptasya parirakṣaṇaṃ kṣemaḥ । 
tayor yatamānasya na
vyavasāyātmikā buddhiḥ ।
ātmavān apramatta ity arthaḥ ।।

na ca traiguṇyaviṣayeṣu vedeṣv adhyayanaśravaṇavyākhyānādipareṇa tvayā kṛtsnam āyuḥ paryupayoktavyam । kiṃ kāraṇam ity āha 

yāvad artha udapāne sarvataḥ saṃplutodake ।
tāvān sarveṣu vedeṣu brāhmaṇasya vijānataḥ ।।

kūpataḍāgādau yāvān arthaḥ snānapānādiḥ puruṣasya tāvān arthaḥ salilapūrṇe deśe prāvṛṭsamaye nādhiko vidyate । yathāyaṃ dṛṣṭāntas tathā jñānakarmasamuccayapratipādanapare vedabhāge yāvān arthas tāvān ekāhāhīnasatrapratipādake kṛtsnavede । ataḥ kāmyakarmābhiyogaṃ vihāya jñānakarmanityakarmapratipādanaparabhoge abhiyogavatā bhavitavyam iti ।

apareṣāṃ vyākhyā yāvān arthaḥ sarvataḥ saṃplutodake tāvān udapāne tatkārye tatraivāntarbhavatīty arthaḥ । tathā vijānataḥ sannyāsino jñāne sarvataḥ saṃplutodakasthānīyeṣu sarveṣu vedeṣu tāvān arthaḥ । tatraiva samastakarmaprayojanam antarbhavatīty arthaḥ iti ।

tad asmin vyākhyāne yadi jñānam āhātmyaṃ tadānīm abhyanujñātaṃ jñānasyaitanmāhātmyaṃ yatkāmātmanāṃ karma saṃsārahetur bhavati tadātmīyasvabhāvaṃ vihāya tatsamparkād utkarṣahetutvaṃ pratipadyate । yathā rasaspṛṣṭatāmravarṇatā suvarṇatāṃ pratipadyate । raso api tāmrasamparkāt puruṣārthasādhanam । evam anyonyasamuccitam apavargārtham ity uktam । tathā ca vasiṣṭhenoktam 

yathānnaṃ madhusaṃyuktaṃ madhu cānnena saṃyutam । evaṃ tapaś ca vidyā ca saṃyuktā bheṣajaṃ mahat ।। iti ।

athaitad vyākhyāne karma niṣprayojanaṃ vaktavyaṃ । jñānād eva kevalād apavargaṃ ity abhiprāyeṇa । tad asad ity ucyate । śābdapramāṇabāhyatvād asyārthasyety uktam anyatra ca nipuṇataraṃ vakṣyate । brāhmaṇasyeti ca sāmānyaśravaṇaṃ na sanyāsina iti 
viśiṣṭam ।
tasmāt sarvāśramāṇāṃ sarvadvijānāṃ ca muktiḥ ।
tathā ca janakādayaḥ smaryante ।
tasmād vyavasāyātmikāyāṃ buddho sthātavyam iti sthitam ।।

tatra yad uktam yoge tv imām iti ko asau yoga ity āha 

karmaṇy evādhikāras te mā phaleṣu kadācana ।
mā karmaphalahetur bhūrmā te saṅgo astv akarmaṇi ।।
svāśramavihiteṣu karmasv adhikāraḥ । phaleṣu cānadhikāraḥ ।metiśabdaḥ pratiṣedhavācī । nāsty adhikāraḥ ।
karmaṇy evety evakāraḥ phalavyavacchedārtho na jñānavyavacchedārthaḥ । 
tasya eṣā te abhihitā ityādyupadiṣṭatvāt ।
nanu karmaṇy evakāraḥ phalaṃ hi kriyāsādhyam ।
na tatrāpi prasakto asau yena pratiṣidhyeta ity āśaṅkyāha 
mā te saṅgo astv akarmaṇi ।।

akaraṇe saktir na kartavyā । kathaṃ tarhi kartavyety āha 
yogasthaḥ kuru karmāṇi saṅgaṃ tyaktvā dhanañjaya ।
siddhyasiddhyoḥ samo bhūtvā samatvaṃ yoga ucyate ।।

yāni nityāni karmāṇi sandhyārādhanasaṅgrāmādīni tāni yogasthaḥ kuru । phalasaṅgaṃ tyaktvā । phalasaṅgena hi kriyamāṇe karmaṇi siddhyasiddhyor vaiṣamyam । siddhau harṣaḥ phalasiddhau viṣāda iti । īśvarārādhanārthe tu kriyamāṇe nāsti vaiṣamyam । sa eva kartā । tadātmakaṃ ca karmeti kriyamāṇaṃ tatsiddhihetutvaṃ 
pratipadyata ity arthaḥ ।
tad idaṃ samatvaṃ yoga ucyate ।।

samatvabuddhitvād asmāt karmaṇaḥ kevalam 

dūreṇa hy avaraṃ karma buddhiyogād dhanañjaya buddhau śaraṇam anviccha kṛpaṇāḥ phalahetavaḥ ।।
hiśabdo hetau । jñānarahitaṃ karma dūreṇātiviprakarṣeṇāvaraṃ
jaghanyam । yujyata iti yogaḥ karma । buddhyuktāt karmaṇaḥ sakāśād ity arthaḥ । yata evaṃ tasmād buddhau śaraṇam anviccha buddhim āśrayety arthaḥ । karmapravṛttikāle । yataḥ kṛṣṇāḥ phalahetavaḥ । kevalaṃ karmaṇaḥ phalaṃ pravṛttihetur yeṣāṃ te phalahetavaḥ ।।

buddhiyuktaḥ kurvann eva kinnu phalaṃ prāpnotīti tad ucyate 

buddhiyukto jahātīme ubhe sukṛtaduṣkṛte ।
tasmād yogāya yujyasva yogaḥ karmasu kauśalam ।।

īśvarārādhanārthaṃ karmety anayā buddhyā yuktaḥ karma kurvan parityajaty anārabdhaphale janmāntarakṛte śubhāśubhakarmaṇī । ye tv ārabdhaphale tayor bhogenaiva kṣayaḥ । asmin śarīre tayor bhogarūpeṇa pariṇatatvāt । tathā ca śrutiḥ tasya tāvad eva ciraṃ yāvad asmāc charīrān na vimokṣye atha sampatsya iti । yāvad asmāc charīrān na vimokṣyate tāvad asya viduṣaś ciram ity avadhikaraṇāt । tasmāt samatvayogāya yujyasva । kaḥ punar yogaḥ । yogaḥ karmasu kauśalam । idaṃ tāvad brahmaṇi samarpaṇaṃ karmaṇaḥ phalasaṅkalparahitatā ca ।।

kiṃ punar evaṃ kṛte syāt 

karmajaṃ buddhiyuktā hi phalaṃ tyaktvā manīṣiṇaḥ ।
janmabandhavinirmuktāḥ padaṃ gacchanty anāpayam ।।

śubhetarakarmajaṃ phalaṃ tyaktvā manīṣiṇo manasa īṣiṇo 
brahmabhāvāpāditamanovṛttayo janmaiva bandhas tato
vinirmuktāḥ padaṃ viṣṇoḥ sthānaṃ gacchanty anāmayaṃ
sarvopadravarahitam ।।

kadā punar evaṃ kramas tvaṃ śuddhatarabuddhir nirvedaṃ pratipadyase । tad āha 

yadā te mohakalilaṃ buddhir vyatitariṣyati ।
tadā gantāsi nirvedaṃ śrotavyasya śrutasya ca ।।

kalilaṃ gahanam ucyate । tathā cābhidhānakośe kalilaṃ gahanaṃ viduḥ iti । moha eva kalilam । moho ajñānam । etad uktaṃ bhavati ajñānaṃ durgaṃ yadā vyatikramiṣyasi 
tadā gantāsi nirvedaṃ
śrotavyasya śāstrasya śrutasya ca ।
tadā ca mohadurgaṃ vyatitīrya te
buddhiḥ sthiram avasthāsyata iti ।।

śrutivipratipannā te yadā sthāsyati niścalā ।
samādhāv acalā buddhis tadā yogam avāpsyasi ।।

acalā iti punar vivakṣyate । tadā paramātmayogam avāpsyasi । tataḥ pūrvoktam upapannam padaṃ gacchanty anāmayam iti ।।

anantaravṛttena ślokadvayena buddher niścalatve pratipādite paramātmano abhimukhīkaraṇāyāvasaraṃ labdhvārjuna uvāca 

sthitaprajñasya kā bhāṣā samādhisthasya keśava ।
sthitadhīḥ kiṃ prabhāṣeta kim āsīta vrajeta kim ।।

sthitaprajñaḥ kena lakṣaṇena bhāṣyate vyapadiśyata ity arthaḥ । sa ca sthitadhīḥ kiṃ prabhāṣeta kim asau vaktīty arthaḥ । 
kimparo bhūtvāsītety arthaḥ ।
akarmakatvād asya dhātor evaṃ yojyate ।
kiṃ vā vrajeta gacchet prāpnuyād iti ।
vyatyayenātmanepadam ।।

tatra kā bhāṣā ity etat prathamaṃ nirucyate 

śrībhagavān uvāca 
aiśvaryasya samagrasya dharmasya yaśasaḥ śriyaḥ ।
vairāgyasyātha mokṣasya ṣaṇṇāṃ bhaga iti dhvaniḥ ।।

prajahāti yadā kāmān sarvān pārtha manogatān ।
ātmany evātmanā tuṣṭaḥ sthitaprajñas tadocyate ।।

bāhyārthaviṣayān nānāsāṅkalpān yadā tyajati tadā bāhyaviṣayasaṅkalpābhāve kvāyaṃ vartate । kena tuṣṭaś caratīty āha ātmany evānandasvarūpe amohitenātmanāntaḥkaraṇena janmamaraṇajamohādiviṣādena mahauṣadhabrahmāmṛtapānāsvādajanitapremaprabandhaniścalavṛttinā parituṣṭaḥ sthitaprajñas tadocyate ।

yānīha sthitaprajñalakṣaṇāni vakṣyante tāny eva sādhanāni prayatnato anuṣṭheyānīti । na hy ananuṣṭhīyamānāni sattāṃ labhamānāni lakṣaṇāni bhavantīti । tatra yad etad ucyate pūrvāvasthāyāṃ lakṣaṇam iti tad anupapannam । 
tasminn eva kāle sādhanatvaṃ tasminn eva ca kāle
lakṣaṇatvam iti tad anupapannam ।
