na tasmin yaugapadyaṃ sādhanatvalakṣaṇatvayoḥ ।।

kiṃ ca 

duḥkheṣv anudvignamanāḥ sukheṣu vigataspṛhaḥ ।
vītarāgabhayakrodhaḥ sthitadhī munir ucyate ।।

yaḥ sarvatrānabhisnehas tat tat prāpya śubhāśubham ।
nābhinandati na dveṣṭi tasya prajñā pratiṣṭhitā ।।

yadā saṃharate cāyaṃ kūrmo aṅgānīva sarvaśaḥ ।
indriyāṇīndriyārthebhyaḥ sthitaprajñas tadocyate ।।

viṣayā vinivartante nirāhārasya dehinaḥ ।
rasavarjaṃ raso apy asya paraṃ dṛṣṭvā nivartate ।।

yatato hy api kaunteya puruṣasya vipaścitaḥ ।
indriyāṇi pramāthīni haranti prasabhaṃ manaḥ ।।

tāni saṃyamya manasā yukta āsīta matparaḥ ।
vaśe hi yasyendriyāṇi tasya prajñā pratiṣṭhitā ।।

dhyāyato viṣayān puṃsaḥ saṅgas teṣūpajāyate ।
saṅgāt sañjāyate kāmaḥ kāmāt krodho abhijāyate ।।

krodhād bhavati sammohaḥ sammohāt smṛtivibhramaḥ ।
smṛtibhraṃśād buddhināśo buddhināśāt praṇaśyati ।।

rāgadveṣaviyuktais tu viṣayān indriyaiś caran ।
ātmavaśyair vidheyātmā prasādam adhigacchati ।।

prasāde sarvaduḥkhānāṃ hānir asyopajāyate ।
prasannacetaso hy āśu buddhiḥ paryavatiṣṭhate ।।

nāsti buddhir ayuktasya na cāyuktasya bhāvanā ।
na cābhāvayataḥ śāntir aśāntasya kutaḥ sukham ।।

indriyāṇāṃ hi caratāṃ yan mano anuvidhīyate ।
tad asya harati prajñāṃ vāyur nāvam ivāmbhasi ।।

tasmād yasya mahābāho nigṛhītāni sarvaśaḥ ।
indriyāṇīndriyārthebhyas tasya prajñā pratiṣṭhitā ।।

yā niśā sarvabhūtānāṃ tasyāṃ jāgarti saṃyamī ।
yasyāṃ jāgrati bhūtāni sā niśā paśyato muneḥ ।।

āpūryamāṇam acalapratiṣṭhaṃ samudram āpaḥ praviśanti yadvat ।
tadvat kāmā yaṃ praviśanti sarve sa śāntim āpnoti na kāmakāmī ।।

vihāya kāman yaḥ sarvān pumāṃś carati niḥspṛhaḥ ।
nirmamo nirahaṅkāraḥ sa śāntim adhigacchati ।।

eṣā brāhmī sthitiḥ pārtha naināṃ prāpya vimuhyati ।
sthitvāsyām antakakāle api brahmanirvāṇam ṛcchati ।।

iti śrībhagavadbhāskarakṛte gītābhāṣye dvitīyo adhyāyaḥ ।।

atha tṛtīyo adhyāyaḥ

arjuna uvāca jyāyasī cet karmaṇas te matā buddhir janārdana । tatkiṃ karmaṇi ghore māṃ niyojayasi keśava ।।

vyāmiśreṇeva vākyena buddhiṃ mohayasīva me ।
tad ekaṃ vada niścitya yena śreyo aham āpnuyām ।।

bhagavān uvāca 

loke asmiṃ dvividhā niṣṭhā purā proktā mayānagha ।
jñānayogena sāṅkhyānāṃ karmayogena yoginām ।।

asmin loke niṣṭhā dvividhā sthitiḥ lakṣaṇahetuḥ । jñānam eva yogaḥ । tena sāṅkhyā jñānino lakṣyante । yathā tridaṇḍena tridaṇḍo anāśramī lakṣyate । ekārthatvāt । evaṃ karmayogena yogināṃ samatvam ayogavatām īśvarārādhanārthaṃ karma kurvatāṃ sākṣātkarmaṇo api jñānotpattyupāyatvāt । tathā coktam 

jñānam utpadyate puṃsāṃ kṣayāt pāpasya karmaṇaḥ ।
yathādarśatalaprakhye paśyanty ātmānam ātmani ।।
ātmani buddhāv ity arthaḥ । pāpakṣayaś ca dharmāt 
dharmeṇa pāpam apanuda iti tapasā brahma vijijñāsasva iti ca śruteḥ । teṣāṃ yam aniyamavattvād alpam api jñānasāmānyam astīti । ataḥ kvacit pradhānam iti । etāvān viśeṣo atra samuccayaḥ

jñānakarmaṇo pratipāditaḥ । na hy atra smārtena karmaṇā śrautena vā jñānasya samuccaya iti । ayam api viśeṣa upayujyate yathā prāktanena karmaṇā aihikasya karmaṇaḥ samuccayasyopapattiḥ । na tv atrāśramavikalpa āśramasamuccayo vā bhagavatā vivakṣitaḥ । ātmanaḥ sākṣātkāraṇāt prāgavasthāyāṃ karmaprādhānyam uttaratra jñānaprādhānyam ity upadeśāt । ataḥ sthiraṃ pratipuruṣam apavargādhikāre jñānakarmaṇī samuccīyeta ity etatparam idaṃ śāstram iti samyag darśitam । tadvākyāni ca tathaiva vyākhyātavyāni ।

anye punaḥ patrair iva phalāni chādayantaḥ praśnam uttaraṃ cānyathā varṇayanti । prajahāti yadā ity ārabhya sarvakarmatyāgināṃ sāṅkhyānāṃ jñānād eva kevalān niḥśreyasaḥ prāptir uktā । mama ca karmaṇy evādhikāras te iti karmaiva kevalam upadiṣṭam । na tata eva śreyaḥprāptir ity ākulitabuddhir arjuna uvāca jyāyasī cet iti । uttaraṃ ca bhāgavatam upapadyate sāṅkhyānāṃ kevalāj jñānān niḥśreyasaprāptiḥ । karmayogināṃ tu niṣṭhayaiveti । dve niṣṭhe bhinnapuruṣaviṣaya iti sarvakarmatyāga eva samyagdarśināṃ sāṅkhyānām itihāsapurāṇopaniṣatsu ca darśitaḥ ।

na ca nityakarmākaraṇe sannyāsināṃ pratyavāyo bhavati adhikārasya nivṛttatvāt । adhikāribhis tyajyamānaṃ karma doṣam

āvahati । na cākaraṇād abhāvāt pratyavāyotpattiḥ ।
tasmād vividiṣāvatām anutpannajñānānām api viduṣāṃ cotpannajñānānāṃ karmatyāga eveti bruvate ।

athānye śrutau tu sāṅkhyānāṃ jñānād eva niḥśreyasam uktam । ātmanaś ca karma kartavyam uktam iti śrutismṛtinyāyanipuṇāḥ pratyācakṣate । tenaivam api yojayituṃ śakyate sāṅkhyānāṃ jñānād eva niḥśreyasam uktam ātmanaś ca karma kartavyam uktam iti vivekenārjuno avagatavān yadi tat kathaṃ tasyākulībhāvaḥ tad ekaṃ vada iti ca nopapadyate । bhāgavataṃ cottaraṃ na saṅgacchate dviprakāroktā niṣṭheti ।

tatraivaṃ vaktavyam । syāt karmaṇy evaadhikāras te na niḥśreyas suniṣṭhayor bhinnapuruṣaviṣayatvāt । jñānaṃ kasyacid eva kasyacit karmaiveti prakāramātropadeśāya । tad uktam vividiṣāvato viduṣaś ca sarvakarmasannyāsa iti । tac chrutismṛtinyāyabāhyaṃ viruddhaṃ ca । yadi tāvad utpanne jñāne prayojanābhāvāt karmatyāge hetur vidyate yadi vā vidvadbhis traivarṇikaiḥ karma tyajyeta svacchandatayā sarve karmiṇo brahmavidaḥ samudraṃ praviśeyuḥ । vividiṣāvatām api karmayogam eva darśayati tam etaṃ vedānuvacanena brāhmaṇā vividiṣanti yajñena dānena tapaseti ca ।

yadi cāviduṣo api karmatyāga eva vihitaḥ syād viduṣaḥ karmānarthakyād iti hetvabhidhānam anupapannam । tad evaṃ viruddhaṃ bhāṣamāṇaḥ kathaṃ grāhyavacanaḥ syāt । na copaniṣatsu sarvatyāgagamakaṃ liṅgam asti । na karmaṇā prajayā dhanena tyāgenaikenāmṛtatvam ānaśuḥ ity atra prajāsāhacaryāl lokaprāptyarthaṃ kāmyakarmatyāgo gīyate । itarāpi śrutiḥ nyāsam eṣāṃ tapasātiriktam āhuḥ iti nyāsaśabdena tatra brahmābhidhīyate na karmatyāgaḥ । prakṛtāṃ vācam ity atra damaśamādīnāṃ tapasāṃ ca tatprāptisādhanatvāt tadapekṣayātiriktavacanam । prāptavyaṃ hi prāptisādhanād atiriktaṃ bhavati । anyaiś ca sannyāsaśabdo atra nyāsaśabdasyānarthāntare prayuktaḥ । yathā ājyaiḥ stuvate ity ājyaśabdaḥ stotreṣu loke ghṛtavacanaḥ । tad iha bhrāntyā tasya tyāgārthakatvaṃ kalpitam । tathā hi dhanimātrakṛto hy eva janānāṃ mativibhramaḥ । paurvāparyāparāmṛṣṭaḥ śabdo anyāṃ kurute matim ।। iti । itihāse ca tatra tatra mokṣārthibhiḥ karma kartavyam ity uktam । tathā hi śukānupreśne karmaṇā manasā vācā yo dharmanirataḥ sadā । aphalākāṅkṣasiddhaś ca sa mokṣam adhigacchati ।। iti ।

yat tu tyaja dharmam adharmaṃ ca iti tasyottaraślokād arthanirṇayaḥ tyaja dharmaṃ saṅkalpajam । tyajādharmam ahiṃsayā iti । phalasaṅkalpatyāgo na svarūpatyāga iti ।

yad uktam akaraṇe pratyavāyo nāstīti tad asat । akurvan vihitaṃ karma iti smṛteḥ । na ca śāstre yaḥ svecchākṛtas tyāgaḥ pratyavāyanivāraṇe samarthaḥ । na cākaraṇasyābhāvasya pratyavāyanimittatvaṃ nāstīti śakyaṃ vaktum । rājājñayā niyuktānāṃ bhṛtyānām uktākaraṇe vadhabandhādidoṣadarśanāt । katham asataḥ saj jāyeta iti dravyābhiprāyā śrutiḥ । asato dravyāntarasyotpattir nāstīti tatrārthaḥ । dravyasya hi suvarṇāder eva svīkāryam । na cāvasthāvattvam antareṇāvasthayopapadyate ity abhipretyāsadutpattiniṣedhaḥ । tathā vihitānuṣṭhāne api prayojanam asti mokṣārthināṃ duritakṣayo anyeṣām abhyudayaḥ । tasmād gītāśāstre anyatra vā karmaṇāṃ mokṣārthatā na kartavyeti sthitam ।

anye punar anyathā ślokaṃ prasthāpayanti । karmādbhutam udgīthādyupāsanam । tena yogāt karmāṇy apavargabhogyāni bhavantīty eva kṛtvoktam jñānayogena sāṅkhyānām iti । karmaṇā nityanaimittikena yogāt karmayogaḥ । tena yogināṃ paramātmopāsakānāṃ niṣṭhokteti । tad etad anṛtaṃ bhāṣitam iti te manyante ।

katham udgīthāvayavādyupāsanakarmaṇaḥ samṛddhyarthatvān nāpavargayogitvam । om ity etadakṣaram udgītham upāsīta ity udgīthāvayavasyauṅkārasyopāsanaṃ tatra vihitaṃ na brahmopāsanam iti tatraivaṃ sthitam । na codgīthādyupāsanasambandhād asyāpavargahetutvam । kiṃ tarhi । yajñena dānena iti । ātmajñānasahakāritayā viniyogādikaṃ ca 
gītādvitīyādhyāyoktena
jñānakarmapravibhāgaprajñāpanārtham ity uktam ।
yogaś ca tatra karmasu kauśalam ity uktaṃ na paropāsanam
ity alaṃ prasaṅgena ।।

sāṅkhyā parivrājakā bruvate kevalād eva jñānān muktiḥ sarvaṃ śrautaṃ smārtaṃ ca karma tyaktavyam ahetutvād iti । teṣāṃ pratyākhyānāya bhagavān uvāca 

na karmaṇām anārambhān naiṣkarmyaṃ puruṣo aśnute ।
na ca sannyasanād eva siddhiṃ samadhigacchati ।।

niṣkarmaṇo bhāvo naiṣkarmyam । karmaśabdena puṇyāpuṇyayor grahaṇam । tadrahitaṃ mokṣam ity arthaḥ । anārambhān mokṣaṃ puruṣo nāśnute na prāpnoti । arthād etad uktaṃ bhavati ārambhāt prāpnotīti । karmasāpekṣāj jñānān muktir na kevalād ityabhiprāyaḥ । atha manyase kiṃ karmaṇā parivrajyāsahitāj jñānān niḥśreyaḥ sambhavaviṣyatīti cen nety āha na ca sannyasanād eva jñānasahitāt sannyāsād eva

turyāśramagrahaṇāt siddhiṃ mokṣaṃ nādhigacchati । karmasahitam eva jñānaṃ siddhisādhanam । āśramapāratantryān manasaḥ । sarveṣām āśramāṇāṃ samuccayāt siddhir iti bhāgavataṃ mataṃ suniścitam ।

yathedam eva sāṅkhyadarśanam āśritya sarvadharmatyāgam ekavaiṇavino vadanti । te api hy etenāpāstā veditavyāḥ nirākaraṇanyāyasyāviśeṣāt ।

atra te pratyavatiṣṭhante asmaddarśane apīyaṃ gītā ghaṭate । kathaṃ karmārambhād eva naiṣkarmyam aśnute jñānotpattyupāyatvāt karmaṇāṃ । tasmāt karma kartavyam । tato jñānotpattiḥ । tato mokṣa iti । na ca sannyasanād eva jñānarahitāt siddhiṃ samadhigacchatīti ।

tad idam apavyākhyānam anye pratyācakṣate । yadi tāvad ayam artho naiṣkarmyaṃ niṣkarmatā karmābhāva iti syāt tadā virodho atra । na karmārambhāt karmābhāvaḥ । kiṃ tarhy anārambhād eva । atha naiṣkarmyaśabdena jñānaniṣṭhatocyate karmākṛtvā jñānotpattyasambhavād iti । tathāpy aviduṣaṃ sarvakarmatyāgopadeśo bhavato viruddhyeta । tathā coktam upadeśagranthe tvaṃpadārthavivekāya sannyāsaḥ sarvakarmaṇām iti ।

asyāyam arthaḥ naiṣkarmyaṃ mokṣaḥ । karmārambhān mokṣaṃ prāpnotīti । evam api

kevalakarmaṇāṃ mokṣaḥ prasajyata iti jñānopadeśānarthakyam । atha jñānasahitāt karmaṇas tatprāptir ity evaṃ saty aṅgīkṛto asmatpakṣo bhavatā bhadramukhena । evaṃ ca pūrvārdhe vyākhyāte na ca sannyasanād eva ity atiricyate । karmatyāgam āśaṅkya na karmaṇām anārambhāt ity uktam ।

sannyāsaśabdenāpi karmatyāga eva tvatpakṣe abhidhīyate । na ca jñānarahitāt karmatyāgān mokṣaḥ kenacit pratijñāto yenedaṃ nirākaraṇārthaṃ syāt । yadi cāvidvāṃsaḥ karmākurvāṇā mucyeran yugapad eva kṛtsnaṃ jagan mucyeta । na ca jñānakarmaṇor virodhāt karmatyāgo varam virodhasyāsiddhatvāt । kin na paśyati bhagavantam varta eva ca karmaṇi iti vadantam । sākṣād brahmaiva svayam evārjunasya sārathyaṃ gatavat ।

kiṃ cāyaṃ vidvān brahmībhūto abhedam ekāntena na paśyati । tasyām avasthāyāṃ na karma kartavyam iti brūmaḥ । yadi tu vyutthitacitto aśanayānādiṣu kartṛtvam anubhavati tasyaiva sandhyopāsanādi kartavyaṃ syāt । viśeṣahetur vā vaktavyaḥ । yac coktam ātmopadeśīyo ayaṃ granthaḥ । tatrāśaṅkye kilottaṅkena gṛhītam amṛtam । yathā karmanāśabhayāj jantor ātmajñānāgrahas tatheti tathyaparyālocanam uktam । uttaraṅkasya yuktasūtradvāravinirgatatvād amṛtadhārāyāḥ sūtrabhrāntyātmajñānāgrahaṇam ।

iha tv ātmajñānān muktim icchatāṃ katham ātmajñānāgrahaḥ । yadi ca karma muktikāraṇaṃ syāt tatas tatparirakṣaṇe prayateran । atra yadi samuccayān mokṣāvāptis tadobhayatra pravṛttiḥ । 
atha kevalāj jñānād apavargaḥ syāt iti tvatpakṣo vartate
karmāśreyaskaratvād viṣavat parityājyaṃ śreyaskāmair iti ।
yat kiṃ cid etat ।
karmaṇaś ca yathā bandhahetutvaṃ nāsti tathā vakṣyāmaḥ ।।

karmākurvataḥ kevalād eva jñānāt siddhir ity ayam artho na kenacid anunmattena śakyate pratijñātum iti । tatra hetum āha 

na hi kaścit kṣaṇam api jātu tiṣṭhaty akarmakṛt ।
kāryate hy avaśaḥ karma sarvaḥ prakṛtijair guṇaiḥ ।।

hīti hetau । neti pratiṣedhe । yasmāt kaścid api puruṣaḥ kṣaṇamātraṃ jātu na kadācit tiṣṭhaty akarmakṛt । tasmāt karmayogapratiṣedhapratijñānupapannā । kathaṃ punar akarmakṛn nāstīty āha । kāryate hy avaśaḥ karma । avaśo asvatantraḥ pumāṃ karma kāryate balāt karmaṇi pravartyate । kena । prakṛtijair guṇaiḥ । prakṛtir mahābhūtānāṃ sūkṣmāvasthā । tato jātaiḥ kāryakāraṇaiḥ sattvādiguṇādhiṣṭhitair guṇaiḥ ।

trividhaṃ karma kāyikaṃ vācikaṃ mānasaṃ ceti । tatrāvaśyam anyatamena bhavitavyam । karma tyaktavyam ity uktimātreṇa

vācikaṃ karma kṛtam eva bhavati । maunāvasthāne api mānasaṃ 
karma duṣpariharaṃ vidyullatāvac cañcalatvāt tasya ।
aśanaśayanasaṅkramaṇādīni chāyevānugatāni ।।

yas tu coditaṃ karma karoti manasā ca viṣayān bhojanādīn abhilaṣati sa kena śabdenocyata ity āha 

karmendriyāṇi saṃyamya ya āste manasā smaran ।
indriyārthān vimūḍhātmā mithyācāraḥ sa ucyate ।।

yas tu coditam anutiṣṭhati sa yathoktakāritvān mārgastha ity āha 

yas tv indriyāṇi manasā niyamyārabhate arjuna ।
karmendriyaiḥ karmayogam asaktaḥ sa viśiṣyate ।।

phalāsaṅgarahitaḥ ।।

yata evam ataḥ 

niyataṃ kuru karma tvaṃ karma jyāyo hy akarmaṇaḥ ।
śarīrayātrāpi ca te na prasiddhyed akarmaṇaḥ ।।

niyataṃ nityaṃ sandhyopāsanādi । sāmānye āsaṅgādi viśeṣe karma kuru yasmāt karma jyāyo adhikataram akarmaṇaḥ । akaraṇāt sakāśād adṛṣṭe viṣaye mandakaraṇam api śreyaskaram । katham । śarīrayātrā śarīrasthitir api na te prasiddhyed akarmaṇo nirvyāpārasya ।

yad atra kecid aśrutaṃ viśeṣaṇaṃ svamanīṣikayā prakṣipanty ajñenādhikṛtena karma kartavyam iti tad asat । 
śarīrasthitir na siddhyatīti viduṣo aviduṣaś ca
samānaṃ hetvabhidhānam ।
vidvān api parivrājako bhojanakāle bhikṣāṭanādau pravartata eva
anyathā śarīrasthityabhāvāt ।।

yac ca manyante sāṅkhyāḥ sarvaṃ karma bandhātmakam iti tad asad ity āha 

yajñārthāt karmaṇo anyatra loko ayaṃ karmabandhanaḥ ।
tadarthaṃ karma kaunteya muktasaṅgaḥ samācara ।।

yajñaśabdenātra kālāntarasthāyī dharmo abhidhīyate yam apūrvam iti mīmāṃsakā bruvate । tasya cādhidevatā viṣṇuḥ । yajño vai viṣṇuḥ iti śruteḥ । tayor abhedena vyapadiśyate । etad uktaṃ bhavati īśvarārādhanārthatvāt karmaṇaḥ śrutismṛtivihitaḥ puruṣavyāpāraḥ karmaśabdenocyate । tato anyatra taṃ varjayitvā loko ayaṃ karmabandhanaḥ । phalārthaṃ yat kriyate tena badhyate jantuḥ । tadarthaṃ yajñārthaṃ kevaladharmasiddhyarthaṃ 
karma muktasaṅgaḥ phalāsaktirahitaḥ samācara ।
itīdam evaṃ dhārayen mokṣāyeti ।
śāstram evātra pramāṇam ।
yathāyaṃ dharmo ayam adharma iti ।।

prajāpativacanāc ca śreyaskaraṃ karma । ato anuṣṭheyam iti darśayann āha 

sahayajñāḥ prajāḥ sṛṣṭvā purovāca prajāpatiḥ ।
anena prasaviṣyadhvam eṣa vo astv iṣṭakāmadhuk ।।

saha yajñena vartanta iti sahayajñā brāhmaṇādyāḥ prajāḥ sargādau sṛṣṭvā tāḥ purovāca anena prasaviṣyadhvam । prasavo vṛddhiḥ । tāṃ prāpnuta । 
eṣa vo yuṣmākam iṣṭakāmadhug astu ।
kāmān dogdhīti kāmadhuk ।।

kathaṃ punaḥ kāmadhug ity āha 

devān bhāvayatānena te devā bhāvayantu vaḥ ।
parasparaṃ bhāvayantaḥ śreyaḥ param avāpsyatha ।।

anena devān bhāvayata vibhūtyā yojayata । te cendrādayo 
devā bhāvayantu yuṣmān vibhūtyā yojayantu vṛṣṭipradānādinā ।
evam anyonyaṃ bhāvayantaḥ śreyaḥ paraṃ svargārthinaḥ svargam
apavargārthinopavargaṃ prāpsyatha ।।

pratyupakāram akurvato aniṣṭārthaprāptim āha 

iṣṭān kāmān hi vo devā dāsyante yajñabhāvitāḥ ।
tair dattānapradāyaibhyo yo bhuṅkte stena eva saḥ ।।
iṣṭān kāmān iti । pūrvārdhena pūrvaślokānuvādaḥ ।
tair devair dattāt bhogān yo bhuṅkte tebhyo adattvā
tān uddiśya yāgam akṛtvā stena eva saḥ ।
kartavyam akurvan pratyavaitīty arthaḥ ।।

ye tu punaḥ 

yajñaśiṣṭāśinaḥ santo mucyante sarvakilbiṣaiḥ ।
bhuñjate te tv aghaṃ pāpā ye pacanty ātmakāraṇāt ।।
yajñārthaṃ niruptaṃ dravyam । tena yajñe nirvartite yad
avaśiṣṭaṃ dravyaṃ tad aśituṃ śīlaṃ yeṣāṃ te 
yajñaśiṣṭāśinaḥ
santo sarvakilbiṣair mucyate ।
ye punar ātmārthaṃ kevalaṃ pacanti
te aghaṃ pāpam eva bhuñjate ।।

jagaccakravṛttihetutvāc cāvaśyaṃ karma kartavyam ity āha 

annād bhavanti bhūtāni parjanyād annasambhavaḥ ।
yajñād bhavati parjanyo yajñaḥ karmasamudbhavaḥ ।।

annād upabhuktād roto abhūd bhūtāni jāyante । tasya ca samudbhavaḥ parjanyāt । sa ca yajñād bhavati । yajñaś ca karmasambhavaḥ । yajamānartvigvyāpāraḥ karma । tadabhivyaṅgyam apūrvaṃ dharmaśabdavācyaṃ jagadvaicitryakāraṇam ।।

tac ca 

karma brahmodbhavaṃ viddhi brahmākṣarasamudbhavam ।
tasmāt sarvagataṃ brahma nityaṃ yajñe pratiṣṭhitam ।।

karma brahmodbhavam । brahma vedaḥ । tatprakāśitam । brahma cākṣarasamudbhavam । akṣaram iti paramātmākhyā tasya mahato bhūtasya niḥśvāsitam etad yad ṛgvedo yajurvedaḥ ity śruteḥ । yata evaṃ tasmāt sarvagataṃ brahmākṣarākhyaṃ sarvagatam iti viśeṣaṇāt । itarat

punar brahma vedākhyaṃ vikāratvād asarvagataṃ tadakṣarākhyaṃ brahma nityaṃ sarvadā yajñe pratiṣṭhitam । 
yajñenopāyabhūtena
prakhyātam iti tatpratiṣṭham ucyate ।
yathopāyakriyāyāṃ pratiṣṭhāśabdaḥ vedāḥ sāṅgāḥ
satyam āyatanaṃ pratiṣṭhā iti ।।

uktena prakāreṇa karmamūlaṃ jagaccakram । atas tad akurvato jīvanaṃ vyartham ity āha 

evaṃ pravartitaṃ cakraṃ nānuvartayatīha yaḥ ।
aghāyur indriyārāmo moghaṃ pārtha sa jīvati ।।
evam ity uktaparāmarśaḥ । pravartitaṃ mayājātinā cakram iva
jagaccakram । karmabhyo bhūtāni bhūtebhyaḥ karmeti । tatra yaḥ karma na karoti tena jagaccakraṃ nānuvartitaṃ bhavati । nimittākaraṇān naimittikam eva nāśitaṃ bhavatīty arthaḥ । so ayam aghāyuḥ pāpāyur indriyair ārāma ākrīḍā viṣayeṣu yasyāsau indriyārāmāḥ । moghaṃ vṛthaiva he pārtha sa jīvati ।।

kiṃ kācid avasthāsti yasyāṃ karmatyāga iṣṭa iti । asti lokavyavahāraḥ । atas tasya brahmabhūtasya tatprāgavasthāyām ity āha 

yas tv ātmaratir eva syād ātmatṛptaś ca mānavaḥ ।
ātmany eva ca santuṣṭas tasya kāryaṃ na vidyate ।।

yas tv ātmaratir eva syāt । tuśabdo avadhāraṇārthaḥ । asyām evāvasthāyām adhikārahetvabhāvāt karmatyāgo bhavati । ātmany eva

ratir yasya na viṣayeṣv asāv ātmaratiḥ । evaśabdo avadhāraṇārthaḥ । manāg api viṣayeṣu ratir nāsti । ātmanaiva ca tṛpto nānnarasādinā । ātmany eva ca santuṣṭo nānyārthalābhena । tad evaṃ trividhena viśeṣaṇena viśiṣṭasya 
śarīrendriyaviṣayavyavahārātītasya paraṃ
jyotīrūpasampannasya kāryaṃ na vidyate ।
kim ataḥ paraṃ sādhyaṃ syāt ।
iyaṃ hi phalāvasthā jñānakarmasamuccayānuṣṭhānasya ।।

kāryaṃ na vidyata itīdaṃ spaṣṭīkartum āha 

naiva tasya kṛtenārtho nākṛteneha kaścana ।
na cāsya sarvabhūteṣu kaścid arthavyapāśrayaḥ ।।

kṛtena yāgādināsya prayojanaṃ nāsti । nākṛteneha kaścana pratyavāyaparihāralakṣaṇo arthaḥ । na ca tasya sarvabhūteṣu bramādiṣu kaścid arthavyapāśrayaḥ prayojanam apekṣā sa eva tad bhavatīti śruteḥ । yas tu śarīrendriyadharmair anurudhyate śayanādīṃś ca karoti vyāpārān katham asāv ātmaratir ātmatṛpta eva vā syāt । iyaṃ cāvasthā karmatyāgasya bhagavatā viyatā tām etāṃ svayam evālocya karma hātavyam anuṣṭheyaṃ vā । nānyasyedānīntanasya durupadeśaḥ krotavyaḥ pramāṇīkartavyo vā vyāmuhyamānatvād ālasyāt ।

tathā cāhuḥ kecid ajñānato naṣṭāḥ kecin naṣṭāḥ pramādataḥ । kecij jñānāvalepena kecin naṣṭais tu nāśitāḥ ।। ।।

yato jīvataḥ karmatyāgānupapattiḥ 

tasmād asaktaḥ satataṃ kāryaṃ karma samācara ।
asakto hy ācaran karma param āpnoti pūruṣaḥ ।।

phaleṣv asaktaḥ kāryaṃ karma yad avaśyaṃ kartavyaṃ tat samācara । kimprayojanam । yasmād asakto hy ācaran karma paraṃ paramātmānam āpnoti pūruṣaḥ ।।

ātmajñaiś ca rājarṣibhir āsevito ayaṃ mārgo yasmāt tvayāpi nirviśaṅkenāstheyam iti darśayann āha 

karmaṇaiva hi saṃsiddhim āsthitā janakādayaḥ ।
lokasaṅgraham evāpi saṃpaśyan kartum arhasi ।।

karmaṇaiva hi saṃsiddhiṃ mokṣam āsthitāḥ prāptā janakāśvapatiprabhṛtayaḥ । hiśabdo hetvarthe । evakāro avadhāraṇārtho nipātitaḥ । karmābhāvavyavacchedaḥ kriyate na jñānaparyudāsaḥ । yady api kṛtakṛtyam ātmānaṃ manyase lokasaṅgraham eva tathāpi sampaśyan kartum arhasi । lokasaṅgraho lokaparipālanam uktena nyāyena । paramārthatas tu svārtham eva karma kartavyam । kevalasya jñānasyāpavargaṃ prati

sādhanabhūtasyāpi jñānasya kartavyasthānīyaṃ karma sahakāritvenāpekṣaṇīyam । tasmāl lokaparipālanam ānuṣaṅgikaṃ prayojanam ।

atra kecid aṅgulibhaṅgaṃ kurvanto vyācakṣate yadi janakādayaḥ prāptasamyagjñānās tato lokasaṅgrahaṇārthaṃ karmaṇaiva saṃsiddhim āsthitāḥ karmasannyāse prāpte apy asannyasyaiva pravṛttakarmatvād iti । athāprāptajñānāḥ karmaṇā sattvaśuddhidvāreṇa jñānotpattim āsādya muktāḥ iti vyākhyeyaḥ śloka iti ।

tad etad asadarthotprekṣaṇam । janakādayo hi brahmavidaḥ smaryante । mokṣadharmeṣu viṣṇudharmeṣu janakānāṃ ṣaṭsaptatir mokṣaṃ gatā smaryate । atra ca karmaṇā mokṣaṃ gatā ity ucyate । na punaḥ karmaṇā lokasaṅgrahaṃ kṛtavanta iti । śrutahānir aśrutaparikalpanā caivaṃ syāt । na ca teṣāṃ karmasu pravṛttatvād iti karmapravṛttau hetuḥ । utpannāyāṃ karmapravṛttau ūrddhvaṃ sarvo hi pravṛttakarmaiva । yadi samyagdarśane samutpanne karmākarmasannyāso janakādibhir apy avaśyaṃ karma kartavyaṃ prāptam । 
na hi khaṇḍamodakabhakṣaṇāt
prītyā kaścit karmaṇi pravartate kleśātmakatvāt ।
tasmāt karmaṇā vinā saṃsiddher asambhavāt karma kurv iti
gītārthaḥ ।।

avaśyaṃ lokasaṅgrahārtham api bhavatā karmaṇi yatitavyam । kutaḥ । śreṣṭhatvāt tad āha 

yadyad ācarati śreṣṭhas tattad evetaro janaḥ ।
sa yatpramāṇaṃ kurute lokas tad anuvartate ।।

guṇādhikaḥ śreṣṭha ucyate । tena yad anuṣṭhitaṃ tattad itaraḥ 
prākṛto jano anutiṣṭhati ।
sa yatpramāṇaṃ kurute laukikaṃ vaidikaṃ
vā karoti tad eva pramāṇīkṛtya loko anuvartate ।।

māṃ ca kiṃ na paśyasi 

na me pārthāsti kartavyaṃ triṣu lokeṣu kiñcana ।
nānavāptam avāptavyaṃ vartāmy eva ca karmaṇi ।।
na me pārthāsti kartavyaṃ triṣu lokeṣu sādhyam । yato
nānavāptam aprāptaṃ prāptavyaṃ vāsti atha ca vartāmy eva ca karmaṇi । varta eveti kecit paṭhanti ātmanepaditvād vṛtadhātoḥ । 
teṣāṃ itihāsapurāṇavad gītāyā pañcam avedatvāc
chāndasaprayogabāhulyād ārṣapāṭhavināśanam
eva prasajyate sarvatra pāṭhāntaraṃ kurvatām ।।

yadi punar aham eva karma na karomy anyo api na kuryād ity āha 

yady ahaṃ pravarteya jātu karmaṇy atandritaḥ ।
mama vartmānuvarteran manuṣyāḥ pārtha sarvaśaḥ ।।

yadi tv ahaṃ na varteya । jātu kadācit । atandrito analasaḥ । tato mama vartma madīyaṃ mārgam akaraṇalakṣaṇam anuvarteran manuṣyāḥ sarvaśaḥ ।।

tataḥ ko doṣa ity āha 

utsīdeyur ime lokāḥ na kuryāṃ karma ced aham ।
saṅkarasya ca kartā syām upahanyām imāḥ prajāḥ ।।

utsīdeyur vinaśyeyur lokā yadi ahaṃ karma na kuryām । saṅkarasya ca kartā syām arthādyabhāvāt । tataś copahanyām imāḥ prajāḥ । tasmān mayāpīśvareṇa satā lokasaṅgrahaṇārthaṃ karma kriyate । so ayam ubhayataḥ śāstrānusāreṇātmārthaṃ parārthaṃ vā karma kartavyam eva । na jñānitvābhimānena karma tyaktavyam । manuṣyasyādhikāritvāc chāstrasya bhagavato api manuṣyaśarīre vartamānasya dharmādhikārāt karmasannyāsānupapatteḥ । karmaṇi pravṛtto hi manuṣyaśarīraṃ vihāya devo vā paramātmā vā 
saṃvṛtto yadā tadā tasyādhikārābhāvaḥ ।
tad uktam yas tv ātmaratir eva syāt iti ।
ato yāvad bhedavijñānam anuvartate tāvat karmādhikāraḥ svārthaṃ
parārthaṃ veti bhāgavataṃ mataṃ mudritam ।।

tatra ca karmaṇi pravṛttasya viduṣo aviduṣaś cāyaṃ viśeṣaḥ 

saktāḥ karmaṇy avidvāṃso yathā kurvanti bhārata ।
kuryād vidvāṃs tathāsaktaś cikīrṣur lokasaṅgraham ।।

phalābhilipsayā karmaṇi saktā avidvāṃso yathā kurvanti bhārata tathā mahatotsāhena vit kuryāt sadasadarthopavargārtham ।

kiñcaitad aparam ānantarīyakaṃ prayojanam ।
cikīrṣuḥ kartum icchur
lokasaṅgraham ।।

yadi cāyaṃ karma na kuryād ajñānāṃ buddhibhedaḥ syād ity āha 

na buddhibhedaṃ janayed ajñānāṃ karmasaṅginām ।
joṣayet sarvakarmāṇi vidvān yuktaḥ samācaran ।।

na buddhibhedaṃ janayed ajñānām ity ajñagrahaṇaṃ jñāpakam 
tatra tatra pūrvatra jñasyaiva karmakartavyatā bhagavatopadiṣṭeti ।
joṣayed ity utsāhayet ।
sarvakarmāṇi svayaṃ yuktaḥ samācaran ।।

avidvān kena prakāreṇa karmaṇi sajjata ity āha 

prakṛteḥ kriyamāṇāni guṇaiḥ karmāṇi bhāgaśaḥ ।
ahaṅkāravimūḍhātmā kartāham iti manyate ।।

prakṛtes tejo'bannalakṣaṇāyāḥ kāryakāraṇarūpair guṇair acetanaiḥ । kriyamāṇāni । śarīrendriyamanaḥsu hi sarvāṇi laukikāni vaidikāni ca karmāṇi vartante nātmani । ātmanas tu sannidhimātreṇāyaskāntavad ayasaḥ pravṛttau aupādhikam eva kartṛtvaṃ na svābhāvikam । yathendhanasaṃyoge dhūmajanakatvam agnes tathā śarīrendriyasaṃyoge ātmanaḥ kartṛtvam । tasya kartṛtvaṃ svena niratiśayānandarūpeṇāvasthitasya nāstīti nirṇayaḥ । tatrāyam ajño ahaṅkāravimūḍhātmā svabhāvata

evāhaṃ karteti manyate ।
so ayam anena mithyābhimānena badhyate ।।

yaḥ punas tattvavin nāsau badhyata ity āha 

tattvavit tu mahābāho guṇakarmavibhāgayoḥ ।
guṇā guṇeṣu vartanta iti matvā na sajjate ।।

guṇavibhāgasya karmavibhāgasya ca yas tattvaṃ vetti sa tattvavit । kaḥ punar vibhāgo guṇānāṃ dehendriyāṇāṃ karmaṇām ātmana iti । karmavibhāgaś ca phaloddeśena kriyamāṇaḥ phalārthaḥ īśvarārthaḥ kriyamāṇopavargārtha iti । 
so ayaṃ guṇā dehādayo guṇeṣu svavyāpāreṣu
svabhāvataḥ pravṛttā
iti matvā na sajjate saktiṃ na karoti ।।

ye punas te 

prakṛter guṇasammūḍhāḥ sajjante guṇakarmasu ।
tān akṛtsnavido mandān kṛtsnavin na vicālayet ।।

prakṛter guṇasammūḍhā ity uktasyānuvādaḥ kañcid viśeṣaṃ vaktum । tān akṛtsnavido mandān ity akṛtsnavidaḥ kevalakarmavido yājñikān kṛtsnavij jñānakarmasamuccayakārī na vicālayen na buddhicālanaṃ sampādayet । teṣāṃ guṇakṛteṣu hi karmasu teṣāṃ

saktatvāc charīrapātenāpi na te bodhayituṃ śakyante । yat punar āgatya pṛccheyus tato bodhayitavyā iti ।।

kañcid viśeṣam upadarśayan prakaraṇārtham upasaṃharati 

mayi sarvāṇi karmāṇi sannyasyādhyātmacetasā ।
nirāśīr nirmamo bhūtvā yuddhyasva vigatajvaraḥ ।।

mayi parameśvare brahmaṇi sarvāṇi karmāṇi kṛtvā tāni sannyasya nikṣipya sarva evāyaṃ kriyākalāpo brahmaṇo adhikāraś cetanatvāt । kāryakāraṇayoś cānanyatvāt tadātmakatvaṃ pratipadya tatprāptaye kalpata ity adhyātmacetasā phalaprārthanarahitaḥ । nirgataṃ mamatvaṃ yasyāsau nirmamaḥ । nāsti me karma brahmaṇa eva tat kṛtaṃ mayi । evaṃ saṅkalpo bhūtvā yuddhyasva vigataśoka iti ।।

ye vidvāṃsaḥ svārthaṃ lokasaṅgrahārthaṃ ca karma na tyajanti teṣām ayaṃ guṇa ity āha 

ye me matam idaṃ nityam anuvartanti mānavāḥ ।
śraddhāvanto anasūyantas te vimucyanti karmabhiḥ ।।

ye punar etan nābhinandanti āṅkhyādidarśanavibhrāntacetasas teṣām adhaḥpātaṃ darśayann āha 

ye tv etad abhyasūyanto nānuvartanti me matam । sarvajñānavimūḍhāṃs tān viddhi naṣṭān acetasaḥ ।।

ye tv iti । ye punar me mataṃ nānuvartante tān sarvebhyo
jñānebhyo vimūḍhān viddhi naṣṭān svargāpavargaprāptyabhāvān nirayagāmitvāt ।।

kasmāt punar vidvāṃso api santaḥ kecid bhagavato mataṃ nānuvartanta ity āśaṅkyāha 

sadṛśaṃ ceṣṭate svasyāḥ prakṛter jñānavān api । prakṛtiṃ yānti bhūtāni nigrahaḥ kiṃ kariṣyati ।।

sadṛśam iti । jñānavān api prakṛter anurūpaṃ ceṣṭate । prakṛtir janmāntarakṛtaṃ karma vāsanārūpeṇa cetasy avasthitaṃ vāsasīva rāgaḥ । 
tatra prakṛtim eva yānti bhūtāni ।
nigrahaḥ śāstrakṛto niyamo anuśāsanam idaṃ kartavyam idaṃ neti ।
sa teṣāṃ kiṃ kariṣyati ।
ato yuktaṃ kecin me mataṃ nānuvartanta iti ।।

ye punar madīyaṃ matam anuvartante janmāntarakṛtapuṇyopacayavaśāt teṣām ayam upadeśaḥ 

indriyasyendriyasyārthe rāgadveṣau vyavasthitau । tayor na vaśam āgacchetau hy asya paripanthinau ।।
indriyasyeti । indriyasyārthe cakṣuṣaḥ śrotasyārthe sve sve
viṣaye anukūle rāgaḥ pratikūle dveṣaḥ । tayor na vaśam āgacchet ।

yatas tau hi mumukṣoḥ paripanthināv antarāyau vidhnakāriṇau । tasmāt taskarāv iva tau dūrataḥ parityajet ।।

na ca paradharme rāgāt pravartitavyam । svadharme ca yuddhādau prāṇāpahāritayā dveṣān nivartitavyam ity āha śreyaś cartum ity arjunoktam anusmaran 

śreyān svadharmo adhiguṇaḥ paradharmāt svanuṣṭhitāt । svadharme nidhanaṃ śreyaḥ paradharmodayād api ।।

śreyān iti । svadharmo adhiguṇa iti kartavyatāhīno api yathākathañcid anuṣṭhito api śreyān praśastataraḥ । kutaḥ । paradharmāt svanuṣṭhāt । ampūrṇetikartavyatākāt । kasmād etad evam । yataḥ svadharme vartamānasya saṅgrāmādau nidhanaṃ maraṇaṃ śreyaḥ paradharmakṛtād udayāj jīvanād ity arthaḥ । apir abhyupagame । yady api svadharme nidhanam anabhyudayaḥ varam paradharmakṛto abhyudayo na varam । na punar etad evam । kiṃ tu svadharmād abhyudayaḥ paradharmāśrayād anabhyudaya iti । svadharmaḥ kartavyaḥ । arthavādo ayam ।।

jānann api tatparityāge na kenāyaṃ preritaḥ । pāpam evānudhāvatīty arjuna uvāca 

atha kena prayukto ayaṃ pāpaṃ carati pūruṣaḥ । anicchann api vārṣṇeya balād iva niyojitaḥ ।।

atha keneti । kenāyaṃ prayuktaḥ preritaḥ pāpam ācarati । anicchann api balād ivākramya gale pādukayā prayojitaḥ prerita iti ।।

bhagavān uvāca 

kāma eṣa krodha eṣa rajoguṇasamudbhavaḥ । mahāśano mahāpāpmā viddhy enam iha vairiṇam ।।

kāma eṣeti । kāmaḥ sūkṣmaḥ । sa eva kenacit pratihataḥ krodhaḥ saṃpadyate । prārthitavastvapratipadyato hi krodho jāyate । rajoguṇaḥ samudbhava utpattisthānaṃ yasya so ayaṃ rajoguṇasamudbhavaḥ । mahadaśanaṃ yasyāsau mahāśanas trailokyam api grasate । mahāṃś cāsau pāpmā samastavyasanahetur ity arthaḥ । viddhi jānīhi । iha mokṣamārge vairiṇam etam ।।

arjuna uvāca 

bhavaty eṣa kathaṃ kṛṣṇa kathaṃ caiva vivardhate । kim ātmakaḥ kim ācāras tan mamācakṣva pṛcchataḥ ।।
bhavatīti ।।
śrībhagavān uvāca eṣa sūkṣmaḥ paraḥ śatrur dehinām indriyaiḥ saha । sukhatantra ivāsīno mohayan pārtha tiṣṭhati ।।

eṣa sūkṣmaḥ paraḥ śatrur dehinām indriyaiḥ saheti sukhatantra ivāsīno mohayan pārtha tiṣṭhati ।।

sa eva kaluṣaḥ kṣudraś chidraprekṣī dhanañjaya ।
rajaḥpravṛtto mohātmā mānuṣāṇām upadravaḥ ।।

kāmakrodhamayo ghoraḥ stambhaharṣasamudbhavaḥ ।
ahaṅkārābhimānātmā dustaraḥ pāpakarmabhiḥ ।।

harṣam asya nivarttyaiṣa śokam asya dadāti ca ।
bhayaṃ cāsya karoty eṣa mohayaṃs tu muhurmuhuḥ ।।

iti sāṅkhyamatānusāriṇaḥ kecanādhīyate । te ca pañca ślokā na vyākhyātāḥ ।।

kathaṃ vairitvam iti dṛṣṭāntena darśayati 

dhūmenāvriyate vahnir yathādarśo malena ca । yatholbenāvṛto garbhas tathā tenedam āvṛtam ।।

dhūmeneti । yatholbena garbhaveṣṭanenāvṛto garbhas tathā tenedam āvṛtaṃ dṛṣṭam ।।

śabdena kim ucyata iti vivṛṇoti 

āvṛtaṃ jñānam etena jñānino nityavairiṇā । kāmarūpeṇa kaunteya duṣpūreṇānalena vā ।।

āvṛtam iti । etena jñānam āvṛtam । kasya kena । jñānino nityavairiṇā kāmarūpeṇa nānārūpeṇa । jñānino hy asau nityavairī । katham । kāmṃ dūrataḥ kṛtvāpavargam adhigantum icchati jñānī । kāmaś ca tadīyaṃ jñānaṃ tiraskṛtya saṃsāre kṣeptuṃ yatate ।

punar ajño yatnaṃ kṛtvā kāmam evānuvartate । na tasya virodhas tena । jñānam ity upapannaṃ viśeṣaṇaṃ nityavairiṇeti । duṣpūreṇa 
duḥkhena pūryate duṣpūraḥ ।
na vidyate alaṃ paryāptir asyety analaḥ ।।

kim adhiṣṭhāno asau jñānam āvṛṇotīty āha 

indriyāṇi mano buddhir asyādhiṣṭhānam ucyate । etair vimohayaty eṣa jñānam āvṛtya dehinam ।।

indriyāṇīti । indriyāṇi mano buddhir asyādhiṣṭhānam āśrayaḥ । tair indriyādibhir jñānam āvṛtya dehinaṃ mohayati mohayitvā kāryeṣu vartayati ।।

yata evam 

tasmāt tvam indriyāṇy ādau niyamya bharatarṣabha । pāpmānaṃ prajahīhy enaṃ jñānavijñānanāśanam ।।
tasmād iti । indriyaṃ mano buddhiṃ ca niyamyādau prathamam eva
pāpmānam enaṃ śatruṃ jahi vināśaya । jñānavijñānanāśanam । jñānam ātmayāthātmyaparijñānam । vijñānam viśiṣṭaṃ tajjñānam । tadubhayanāśanam । tad api pṛthakkartavyatayā vidhīyate śrutau 
vijñāya prajñāṃ kurvīta iti ।
anyathā jñānavijñānaśabdayor
arthe bhedo na syāt ।।

kasya sannidhau kāmas tiṣṭhatīti sākṣād darśayitum āha sthūlaṃ śarīram apekṣya 

indriyāṇi parāṇy āhur indriyebhyaḥ paraṃ manaḥ । manasas tu parā buddhir yo buddheḥ paratas tu saḥ ।।

indriyāṇīti । indriyāṇi parāṇy āhur viṣayagrāhakatvenotkṛṣṭatvāc ca parastvam । indriyebhyaḥ paraṃ manaḥ saukṣmyāt prādhānyāc ca । manasas tu parā buddhiḥ । sa eva hetuḥ । atha buddhimanasoḥ ko bhedaḥ । saṅkalpavikalpavṛttihetur manaḥ । buddhir adhyavasāyātmikā । 
yathā sthāṇur vā puruṣo veti saṃśaye sthāṇur
evāyam ity adhyavasāyaḥ ।
yo buddheḥ parataḥ sa kāmaḥ parāmṛśyate tasya prakṛtatvāt ।
na punar ātmā sa iti nirdiśyate pūrvatrāsaṅkīrtanāt ।।

idānīm upasaṃharati 

evaṃ buddheḥ paraṃ buddhvā saṃstabhyātmānam ātmanā । jahi śatruṃ mahābāho kāmarūpaṃ durāsadam ।।
evam iti । evam uktena prakāreṇa buddheḥ paraṃ kāmaṃ buddhvā
jahi śatruṃ mahābāho । kāmarūpaṃ duḥkhenāsadanīyam । kiṃ kṛtvā । 
saṃstabhyātmānam ātmani saṃstabhya niruddhya cātmānaṃ kṣetrajñam
ātmani paramātmani saṃyojyaikīkṛtya brahmarūpeṇāvasthāpya
kāmaṃ jahīti tātparyārthaḥ ।।

iti śrībhagavadbhāskarakṛte gītābhāṣye tṛtīyo adhyāyaḥ ।।

atha caturtho adhyāyaḥ śrībhagavān uvāca 

imaṃ vivasvate yogaṃ proktavān aham avyayam । vivasvān manave prāha manur ikṣvākave abravīt ।।
imam iti । vivasvān ādityaḥ tasmai proktavān aham avyayam ।
nityatvaṃ nityavedavihitatvāt । sa ca vivasvān svaputrāya manave daṇḍadharāya prāha manur ādirājāyekṣvākave abravīt ।।

evaṃ paramparākhyātam imaṃ rājarṣayo viduḥ । sa kāleneha mahatā yogo naṣṭaḥ parantapa ।।
evam iti । evaṃ paramparākhyātam ācāryaparamparayā kathitam imaṃrājarṣayo viduḥ । rājānaś ca te darśanaśaktiyuktāś ceti rājarṣayaḥ ।
sa yogaḥ kālena mahateha loke kathañcid viṣayāsaktacetasaṃ rājānām āsādya naṣṭaḥ । parān śatrūṃs tāpayatīti he parantapa ।।

sa evāyaṃ mayā te adya yogaḥ proktaḥ purātanaḥ । bhakto asi me sakhā ceti rahasyaṃ hy etad uttaram ।।

sa eveti । sa eva sanātano yogo mayā proktaḥ । kasmāt । bhakto asi me sakhā ceti । rahasyaṃ hy etan mayoktam aprakāśitam । yan mayi bhaktatvasakhitvābhyāṃ naitad avajñātum arhasi । idānīṃ

yuddhaāya protsāhanārthaṃ prāptāvasaraṃ proktam ity abhiprāyaḥ ।।

pūrvaparavirodhaṃ paśyann arjuna uvāca 

aparaṃ bhavato janma paraṃ janma vivasvataḥ । katham etad vijānīyāṃ tvam ādau proktavān iti ।।

aparam iti । bhavato janmāparam idānīntanam । param ādityasya sargādau । katham etad vijānīyāṃ jñātuṃ śaknuyām । tvam ādau proktavān iti । yathāvirodhas tathā māṃ pratipādayeḥ ।।

amarajīvavyatirikteśvarapratipādanadvāreṇottaraṃ dīyate 

bahūni me vyatītāni janmāni tava cārjuna । tāny ahaṃ veda sarvāṇi na tvaṃ vettha parantapa ।।

bahūni । bahūni me vyatītāni prādurbhāvarūpāṇi । mayi sarvāṇi iti vacanam idānīṃ siddhaṃ bhavati । anyathā vyatirikteśvarābhāve kva karmāṇi sannyaseran । tāny ahaṃ 
veda ।
tvaṃ tāni na vettha jānāsy anīśvaratvāt ।।

kathaṃ punar īśvaro ajaḥ san sambhavatīti codyam āśaṅkya nirākaroti 

ajo api sann avyayātmā bhūtānām īśvaro api san । prakṛtiṃ svām adhiṣṭhāya sambhavāmy ātmamāyayā ।।

aja iti । na jāyate avinaśvara ātmā svarūpaṃ yasyāsāv avyayātmā । prakṛtiṃ svām avaṣṭabhya । prakṛtis tejo'bannalakṣaṇā parameśvarād utpannā । tām avaṣṭabhya āśritya sambhavāmy ātmamāyayā । māyāśabdaḥ prajñāvacanaḥ । svecchayety arthaḥ । nāhaṃ dharmaprayojyaḥ saṃsārī । vaśyaprakṛtitvād dehopādānāny asau svecchayā grahīṣyatīti avirodhaḥ ।।

kadā punar ātmānaṃ sṛjasīty āha 

yadā yadā hi dharmasya glānir bhavati bhārata । abhyutthānam adharmasya tadātmānaṃ sṛjāmy aham ।।
yadeti । yadā hi dharmasya varṇāśramādilakṣaṇasya glānir hāniḥ ।
abhyutthānaṃ vṛddhir adharmasya । tadātmānaṃ sṛjāmy aham ।।

tat 

paritrāṇāya sādhūnāṃ vināśāya ca duṣkṛtām । dharmasaṃsthāpanārthāya sambhavāmi yuge yuge ।।

paritrāṇāyeti । paritrāṇāya sādhūnāṃ svakarmaniratānām । vināśāya ca duṣkṛtām । evaṃ dharmasaṃsthāpanaya yuge yuge sambhavāmi ।।

janma karma ca me divyam evaṃ yo vetti tattvataḥ । tyaktvā dehaṃ punar janma naiti mām eti so arjuna ।।

janmeti । janma mathurādiṣu । karma ca sādhuparitrāṇalakṣaṇam

uktaprakāraṃ divyam amānuṣaṃ yo vetti sa tyaktvā dehaṃ punar janma na gacchati । mām eva prāpnotīti । nanu caivaṃ śabdaśravaṇamātreṇa sarvaloko mucyate । upaniṣaduktaparamātmajñānopāsanābhyāṃ yāvajjīvaṃ kṛtābhyāṃ svāśramavihitakarmayajñābhyāṃ muktir iti sthitam । ihāpi ca yajñānuṣṭhānād apavarga iti sthāpitaṃ pratyuddhriyeta । atrocyate nāyaṃ virodho asti । īśvaraḥ svatantraḥ samastasaṃsāraparipālanāya । prākṛtas tu tatparas tadupāsanayā mucyata ity anavadyam ।।

uttaraśloke cāyam arthaḥ spaṣṭhīkriyate 

vītarāgabhayakrodhā manmayā mām upāśritāḥ । bahavo jñānatapasā pūtā madbhāvam āgatāḥ ।।

vīteti । vītāḥ rāgaś ca bhayaṃ ca krodhaś ca te vigatā yebhyas te vītarāgabhayakrodhāḥ । kvacid vastuni snehamātraṃ rāgaḥ । manmayā mām ātmatvenābhiprapannā nityam evaṃ svarūpaṃ cetasā mām eva copāśritāḥ । nānyo asmākaṃ śaraṇam astīty ubhayaviśeṣaṇopādānam । yathā kaścit srtīmayo bhavati na śaraṇaṃ prapannaḥ । kiṃ tu rājānaṃ yogakṣemāv ahaṃ jñānatapasā jñānaṃ ca tapaś ca jñānatapaḥ । tayor dvandvaikavadbhāvaḥ । sarvo dvandvo ekavad bhavati iti

smaraṇāt । jñānena tapasā ca pūtā ity arthaḥ । jñānam eva tapo jñānatapaḥ iti kecit । tad ayuktam । jñānasya tapaḥśaraṇānarthakyāt । jñānena pūtā iti siddhatvāt । na hi jñānena sadṛśam iti coktatvāt ।।

nanu jñānatapobhyāṃ bhaktā eva madbhāvaṃ pratipadyante netare । kin nu khalu kāraṇam । ata āha 

ye yathā māṃ prapadyante tāṃs tathaiva bhajāmy aham । mama vartmānuvartante manuṣyāḥ pārtha sarvaśaḥ ।।

ya iti । ye phalārthino māṃ yathā prapadyante tāṃs tathaiva bhajāmi phalapradānena । ye apy apavargārthino māṃ bhajante tāṃś cāpavargapradānenānugṛhṇāmi । tathā ca vājināṃ śrutiḥ taṃ yathāyathopāsate iti । ato mama vartma phalārthino mokṣārthinaś cobhayārthino manuṣyāḥ sarvaśaḥ sarva eva tṛtīyasya rāśer abhāvāt anuvartante ।।

te ca phalārthino mokṣaṃ na kāṅkṣantīty āha 

kāṅkṣantaḥ karmaṇāṃ siddhiṃ yajanta iha devatāḥ । kṣipraṃ hi mānuṣe loke siddhir bhavati karmajā ।।

kāṅkṣanti iti । karmasambandhinīṃ siddhiṃ kāṅkṣanto yajante

devatā yāgena pūjayanti । yataḥ kṣipraṃ hi mānuṣe loke iti
anuvādaḥ । karmavipariṇāmasyāniyatakālatvāt mānuṣe loka iti niyamārtham ।

karmajā siddhir manuṣyaloka eva manuṣyādhikāratvāc chāstrasya । jñānajā tu siddhir brahmalokādāv api bhavati । śrutir api tad yo yo devānāṃ pratyabuddhyata sa eva tad abhavat tatharṣīṇāṃ tathā manuṣyāṇām iti । tatraiva jñānaprakarṣam āsādya mucyate । tathā ca purāṇasmṛtiḥ 

brahmaṇā saha te sarve samprāpte pratisañcare । parasyānte kṛtātmānaḥ praviśanti paraṃ padam ।। iti ।

iha ca vakṣyati daivī siddhir vimokṣāya iti ।
tasmān manuṣyeṇa tvayārjunenāvaśyaṃ karma kartavyam iti
tātparyārthaḥ ।।

manuṣyāḥ sarve mama vartmānuvartanta ity uktam । ke punas te । kena vā te sṛṣṭā ity āha 

cāturvarṇyaṃ mayā sṛṣṭaṃ guṇakarmavibhāgaśaḥ । tasya kartāram api māṃ viddhy akartāram avyayam ।।
cāturvarṇyam iti । catvāra eva varṇāś cāturvarṇyam ।
tan mayā

sṛṣṭam । katham । guṇakarmavibhāgaśaḥ । guṇavibhāgena karmavibhāgena ca । tatra brāhmaṇasya ṛjutānṛśaṃsatvaṃ prasannacittatetyādayo guṇāḥ sattvapradhānatvāt । kṣatriyasya śauryatejodhṛtyādayo alpasattvānuvimarśatvāt । vaiśyasya rajaḥpradhānyād upaṣṭambhaś calacittatā ca guṇāḥ । śūdrasya tamaḥprādhānyād dāsatā guṇaḥ । atha karma adhyāpanādi brāhmaṇasya raṇādi rājanyasya kṛṣyādi vaiśyasya śuśrūṣā śūdrasyeti । tasmād ye yathāyogaṃ karmasv adhikṛtā tathā te mama vartmānuvartante । tasya kartāram avyayaṃ māṃ viddhi ।

nanu vipratiṣiddham abhidhīyate । nāyaṃ virodhaḥ । saṅkalpamātreṇa jagatsṛṣṭisthitibhaṅgakartṛtvāt kartāraṃ strīpuṃyogenedānīṃ evānutpādanād akartāraṃ viddhi । cāturvarṇyagrahaṇaṃ jagatpradarśanārtham ।

yad vā svātantryeṇa pṛthivyādinirmāṇasadbhāvāt kartṛtvam ।
prāṇikarmasāpekṣatvena sāpekṣatvād akartṛtvam ।।

na ca jagatsargādīni karmāṇi māṃ limpanti tad āha 

na māṃ karmāṇi limpanti na me karmaphale spṛhā । mām evaṃ yo abhijānāti karmabhir na sa badhyate ।।

na mām iti । na māṃ karmāṇi limpanti । kutaḥ । na me karmaphale spṛhā । na hi sṛṣṭyādikarmaṇā prāptavyaṃ sādhyaṃ mamāsti āptakāmatvāt । mām evaṃ yo abhijānāti karmabhir na sa badhyate ।

nanu cāptakāmatvād īśvaraṃ na limpanti karmāṇi । anyaṃ punar anavāptakāmaṃ sukṛtāni kasmāt tāni limpanti । atrocyate । ayam atrābhiprāyaḥ vītatṛṣṇatvam alepakāraṇam । anyo api yaḥ svavyāpāre vītatṛṣṇaḥ parameśvarārpitakarmaṇi pravartate so api karmabhir na badhyata iti yuktataram uktam ।।

etam eva phalavaitṛṣṇyalakṣaṇaṃ hetum upajīvayann āha 

evaṃ jñātvā kṛtaṃ karma pūrvair api mumukṣubhiḥ । kuru karmaiva tasmāt tvaṃ pūrvaiḥ pūrvataraiḥ kṛtam ।।
evam iti । evaṃ jñātvā kṛtaṃ karma pūrvair api cirantanair
mumukṣubhiḥ । kuru karmaiva tasmāt tvaṃ pūrvaiḥ kṛtam । nedānīntanair anuṣṭhitam ।।

tac ca karma durvijñeyasvarūpaṃ katham ity āha 

kiṃ karma kim akarmeti kavayo apy atra mohitāḥ । tat te karma pravakṣyāmi yaj jñātvā mokṣyase aśubhāt ।।

kim iti । kiṃ karma kim akarmeti kavayo api
pratyakṣādiṣaṭpramāṇakuśalā apy atra karmapravibhāge mohitāḥ । pravibhāgaṃ jñātum aśaktās te । tat karma te prakarṣeṇa vakṣyāmi । 
yaj jñātvā kṛtvā ca karmaprakaraṇāt kuru karmaiva iti
cānantaraṃ karmānuṣṭhānasya vihitatvān mokṣyase vimokṣase aśubhāt
saṃsāraparivartāt ।।

syān mataṃ karmākarma ca prasiddham । kim atra boddhuṃ ity āśaṅkyāha 

karmaṇo hy api boddhavyaṃ boddhavyaṃ ca vikarmaṇaḥ । akarmaṇo api boddhavyaṃ gahanā karmaṇo gatiḥ ।।

karmeti । satyaṃ śrutismṛtivihitaṃ karma prasiddhaṃ tathāpi tasya svarūpaṃ boddhavyam asty apavargādhikṛtena puruṣeṇa । boddhavyaṃ ca vikarmaṇaḥ । vikarma yac chāstrabāhyaṃ pāṣaṇḍibhir ācaryamāṇaṃ dhātuvādaśilpakarmādi ca । akarmaṇaś ca pratiṣiddhalaśunabhakṣaṇādeḥ । kāmyasya cāpavargārthinaḥ । tad apy akartavyam eva । evaṃ ca trividhasyāpi gahanā gambhīrā durvijñeyā gatiḥ ।।

pravibhajyedānīṃ nirṇayaṃ karoti 

karmaṇy akarma yaḥ paśyed akarmaṇi ca karma yaḥ । sa buddhimān manuṣyeṣu sa yuktaḥ kṛtsnakarmakṛt ।।

karmaṇīti । nitye karmaṇi smārte śraute ca । karma

kriyata iti karmaphalam ucyate । phalābhāvaṃ yaḥ paśyed īśvaroddeśena kriyamāṇatvāt । tadvyatirikto abhyudayaḥ sarva ete puṇyalokā bhavanti ity evamādiprāpto vāryate । akarmaṇi kāmye pratiṣiddhe ca karmaphalabhāvaṃ kāmye svargapaśvādi yathāśrutaṃ pratiṣiddhe ca narakapātādir vigarhaṇāṃ ca । ubhayatra viṣayasaptamī । na punar adhikaraṇasaptamī । yathā śarāve badarāṇīti । tad etat paśyet vicārayet । jñātvā caitad ubhayaṃ parihared iti । sa buddhimān adhyātmaśāstravihitabuddhitvāt । sa ca yukto yogī kṛtsnakarmakṛt । kṛtsna ātmā । tadarthaṃ karma karotīti kṛtsnakarmakṛt ।

na cāpavargo nāma karmaṇaḥ phalaṃ jñānakarmabhyāṃ pūrvakarmavidhinivṛttidvāreṇa tasyābhivyajyamānatvāt । yathā pradīpenāndhakāranivṛttidvāreṇa ghaṭādir abhivyajyate । mokṣo hi nitya eva na ghaṭa iva kumbhakāreṇa kriyate । ato yuktaṃ karmaṇy akarma yaḥ paśyed iti । anye punar anyathā vyācakṣate । kāmye karmaṇy akarma yaḥ paśyet phalābhāvam । akarmaṇi nitye karmāpavargānuguṇaṃ phalaṃ paśyed iti ।

tad idam asadvyākhyānam । kuru karma iti karmaśāstreṇa nityaṃ karma mokṣārthinaḥ kartavyam upadiśyate na kāmyam । na cākāmyeṣv agnihotrādiṣu śrūyamāṇaphalābhāve kartavyatāsti vidhyantarābhāvāt । na ca phalāntaraṃ kalpayituṃ śakyaṃ svamanīṣikayā । tathā coktam

aśakyaṃ hi tatpuruṣeṇa jñātum ṛte vacanād iti । na cākarmaśabdena nityaṃ karmocyate । kiṃ karma kim akarmeti prakramavirodhāt ।

apare tu karmadveṣiṇaḥ svamatiparikalpitaślokabāhyam artham asminn āropitum īhamānāḥ śrotriyaśrutiniṣṭhabuddhivyāmohanaṃ kurvanto bahu bhāṣante । prakṛtasambandhaṃ ca karmaṇi vyāpāre karmābhāvaṃ yaḥ paśyet । na hi paramārthataḥ kriyā nāmāsti । yathā kila nauyāyināṃ tīragatavṛkṣeṣu gamanabuddhir bhrāntis tathā sarvakriyābuddhir iti । yathā kṣaṇikavādino bauddhā devadattādigantṛvyatirekeṇa gamanakriyāṃ necchanti । tathāpy atra brūmahe kriyā nāstīti na pratijñātuṃ śakyate । aṅguliś calati । devadatto gacchati । brahmadattaḥ pacati । parṇaṃ calatīti sarvaprāṇipratyakṣatvāt ।

pratyakṣadravyasamavetā hi kriyā pratyakṣā । apratyakṣadravyasamavetā tv anumeyā । yathā parṇādicalanena kāryeṇa vāyor gamanam anumīyate । na cātra kāraṇadoṣo bādhakapratyayo vā vidyate । nauyāne tu tatra kāraṇadoṣas tīragatanagagamanabhrāntitvena ca । mṛgatṛṣṇikāyāṃ salilaṃ nāstīti gaṅgāmbho nāstīti na śakyate vaktum ।
bauddhasyāpy etad evottaram । ataḥ karmaṇo abhāvapratijñā tāvad
asambaddhā । atha karmaṇy ātmani karmābhāvaṃ paśyed iti vyākhyāyate tad apy asat । na hi karmaśabdenātmābhidhīyate । tadānīṃ karmaṇīty api na vaktavyam । saptamyantaṃ karmaśabdam anuccāryātmany akarma paśyed iti vaktavyam । vyāmohāyātmany akarma karmābhāvaṃ paśyed ity ukteḥ tatra karma nāstīti gamyate । kiṃ ca na jāyate mriyate vā ity ātmani ṣaḍ api bhāvavikārāḥ pūrvam eva nirākṛtāḥ । ahaṅkāravimūḍhātmā iti coktam । ataḥ punaruktam iha syāt aprastutaṃ ca । karmaprakaraṇaṃ caitad vartate ।

kiṃ ca yady akarmaṇi ca karma ya iti svamanīṣikayā vyākhyātam । śarīrendriyavyāpāropagame ahaṃ sukham āsiṣya iti

kila kaścin manyate । tadoparame karmaṇi karmavyāpāraṃ paśyed iti tad apy a[pa]vyākhyānaṃ pūrvaṃ nirākṛtatvāt । karmendriyāṇi saṃyamya iti yaś coparamātmasukhaṃ manyate nāsau punas tatra karmakartavyatāṃ pratipadyate nimittābhāvāt । athānyaḥ paśyet sa tarhi draṣṭā karma karotīti । nanu pūrvam eva bhagavatā niyukto niyataṃ kuru karma tvam iti । idānīṃ punaruktam । na ca gahanatvād asyārthasya punaḥ punar vaktavyatā । ātmani karmaṇas tūparamaś ca na kartavya iti 
pūrvoktasyāpi bhagavadvacanasya viviktārthatvād anavasthāprasaṅgāc
ca ।
tasmāt pūrvokta eva ślokārthaḥ ।।

pūrvaślokārtham uttareṇa spaṣṭhīkartum āha 

yasya sarve samārambhāḥ kāmasaṅkalpavarjitāḥ । jñānāgnidagdhakarmāṇaṃ tam āhuḥ paṇḍitaṃ budhāḥ ।।

yasyeti । samārabhyanta iti samārambhā vyāpārāḥ । kāmyata iti kāmaḥ phalam । tatsaṅkalparahitā brahmajñānāgnidagdhakarmāṇas tam āhur brahmavidaḥ paṇḍitam । ye punar anātmavidaḥ karma kurvanti na te paṇḍitā iti । yathābhūtārthakathanam etat ।

stutyartho ayaṃ śloka iti kecit । tad ayuktam । vidhiśeṣatvena hi stutiḥ pravartate । yathā pūrṇāhutividheḥ stutyarthaḥ pūrṇāhutyā

sarvān kāmān avāpnoti iti । stutiś cāsmatpakṣe yujyate । pūrvatra phalābhisandhirahitasya karmaṇo vidhānatvāt । tvatpakṣe kiṃ stūyate । karmaṇi hi karmābhāvadarśanaṃ mithyā । jñānaṃ stūyate । na hi sarvalokapratyakṣā kriyā pratyākhyātuṃ śakyety uktam ।।

yaś caivaṃ phalasaṅkalparahitaḥ paramārthadarśī sa karmaṇi pravṛtto api naiva kartety ucyata ity āha 

tyaktvā karmaphalāsaṅgaṃ nityatṛpto nirāśrayaḥ । karmaṇy abhipravṛtto api naiva kiñcit karoti saḥ ।।

tyaktveti । anityebhyaḥ phalebhyo vyāvṛttacetā nityena paramātmanā tṛpto nityatṛpto nirāśrayaḥ phalasādhanabhūta āśrayo yasya na vidyate sa kurvann api na karoti phalānuṣaṅgābhāvāt । karmaṇy evādhikāras te iti yady api dharmādhikāraḥ phalānadhikāraś coktas tathāpy atra na punar uktatā । asya prakaraṇasya viśeṣārthatvāt । karmākarmapravibhāgadvāreṇākarma kāmyaṃ pratiṣiddhaṃ ca na kartavyam । nityaṃ ca karma brahmārādhanārthaṃ kartavyam । kurvaṃś cāpnoti kilbiṣam iti brahmārpaṇanyāyenādvaitāvasthitacetasā kartavyam iti ।।

kiṃ ca 

nirāśīr yatacittātmā tyaktasarvaparigrahaḥ । śārīraṃ kevalaṃ karma kurvann āpnoti kilbiṣam ।।
nirāśīr iti । nirgatā phalāśīr yasya sa nirāśīḥ ।cittaṃ cātmā ca cittātmānau । tau saṃyatau yasya sa yatacittātmā ।
ātmaśabdena sendriyaṃ śarīraṃ gṛhyate । naiṣu putrādiṣu vā mamaite aham eteṣām iti parigrahabuddhir yasya nāsty asau tyaktasarvaparigrahaḥ । kim idaṃ śārīraṃ nāma । śārīranirvartyam āho śarīrasthityartham iti । na tāvat sthityartham । dhriyamāṇaśarīrasyārthaprāptatvād upadeśo anarthakaḥ śarīrayātrāpi ca ity uktatvāc ca । tasmāc charīraṃ śarīrendriyanirvartyaṃ śāstracoditaṃ karma । nanu pratiṣiddham api śarīranirvartyaṃ syāt । naiṣa doṣaḥ । vaidikakarmaprakaraṇāt । kevalam iti ca phalarahitam । nanu śāstrīyaṃ karma kurvataḥ kilbiṣaṃ nāpnotīty aprāptapratiṣedhaprasaṅgaḥ । atrābhidhīyate vākyatātparyāparijñānam atrāparādhyati । kurvann eva na prāpnoti akurvaṃs tu vihitākaraṇād āpnoti kilbiṣaṃ pāpam । atha vā kilbiṣaṃ saṃsāraṃ pratipadyata iti yojanāntaram ।

apare tu śarīrasthityarthaṃ bhikṣāṭanāśanapānādi kurvanti iti yojayanti । tad api kevalam abhimānarahitam iti । tad apavyākhyānam । na hi bhikṣāṭanaṃ karomīty abhimānarahitasya buddhipūrvam antareṇa tatra pravṛtter eva kalpate । kṣutpipāsābhyāṃ pīḍyamānas tatpratīkārāya bhojanādau kartṛtvam anubhavan vaidike karmaṇi kathaṃ kartṛtvaṃ na pratipadyeta । tad idaṃ rājaputraceṣṭitam । yadi vaidike karmaṇi brahmajñānavirodhāt kartṛtvaṃ nivṛttaṃ tathā laukike apīty aviśeṣaḥ । atha vobhayatrāpi kartṛtvaṃ na labhyam ardhajaratīyam । tasmād avyutpannavipralabdhabuddhiṣu vyākhyānam idaṃ śobhate । nāsmāsu ye pramāṇavṛttam anurundhāmahe ।।

yathaiva phalasaṅkalpo na kartavyas tathānye api cittadharmā upadiśyante 

yadṛcchālābhasantuṣṭo dvandvātīto vimatsaraḥ । samaḥ siddhāv asiddhau ca kṛtvāpi na nibandhyate ।।

yadṛccheti । yadṛcchālābhena prārthitopanatalābhena santuṣṭo rāgadveṣasukhaduḥkhādidvandvātīto vigataṃ mātsaryaṃ pareṣu vairabandho yasyāsau vimatsaro abhīṣṭavastusiddhāv asiddhau ca samaḥ । karma kṛtvāpi na nibadhyate । bandhahetūnāṃ cittadoṣāṇām abhāvāt ।।

prakaraṇopasaṃhārārthaḥ ślokaḥ 

gatasaṅgasya muktasya jñānāvasthitacetasaḥ । yajñāyācarataḥ karma samagraṃ pravilīyate ।।

gatasaṅgasya muktasya jñānāveti । gatasaṅgasya muktasya rāgādibhir doṣair ātmajñānāvasthitacetaso yajñāya paramātmārādhanāyārabhataḥ karmārabhamāṇasya tatsamagram । sam ity ekībhāve agraṃ phalaṃ tena saha pravilīyate brahmarūpaṃ pratipadyate । karmāpi brahmaiva tatprabhavatvāt । yo hi karma tyajati tena brhamaiva tyaktaṃ bhavati । asmiṃ karmaprakaraṇe sarvāsu gītāsu karmapravṛttir eva bhagavatā darśitā yasya sarve samārambhāḥ ity ārabhya ।

tad atra bhagavanmatavināśakāḥ kecin mahāmāyāvinaḥ sūtrakam iva paṭaṃ kurvantaḥ karmanivṛttim eva varṇayanto lokaṃ vipratārayanti ।।

kriyākārakeṣu sarveṣu brahmābhigataṃ paśyan svayaṃ brahmāsmīti bhāvitātmā tenaiva rūpeṇāvasthāya karma kurvan brahmaiva āpnotīti phalaṃ darśayann āha 

brahmārpaṇaṃ brahmahavir brahmāgnau brahmaṇā hutam । brahmaiva tena gantavyaṃ brahmakarmasamādhinā ।।

brahmeti । arpyate samarpyate yena juhūr hastādinā tatkaraṇaṃ kārakaṃ brahma haviḥśabdasāhacaryād dhavyasevārpaṇaṃ pratīyate । haviḥ somājyapayaḥprabhṛti hūyamānaṃ dravyam । devatām uddiśya hūyata iti sampradānakārakaṃ devatāpy ākṣiptaiva । brahmaiva agnir brahmāgnir āhavanīyaḥ smārtaś copāsanīyas tasminn adhikaraṇe svayaṃ brahmaṇā kartrā hutaṃ havanaṃ nirvartitam ।

tenaiva kurvatā brahmaiva gantavyaṃ prāptavyam । brahmātmakaṃ karma brahmakarma tasmiṃ karmaṇi samādhir yasyāsau brahmakarmasamādhis tena । pañcakārakagrahaṇaṃ pradarśanārtham । yāvān yatra śrautaḥ smārto vā kārakagrāmas tatsarvaṃ brahmeti pratipattavyam iti । brahmaiva samastaḥ prapañcaḥ sarvaṃ khalv idaṃ brahma iti śruteḥ । tatra yaḥ sarveṣu vikāreṣu kāraṇarūpaṃ brahmānugataṃ paśyati sa samyagdarśī । yathā śarāvādiṣu mṛtsvarūpam anugatam । na cātra mano brahma itivad brahmadṛṣṭyā kārakopāsanaṃ codyate kiṃ tu tattvadarśanam । tatra hi yuktam iti śabdaprayogāt pratīkopāsanam । ata eva sarvātmadarśitvāt brahmaiva tena gantavyam iti brahmaprāptivacanaṃ yuktam ।

nanu śreyān dravyamayāt iti jñānayajñastutyarthaṃ

prakaraṇam । keyam ākasmikī pratibhā । anekavidhāyakavākyasamūho hi prakaraṇam ucyate । te cāneke yajñaviśeṣāḥ prativākyaṃ brahmaprāptyupāyā upadiśyante । jñānajñāpakatvān nānuvādaḥ । stutiś ca tenaikena ślokena siddheti na kṛtsnaṃ prakaraṇaṃ stutyartham । na ca vidhim antareṇa stutiḥ kvacid arthavatī । kiñca vidyamānena guṇena pādakaṃ tarhi śāstraṃ na stutiparam । dvitīye ca kalpe sarvavedoktam anṛtam iti pratipadyeta । aniṣṭaṃ caitat ।

anye tu brahmārpaṇam ity oṅkāre brahmopāsanam ity upadiśyate iti vadanti ।

teneyaṃ trayī vidyā vartate । etasyaivākṣarasya praśāsane gārgi sūryācandramasau iti śrutiḥ kilaitam arthaṃ darśayatīti tad asat । udgīthāvayavasyauṅkārasya varṇātmakasyopāsanaṃ tatra vidhīyate śrutatvān na brahmopāsanam iti sthitam । tena iyam ity etasyaiva stutyartham iti vyākhyātam ity alaṃ prasaṅgena ।।

idānīṃ yajñabhedāḥ pradarśyante । kvacit kasyacid adhikāraḥ sambhavati 

dvaivam evāpare yajñaṃ yoginaḥ paryupāsate । brahmāgnāv apare yajñaṃ yajñenaivopajuhvati ।।
daivam iti । deveṣu bhavaṃ yajñaṃ daivaṃ hiraṇyagarbhopāsanam
ādityādyupāsanaṃ ca । tathā ca brāhmaṇam vidyayā devaloko devo bhūtvā devān apy eti iti । karmayoginaḥ paryupāsate । devādibhāve api jñānotpattir iṣyate । tad yo yo devānāṃ pratyabudhyata sa eva tad abhavat tatharṣīṇāṃ tathā manuṣyāṇām iti śruteḥ । brahmaivāgnis tasmin yajñaṃ svam ātmānam antaḥkaraṇaṃ vivakṣitam । na jīvaḥ । yat kiñcij jñeyaṃ jānātīti yajña ity ātmavacano atra nirdiśyate । yajñenātmanātmasamīpavartinā manasopajuhvati । brahmātmanor ekīkaraṇaṃ vivakṣitam ।।

śrotrādīnīndriyāṇy anye saṃyamāgniṣu juhvati । śabdādīn viṣayān anya indriyāgniṣu juhvati ।।
śtoreti । anye gurukulavāsino naiṣṭhikā brahmacāriṇaḥ ।saṃyama evāgniḥ saṃyamāgniḥ । pratīndriyaṃ saṃyamabhedād
bahuvacanam । teṣu śrotrādīni juhvati । brahmacaryeṇa kālaṃ kṣapayantīty arthaḥ ।

śabdādīn viṣayān anye gṛhasthāḥ śāstrābhyanujñānād indriyāgniṣu juhvati yojayanti । tathā ca smṛtiḥ nityaṃ sugandhasnānaśīlaḥ

iti ।।

apare tu 

sarvāṇīndriyakarmāṇi prāṇakarmāṇi cāpare । ātmasaṃyamayogāgnau juhvati jñānadīpite ।।
sarvāṇīti । sarvāṇīndriyakarmāṇi buddhīndriyāṇāṃ karmāṇi
rūpādigrahaṇāni । karmendriyāṇāṃ ca vacanād ānaviharaṇotsargānandalakṣaṇāni । prāṇaḥ pañca vāyavaḥ । teṣāṃ karmāṇi । bahir nirgamanaṃ prāṇakarma । adhastād avanayanam apānakarma । vyāyamanaṃ vyānakarma । ākuñcanaprasāraṇād yaśitapītasya samānayanaṃ samānakarma । ūrdhvanayanam udānakarma । ātmani saṃyama evāgnis tasmin juhvati । 
samyagjñānadopite yo ayaṃ jñānaprabandhaḥ kriyāvistāraś
cātmaprabandhād ātmany evāsau pralīyata iti manyamānās tatkṛtena
guṇadoṣeṇa pratyahaṃ na lipyanta iti ।।

amī cāpare 

dravyayajñās tapoyajñā yogayajñās tathāpare । svādhyāyajñānayajñāś ca yatayaḥ saṃśitavratāḥ ।।

dravyeti । dravyaiḥ somājyapayaḥprabhṛtibhir nirvartyo yajño yeṣāṃ te dravyayajñāḥ । tapaḥ kṛcchracāndrāyaṇādi yajante tapoyajñāḥ । 

pratyāhāras tathā dhyānaṃ prāṇāyām atho dhāraṇā ।
tarkaś caiva samādhiś ca ṣaḍaṅgo yoga ucyate ।।

sa eva yajño yeṣāṃ te yogayajñāḥ । svādhyāyayajño vedābhyāsaḥ । 
jñānayajño vedārthajñānaṃ yajño yeṣāṃ te jñānayajñāḥ ।
mīmāṃsā śārīrakādivyākhyātāro yatayo yatnavantaḥ saṃśitavratā
akhaṇḍitavratāḥ ।।

amī cāpare 

apāne juhvati prāṇaṃ prāṇe apānaṃ tathāpare । prāṇāpānagatī ruddhvā prāṇāyām aparāyaṇāḥ ।।

apāneti । apāne pūraṇavṛttau prāṇaṃ recakavṛttiṃ juhvati । mastakamadhyavartinī suṣumṇā nāḍī । taddvāreṇa bāhyaṃ vāyumantaḥ praveśayanti । ādityamaṇḍalād ārabhya hṛdaye cittapraveśānusārī vāyuḥ praveśito bhavati । atha viparyayeṇa prāṇe recakavṛttau pūraṇavṛttiṃ yāvad ādityas tāvac cittavṛttim ūrdhvām udgamayanti । so ayaṃ brahmapatho yoginām utkrāntikāle samyagabhyasta upayujyate । 
prāṇāpānagatī prāṇāpānavṛttī ruddhvā niruddhya
yativaccharīraṃ kumbhakavṛttyā pūrayitvā kumbhakaprāṇāyām
aprāyaṇāḥ ।।

uttareṇa gītārthaḥ parisamāpyate 

apare niyatāhārāḥ prāṇān prāṇeṣu juhvati । sarve apy ete yajñavido yajñakṣapitakalmaṣāḥ ।।
apara iti apare niyatāhārāḥ । udarasyārdham annena pūrayet
tṛtīyaṃ bhāgam udakena caturtho vāyusañcārārthaḥ iti yogaśāstre darśitam । te kumbhakenāvasthitāḥ prāṇān prāṇeṣu juhvati । sarve prāṇāpānād ayas tasyām avasthāyām ekībhavantīty arthaḥ । sarve apy ete yajñavidaḥ pūrvoktās tenaiva yajñena kṣapitaṃ kalmaṣaṃ pāpaṃ yeṣāṃ te tathoktāḥ ।।

yajñaśiṣṭāmṛtabhujo yānti brahma sanātanam । nāyaṃ loko asty ayajñasya kuto anyaḥ kurusattama ।।

yajñeti । yajñārthaṃ viniyuktaṃ dravyam । tacchiṣṭaṃ tad evāmṛtaṃ bhuñjata iti yajñaśiṣṭāmṛtabhujo yathāsambhavaṃ yānti prāpnuvanti brahma sanātanaṃ purāṇam । sākṣāt pāramparyeṇa vā 
phalākāṅkṣibhiḥ kriyamāṇā brahmaprāptihetavo bhavanti ।
yaḥ punar ayajñas tasya nāyaṃ loko asti ।
kuto anyaḥ paraloka iti saṅkṣepaḥ ।।

evaṃ bahuvidhā yajñā vitatā brahmaṇo mukhe । karmajān viddhi tān sarvān evaṃ jñātvā vimokṣyase ।।
evam iti । evamuktena prakāreṇa brahmaṇo mukhe brahma vedaḥ tasya
mukhaṃ dvāram upalabdhisthānaṃ vedavākyeṣu vitatāḥ prathitāḥ ।

ete yajñā vaidikā eva । ete na puruṣabuddhiprabhavā ity abhiprāyaḥ । karmajān kāyikavācikamānasajān evaṃ jñānaṃ kṛtvā vimokṣyase saṃsārāt । kuru karmaiva iti kartavyatāyāḥ pratiślokam adhikṛtatvāt kṛtveti noktam ।।

yadi tarhi yajñair eva mokṣaṃ prāpyate kim ātmajñānenety āśaṅkyām āha 

śreyān dravyamayād yajñāj jñānayajñaḥ parantapa । sarvaṃ karmākhilaṃ pārtha jñāne parisamāpyate ।।

śreyān iti । pūrvatra kevalād eva jñānān mokṣo nāsti । kiṃ tarhi । karmasahitād ity uktam na karmaṇām anārambhād iti ārabhya । atra punaḥ kevalād eva karmaṇo mokṣaḥ syād ity āśaṅkya nirasyate । asti cedam api darśanam । yājñikānāṃ keṣāñcin mokṣo nāma svarga eva tāratamyāvasthitaḥ । sa ca karmasādhyo nānyo astīty āśaṅkābījaṃ cedam । evaṃ jñātvā vimokṣyasa iti । śreyān praśasyataro dravyamayād agniṣṭomāder jñānayajñaḥ । kutaḥ । sarvaṃ hi jñāne sati parisamāpyate apavargāya samarthaṃ bhavatīty arthaḥ । tathā ca śrutiḥ sa ya ātmānam eva lokam upāste hāsya karma kṣīyate iti । jñānasahitaṃ karmākṣayaphalatvān na kṣīyata ity ucyate । svarūpato hi kṣaṇikaṃ karma । tathā yo vā etad akṣaram aviditvā

gārgy asmalloke juhoti dadāti tapasyaty api bahūni varṣasahasrāṇi antavān evāsya sa loko bhavati iti ।।

tatpunar ātmajñānam itthaṃ vijānīhīty upadiśati 

tad viddhi praṇipātena paripraśnena sevayā । upadekṣyanti te jñānaṃ jñāninas tattvadarśinaḥ ।।

tad iti । prakarṣeṇa nipatya pātaḥ praṇipātas tena dīrghanamaskārādinā ca taj jānīhi । paripraśnaḥ kim ātmatattvaṃ kā vidyā kā cāvidyeti । devā śuśrūṣā । 
jñānino api santaḥ kecid atattvadarśino bhavanti ।
ato viśeṣayati tattvadarśina iti ।
sākṣātkṛtātmasattattvā ity arthaḥ ।।

kīdṛśaṃ taj jñānam iti 

yaj jñātvā na punar moham evaṃ yāsyasi pāṇḍava । yena bhūtāny aśeṣeṇa drakṣyasy ātmany atho mayi ।।
yad iti । yaj jñātvādhigamya pūrvavan mohaṃ na yāsyasi ।
yena jñānena bhūtāny aśeṣeṇa kārtsyena drakṣyasy ātmany atho mayi parameśvare । yathā samudre sarvā āpaḥ praviśyaikībhavanti tathātmani sarvādikāraṇe sarvo ayaṃ prapañcaḥ praviśyaikībhavatīty arthaḥ । kāryakāraṇayor

abhedāt suvarṇarucakādivat ।
īdṛśaṃ jñānam apare upadekṣyantīti ।।

jñānam āhātmyam adhunā kathyate 

api cedasi pāpebhyaḥ sarvebhyaḥ pāpakṛttamaḥ । sarvaṃ jñānaplavenaiva vṛjinaṃ santariṣyasi ।।
apīti । yady api pāpebhyaḥ puruṣebhyaḥ pāpakṛttamo asi sarvaṃ
vṛjinaṃ pāpaṃ jñānam eva plavas taraṅgas tena samyak tariṣyasi ।।

tatra dṛṣṭāntam āha 

yathaidhāṃsi samiddho agnir bhasmasāt kurute arjuna । jñānāgniḥ sarvakarmāṇi bhasmasāt kurute tathā ।।
yatheti । yathaidhāṃsīndhanāni samyagiddho agnir bhasmasāt kurute
bhasmībhāvaṃ nayati tathā jñānāgniḥ sarvakarmāṇi yāny ārabdhaphalāni janmāntarakṛtāni bhaviṣyaccharīrahetutvenāvasthitāni yāni cāsmiṃ janmani prāgjñānotpatteḥ kṛtāni tāni bhasmīkaroti । 
yāni punar ārabdhaphalāni teṣām upabhogenaiva kṣayaḥ ।
tathā ca śrutiḥ tasya tāvad eva ciraṃ yāvan na vimokṣye atha
sampatsye iti ।।

yataś caivam 

na hi jñānena sadṛśaṃ pavitram iha vidyate । tat svayaṃ yogasaṃsiddhiḥ kālenātmani vindati ।।

nahīti । na hi jñānena sadṛśaṃ pavitraṃ pāvanam iha śāstrīye arthe vidyate । nirdhāraṇe saptamī । tac ca jñānaṃ svayam ity ātmavācī । karmayogena saṃsiddhaḥ kālena paripākahetunātmani svabuddhāv eva labhate ।।

praṇipātādi bāhyanimittam uktam । idānīm ābhyantaraṃ nimittam āha 

śraddhāvāṃl labhate jñānaṃ tatparaḥ saṃyatendriyaḥ । jñānaṃ labdhvā parāṃ śāntim acireṇādhigacchati ।।

śraddhāvān iti । śraddhāstikyabuddhir ādarapratyayas tadvāṃs tatparaś ca śravaṇamananādiṣu vyāpṛtaḥ । kaś ca vyāpriyate । saṃyatendriyaḥ । sa labhate । tac ca labdhvā parāṃ śāntiṃ muktim acireṇa kṣipraṃ cādhigacchati ।।
śraddhāvān ity uktam । tasya pratyudāharaṇārtham āha 
ajñaś cāśraddadhānaś ca saṃśayātmā vinaśyati । nāyaṃ loko asti na paro na sukhaṃ saṃśayātmanaḥ ।।
ajñeti । ajño anātmavādī yathokte arthe śraddhām akurvann
aśraddadhāno bhavati vā mokṣo na veti saṃśayātmā sa vinaśyati । ajñānāt ।

saṃśayaḥ pāpīyān ity āha nāyaṃ loko asti sarvaprāṇisādhāraṇaḥ paro dūrataḥ । sukhaṃ ca tasya nāstīti । idam arthād uktam avidvān saṃśayātmā ca karmabhir badhyata iti ।।

kaṃ punar na karmāṇi nibadhnanti tad āha 

yogasannyastakarmāṇaṃ jñānasañchinnasaṃśayam । ātmavantaṃ na karmāṇi nibadhnanti dhanañjaya ।।

yogeti । yogena brahmārpaṇanyāyena paramātmani sannyastaṃ samyag nyastam ekīkṛtaṃ karma yenātmajñānena ca samyak chinnaḥ saṃśayo yena tam ātmavantam apramādinaṃ na karmāṇi nibadhnanti ।।

prakaraṇārtham upasaṃharati 

tasmād ajñānasambhūtaṃ hṛtsthaṃ jñānāsinātmanaḥ । chittvainaṃ saṃśayaṃ yogam ātiṣṭho attiṣṭha bhārata ।।
tasmād iti । tasmād ajñānasambhūtam ajñānād utpannaṃ hṛdaye
sthitaṃ saṃśayaṃ jñānam evāsis tena chittvā nirasya yogam ātiṣṭha brahmārpaṇanyāyena karmānutiṣṭha । utthiṣṭha ca । kim āsse viṣaṇṇamanā iveti ।

iti śrībhagavadbhāskarakṛte gītābhāṣye caturtho adhyāyaḥ ।।

atha pañcamo adhyāyaḥ ।

mayi sarvāṇi karmāṇi ity anena kartuḥ kṛtānāṃ karmaṇām īśvare sannyāsa uktaḥ । anantaram brahmārpaṇam ity ārabhya brahmaiva kartṛ kārakānantaraṃ karma ca ity uktam । anayoḥ karmasannyāsakarmayogayor bhedābhedajñānaviṣayayoḥ parasparavirodhād ekapuruṣānuṣṭheyatvānupapattau katarad anayoḥ praśastataram iti praṣṭum arjuna uvāca 

sannyāsaṃ karmaṇāṃ kṛṣṇa punar yogaṃ ca śaṃsasi । yaḥ śreyān etayor ekas taṃ me brūhi viniścitam ।।

sannyāsam iti । mayi sarvāṇi iti sannyāsaṃ kathayasi brahmārpaṇam yogasannyastakarmaṇām yogam ātiṣṭha iti karmayogam । śeṣaṃ nigadavyākhyātam ।।

śrībhagavān uvāca 

sannyāsaḥ karmayogaś ca naiḥśreyasakarāv ubhau । tayos tu karmasannyāsāt karmayogo viśiṣyate ।।
sannyāsa iti । mayi sarvāṇi iti ya uktaḥ sannyāso yaś cāyam
anantaroktaḥ karmayogas tāv ubhau naiḥśreyasakarau । niḥśreyasam eva naiḥśreyasam । ayaṃ tu viśeṣaḥ karmasannyāsāt karmayogo viśiṣyate । katham । dvaitaviṣayo hi sannyāsaḥ ।

karmayogaḥ punar advaitaviṣayaḥ । sākṣātsamyagdarśanāśrayo
brahmaivedaṃ sarvaṃ kartrādi sarvaṃ taṃ parād ādyo anyatrātmanaḥ sarvaṃ veda iti śruteḥ । ataḥ karmayogo viśiṣyate ।।

tatra sannyāsalakṣaṇaṃ tāvad upadiśyate 

jñeyaḥ sa nityasannyāsī yo na dveṣṭi na kāṅkṣati । nirdvandvo hi mahāvāho sukhaṃ vandhād vimucyate ।।

jñeya iti । yo hi paramahitaṃ na dveṣṭi na ca hitaṃ phalam ākaṅkṣati । kartavyam eveti nityakarma kṛtvā tatphalam īśvare samarpayati sa nityasannyāsīti boddhavyaḥ । sa cetthaṃlakṣaṇaḥ karmastho api nirdvandvo rāgadvaṣādirahitaḥ sukham anāyāsenaiva saṃsārabandhān mucyate mokṣaṃ prāpnotīty arthaḥ ।।

nanu sannyāsakarmayogayor naiḥśreyasaphalatvam ayuktam । svarūpabhedavat phalabhedo yukta iti । imām āśaṅkām apanetum āha 

sāṅkhyayogau pṛthagbālāḥ pravadanti na paṇḍitāḥ । ekam apy āsthitaḥ samyag ubhayor vindate phalam ।।
sāṅkhyeti । nanu ca sannyāsayogau prastutau ।
kim idam avāntaram aprastutam upanyasyate । nāyaṃ doṣaḥ । tāv eva sannyāsayogau sāṅkhyayogaśabdābhyāṃ nirdiṣṭau । yogaśabdas tāvat prakṛtaṃ yogaṃ na

jahāti । sāṅkhyaśabdo api sannyāsaṃ pratyāyayati bhedadarśanasāmānyāt । yathā ya evaṃ vidvān paurṇamāsīṃ yajate । ya evaṃ vidvānam āvāsyām iti paurṇamāsyam āvāsyāśabdābhyāṃ prastutya śabdāntareṇa tayor upādānaṃ kriyate darśapūrṇamāsābhyāṃ yajate

iti । tatra darśaśabdo amāvāsyāvacanaḥ । tadvad atra sāṅkhyaśabdaḥ sannyāsavivakṣayā prayukta ity avirodhaḥ । kṛtvā karmāṇīśvare yaḥ samarpayati sa sannyāsī । sāṅkhyo na kāpilo niragnir niṣkriyaś ca iti sāṅkhyaśabdopādānaprayojanam । tau sāṅkhyayogāv ity arthaḥ । pṛthakphalau bālā avivekino vadanti । vastutas tu ekam apy āsthitaḥ samyagubhayor vindate phalam । sannyāsināpi bhedena karma kṛtvā samarpaṇakāle bhedadarśanam evāśrīyate । sarvaṃ karma brahmaprabhavaṃ tad brahmasvarūpam eva pratipadyata ity evaṃ samarpaṇāt ।।

avasthāmātram atra bhidyate । sannyāsaḥ pūrvāvasthā । ghaṭamānayogitvāt karmayogas tv anantarāvasthā jñānaparipākāt । tac ca 

yad eva sāṅkhyāḥ paśyanti yogais tad anugamyate । ekaṃ sāṅkhyaṃ ca yogaṃ ca yaḥ paśyati sa paśyati ।।

yad eveti । yad eva sāṅkhyāḥ paśyanti brahma yogais tad anugamyate । tad eva cintyata ity arthaḥ । evaṃ ca paramārthata ekaṃ sāṅkhyaṃ ca yogaṃ ca yaḥ paśyati sa paśyati । tārkikāṇāṃ tu kāpilāḥ sāṅkhyāḥ । teṣām anyad darśanam । yogā naiyāyikāḥ prasiddhās teṣām anyad darśanam iti ।

na ca te sāṅkhyā yogāś ca na ca tārkikāḥ samyak paśyantīti bhagavato abhiprāyaḥ ।।

tayor ekatvam upapādayitum āha 

sannyāsas tu mahābāho duḥkam āptum ayogataḥ । yogayukto munir brahma na cireṇādhigacchati ।।

sannyāseti । sannyāsa iti sannyāsī cety arthaḥ । sannyāsa iti prathamāvibhakter nirdeśān nāsāv āptavyaḥ । tathā hi sannyāsam iti dvitīyā syāt । atra sannyāsaśabdena sannyāsī lakṣyate । atra arśāditvān matvarthīyo akāraḥ । yathā pāpebhya iti tadvān ucyate । sannyāsī brahmaprāptum ayogato duḥkhaṃ prāptuṃ śaknuyāt । duḥkham iti kriyāviśeṣaṇam । kliṣṭataram ity arthaḥ । yogenābhedadarśanena yukto muniḥ sannyāsī na cireṇa brahmādhigacchati । tasmāt so api samarpaṇavelāyām abhedadarśanastha ity upapannaṃ samānaphalatvam ।।

yataḥ sannyāsī yogam āsādya brahma pratipadyate nānyathā । ato yogasya yad uktaṃ viśiṣṭatvaṃ tad upapannam ity upasaṃharati 

yogayukto viśuddhātmā vijitātmā jitendriyaḥ । sarvabhūtātmabhūtātmā kurvann api na lipyate ।।
yogeti । yogena yukto advaitadarśane avasthito viśuddhātmā
nirmalīkṛtabuddhir vijitātmā jitamanovṛttir ata eva jitendriyaḥ

sarvabhūtānām ātmabhūta ātmā yasya so ayaṃ kurvann api na lipyate । 
karmāpi brahmarūpeṇa bhāvyamānam amṛtatvāya kalpate ।
na hi tatra lepaśaktir astīti ।।

vaidikād anyeṣv api pramādakṛteṣu karmasv avaśyaṃbhāviṣu 

naiva kiñcit karomīti yukto manyeta tattvavit ।
paśyac chṛṇvan spṛśaṃ jighran bhuñjan gacchaṃ chvasan svapan ।।

pralapan visṛjan gṛhṇann unmiṣan nimiṣann api । indriyāṇīndriyārtheṣu vartanta iti dhārayan ।।
naiveti । naiva kiñcit karomīti yukto yogī manyeta tattvavit ।
teṣāṃ brahmakāryatvāl lepadoṣāpanuttaye । kāni punas tāni । paśyann ityādi । prāṇendriyavyāpāro atra nirdiśyate । paśyann iti buddhivyāpāraḥ । buddhyā paryālocayann ity arthaḥ । śṛṇvann iti śrotrayoḥ । spṛśann iti tvagindriyasya । jighrann iti ghrāṇendriyasya । bhuñjann iti rasanendriyasya । gacchann iti pādayoḥ । śvasann iti prāṇasya । svapann iti manasaḥ । pralapann iti vāgindriyasya । visṛjann iti pāyūpasthayor vyāpāraḥ । gṛhṇann iti hastayoḥ । unmeṣanimeṣau netrayoḥ । cittaṃ dhārayed yukto manyeta ity asyārthe dhārayed iti nirdiṣṭaḥ ।।

atra kecid agṛhyamāṇakāraṇaṃ sarvakarmatyāgaṃ bahuśaḥ purastād

asmābhir nirastam api śiṣṭavigarhaṇabhayāc chāstrārthatayā sampādayituṃ tu samīhante । kaṣṭam aho yat tapasvinaḥ prathamam aśreyaskare vartmani kenacit pralobhya pravartitāḥ paścāt paridūyamānahṛdayā yuktyābhāsais tad eva samarthayituṃ yatante nāsadgrahaṃ vimuñcanti ।

tān atra pṛcchāmaḥ kena pramāṇena sarvatyāgaḥ pratijñāyata iti । yadi vacanatas tan nāsti । pratyuta tṛtīyacaturthayoḥ karmakartavyataivoktā । niyataṃ kuru karma tvam iti ityādinā vidvān yuktaḥ samācaran iti ca vidvadaviduṣoḥ karmoktaṃ svārthaṃ parārthaṃ vā । atha nyāyataḥ so api nāsti । katham । yadi tāvad ātmajñānakarmayogayor virodhāt karmānupapattir ucyate mithyājñānahetuko hi karmayogaḥ । tac ca mithyājñānaṃ vidyayā nirastam kuru kramapravṛttiḥ iti ।।

yady evaṃ laukikavaidikakarmaṇor yugapan nivṛttiḥ prasajyate mithyājñānabhāvasyāviśeṣāt । tataś ca śaucācamanabhikṣāṭanādīnām apy abhāvaḥ syāt । ekahetunibandhanānāṃ saha vā pravṛttiḥ saha vā nivṛttir nānyā gatir asti । kasya vā śaucam । nātmano nityaśuddhatvāt । na śarīrasya mamedam iti sambandhābhāvāt ।

paraśarīravat karmatyāgavac ca dehatyāgo yuktaḥ । kṛtaprayojanatvān na bhojanādibhis tasya poṣaṇam । aiśvaryāc ca muktasya tyāgaśaktir asti । ko nāmāparatantraḥ san skandhena kuṇapaṃ vahet । kiṃ ca bhedavijñānopaśamāt sarvakarmatyāgāc ca muktim anvicchatā saiva nāstīti pratijñātaṃ syāt । aśakyatvāt । yathā samudre taraṅgāpanayād aśakyaṃ snānam । dehendriyamanāṃsi hi nimittabhūtāni । teṣu vidyamāneṣu naimittikaṃ bhedajñānaṃ kāyikaṃ mānasikaṃ vācikaṃ ca trividhaṃ karmāvaśyaṃ pravartate । agnīndhanasaṃyoge dhūmavat tasmāj jñānakarmaṇor virodhād iti hetvābhāsaḥ paravyāmohārtham upanyasto asiddhaś coddālakayājñavalkyādīnāṃ brahmavidāṃ putrajanakādyupadeśapravṛttiśravaṇāt । upadeśo api karmaiva । tvaṃ ca kevalaṃ niṣkriyātmavit kriyā nāstīti bravīṣi । na ca tathā vartase । bhikṣāṭanādi vyāpāraṃ karoṣi । ataś ca tatkārī ca bhavāṃs taddveṣī ca bhavān iti । kas tvadīyaṃ vacanaṃ pramāṇīkuryāt ।

atha jñānakarmaṇor viruddhaphalatvāt tyāga iti cet । tan na । viduṣā kriyamāṇasya karmaṇopavargārthatvād avirodhaḥ । bhinnaphalatve hi virodhaḥ syāt । kiṃ ca praśno api tena nopapadyeta sannyāsaṃ

karmaṇāṃ kṛṣṇa iti । na hi sannyāsaśabdena purastāt tyāgaḥ
kvacid uktaḥ । mayi sarvāṇi karmāṇi itīśvare teṣāṃ samarpaṇam uktam । tasmāt tatraivāyam anuvādo na tyāgaya ।

yogaś ca brahmārpaṇam ity atrokto anūdyate । tatra praśnopapattir vyākhyātā । yadi ca viduṣaḥ karmatyāgaḥ purastād uktaḥ syād arjunena pratipannaḥ syāt tatra tyāgakarmayogayor bhinnapuruṣaviṣayatvāt kutaḥ praśnāvatāro bhāgavataṃ cottaraṃ nāma pratipadyate । naiḥśreyasakarāv ubhau । karmasannyāsāc ca karmayogo viśiṣyata iti । kathaṃ karmatyāgas tadanuṣṭhānaṃ ca niḥśreyasakaram । tyāgo hy abhāvaḥ । nāsau niḥśreyasakāraṇam avastutvāt । yadi cābhāvān niḥśreyasaprāptiḥ ko hi gurukarmabhāraṃ śirasodvahet । na ca vidvatkartṛkayos tyāgakarmaṇoḥ praśnottaraṃ sambhavati viduṣo api karmatyāgānupapatter uktatvād nyāyato vacanataś ca ।

nāpy avidvatkartṛkaviṣayaṃ praśnottaram । aviduṣo api karmaṇy evādhikāra iti tyāgasya niṣiddhatvāt । tad evam avācakena granthena svābhipretasamarthanā kriyate yena tasya syād gomayenāpi pāyasam ity alam atiprasaṅgena । idaṃ tāvat tattvaṃ śreyo'rthinām uktam । nāsmākaṃ vyasanitā । 
ye viparītavartmagāminas te sarve pathi sthāpayitavyā iti ।
asadvartmani hi prāyeṇa prāṇino rasanta iti ।।

athedānīṃ prakṛtam anusarāmaḥ । yāni punaḥ śāstracoditāni 
brahmaṇy ādhāya karmāṇi saṅgaṃ tyaktvā karoti yaḥ । lipyate na sa pāpena padmapatram ivāmbhasā ।।

brahmeti । dṛṣṭāntopanyāsārthaḥ ślokaḥ ।।

taiḥ karma kriyate । kiṃ viśiṣṭaiḥ kimarthaṃ cety ucyate 

kāyena manasā buddhyā kevalair indriyair api । yoginaḥ karma kurvanti saṅgaṃ tyaktvātmaśuddhaye ।।

kāyeneti । kevalaśabdaḥ kāyādibhiḥ pratyekaṃ sambadhyate । kevalaśabdaḥ śuddhavacanaḥ । kevakaiḥ phalāsaṅgadoṣarahitaiḥ । saṅkalpavikalpātmakaṃ manaḥ । buddhir adhyavasāyātmikā । ātmaśuddhaye । śuddhiḥ kaivalyaṃ muktir ity arthaḥ । kāyādiviśuddho mukta ity ucyate ।।

tasyeva spaṣṭīkaraṇārtham idam ucyate 

yuktaḥ karmaphalaṃ tyaktvā śāntim āpnoti naiṣṭhikīm । ayuktaḥ kāmakāreṇa phale sakto nibadhyate ।।

yukta iti । yuktaḥ karmaphalaṃ tyaktvā śāntiṃ muktiṃ prāpnoti naiṣṭhikīṃ niścalām । yaḥ punar ayuktaḥ kāmakāreṇa । kāmaḥ pravṛttīcchā । pravṛttyā phale sakto nibadhyate na mucyate । tasmād yogī brahmaṇi niḥkṣipya karma kurvan mucyata ity upasaṃhārāthaṃ vacanam etat ।।

śāntiṃ prāptasya kīdṛśī phalāvasthā bhavatīti tāṃ pradarśayati । yadi hi sāvasthā nirāyāsā syāt tatas tatprāptyupāye jñānakarmasamuccaye tadarthinaḥ pravartante nānyatheti 

sarvakarmāṇi manasā sannyasyāste sukhaṃ vaśī । navadvāre pure dehī naiva kurvan na kārayan ।।

sarveti sarvaśabdaḥ prakṛtavācī । laukikaṃ vaidikaṃ ca karma manasādhyātmacetasā brahmaṇi sannyasya samyaṅ nikṣipya sarvaṃ karma brahmaiva tad eva kartṛ tatphalaṃ ca tad evety ekatvam anudṛśya pūrvam anuṣṭhānāvasthāyāṃ paścāl labdhajyotiḥ paramātmabhūtaḥ sukham āste । vimuktasamastabandhano antaryāmivat । bhogenaiva prārabdhakāryakarmakṣayapratijñānāc charīrapātaṃ yāvat । tathā ca śrutiḥ tasya tāvad eva ciraṃ yāvan na vimokṣye atha sampatsya iti । yāvac charīrān na vimokṣyate । prārabdhaphalakarmaphalabhogapratibandhāt tāvad evāsya viduṣaś ciram । bhuṅkte tu karmaṇi pratibandhābhāvāt । atha sampatsye mucyata ity arthaḥ । śarīrastho api kaunteya na karoti na lipyata iti smṛteḥ । ata eva vaśī svatantraḥ । atha āsir audāsīnye dhātur vartate । yathā gṛhaṃ parigṛhyāste । kṣetraṃ parigṛhyāste ity audāsīnyavacano nopadeśavacanas tadvat । idānīṃ

paramātmā saṃvṛtaḥ san navadvāre pure sapta śīrṣaṇyāni dvārāṇi dve nāsike dve netre tathā kṣotre mukham ekam adhastād dve pāyūpasthe pure śarīre dehī naiva kurvann akārayan । dehasambandhasya nivṛttatvāt tadānīṃ tatkāryābhāvaḥ । prāgavasthāyāṃ tu dehasambandhānuvṛttteḥ kurvan kārayaṃś cāste । kurvann iti svatantrakartṛtvam । kārayann iti hetukartṛtvam । yathā pacati pācayati iti । tathā ca śrutiḥ salila eko draṣṭā dvaito bhavati iti । evaṃ paramātmasthitivarṇanārthāyām asyāṃ gītāyām uttarā gītā samyag ghaṭate । na kartṛtvaṃ na karmāṇi lokasya sṛjati prabhuḥ iti । yadi punaḥ sthitaprajñasya yogino dhriyamāṇaśarīrasya kṣutpipāsāparītasyāvastheyam ucyate । tasyāḥ kaḥ prasaṅgo lokasya kartṛtvakarmasarjane yena pratiṣiddhyate । prabhuśabdaprayogo api paramātmāvasthāvarṇane yujyate ।
karmatyāgavādino anyathā vyācakṣate । samyagdarśī vidvān
sarvakarmāṇi nityanaimittikādīni samyaṅ nyasya tyaktvāste sukhaṃ vaśī jitendriyaḥ । kva punar āste tadā navadvāre śarīre । naiva kurvan na kārayann iti । tad idaṃ svapakṣarāgāviṣṭacetaso apavyākhyānam । na hi brahmabūtasya viduṣo deha āsanam upapadyate । nāsau parimite deśe kāle viśeṣe vāste sarvadeśakālavyāpitvāt । uktaṃ ca nityaḥ sarvatragaḥ sthāṇuḥ iti । na cāmūrtasyātmanaḥ

śarīre mūrtavad upaveśanaṃ yujyate । abhimānakṛtam eva tv āsanam । mamedaṃ śarīram aham asya svāmīty akurvann akārayaṃś ceti cāsminn api vyākhyānaviśeṣaṇaṃ nāvakalpate । sarvaśabdaś ca śaucācamanāśanapānādīnāṃ śiṣyapraśāsanādīnām anantānām abhipretānāṃ kriyamāṇatvāt sarvatyāgavādinaḥ sutarām avācakaḥ ślokaḥ ।

manograhaṇaṃ ca kartavyaṃ sarvakarmāṇi tyaktvā manasaiva hi tyajyante । sannyāsagrahaṇaṃ ca na kuryāt । santyajyeti brūyād asandehāya । tasmān manasā sannyasyeti pūrvoktasannyāsapratipattyarthaṃ yogasannyastakarmāṇām iti । tasmād yathā vyākhyāta evārtha iti sthitam ।। so ayaṃ paramātmā 

na kartṛtvaṃ na karmāṇi lokasya sṛjati prabhuḥ । na karmaphalasaṃyogaṃ svabhāvas tu pravartate ।।

neti । muktaḥ prabhur īśvaraḥ saṃpannaḥ prāṇinam iva putrabhṛtyakalatrāder niyantavyasyeha vidyamānatvād ucyate । na kartṛtvādi । ātmīyasya poṣyavargasya vidhatte svasvāmisambandhanivṛtteḥ । na ca tatkṛtasya śuśrūṣādilakṣaṇasya karmaṇo anurūpaṃ phalaṃ sṛjaty āptakāmatvād iti । muktasya prāg iva bhṛtyādeḥ kartṛtvādiniṣedhaḥ । kartṛtvādinibandhanaṃ

hi svābhāvikam ajñānam । tatsahatā yatnenāpanayan । yathā prabhur lokasya kartṛtvādi svecchayā na sṛjati na ca karmaphalasaṃyogam āptakāmatvāt । sve mahimni hi paramātmā sthitaḥ । prāṇikarmaiva sṛṣṭau phalotpattau ca nimittam । īśvaras tu karmānuvidhāyī tanniyantā । na hi tasya kartṛtvādyāpādane lokasya prayojanam asti । udāsīno hi saḥ । anyathā vaiṣamyanairghṛṇyaprasaṅgād īśvaro rāgādimān syād yathā rājā bhṛtyānāṃ karmāṇi ca vidhatte । rājabhṛtyānāṃ ca parasparasāpekṣatvam anyonyopakārakatvāt । kathaṃ tarhi lokasya kartṛtvakarmaphalasaṃyogas tad āha 

svabhāvas tu pravartate । ajñānaprabhavau rāgadveṣau । tanmūlaṃ ca karma । tataḥ śarīragrahaṇam । punaḥ karma । punar ajñānam । punā rāgadveṣāv iti । tad idaṃ cakram eva samāvartate । avyāpṛtāvastheśvaratulyateha paripakvayogasya yogino dṛṣṭāntārtham uktā । vyāpṛtāvasthasya tv īśvarasya jīvakarmānurūpaṃ jagad vidhātṛtvaṃ śrutismṛtisiddhaṃ sthitam eva ।।

yasmād ayam īśvaro na rāgādivaśena lokaṃ prerayati tasmāt 

nādatte kasyacit pāpaṃ na caiva sukṛtaṃ vibhuḥ । ajñānenāvṛtaṃ jñānaṃ tena muhyanti jantavaḥ ।।

nādatta iti । kasyacit sambandhi pāpaṃ na gṛhṇāti । na ca sukṛtam ādatte । hetvabhāvāt । yad īśvaraḥ svārthaṃ na prayuṅkte lokaṃ kena tarhi muhyanti jantavaḥ । tad āha svabhāvas tv ajñānenāvidyayā avidyā viparītajñānam । dehādiṣv ātmābhimāno brahmasvarūpāgrahaṇaṃ cāvidyocyate । tayāvṛtam ācchannaṃ jñānam । tena muhyanti ।।

yeṣāṃ tu 

jñānena tu tadajñānaṃ yeṣāṃ nāśitam ātmanaḥ । teṣām ādityavaj jñānaṃ prakāśayati tatparam ।।

jñāneneti । ādityavad yathādityo bhuvanamaṇḍalaṃ prakāśayati 
tathā jñānam ajñānaṃ vināśya tatparaṃ brahma prakāśayati ।
brahmaivedaṃ sarvam ahaṃ ca brahmeti jñānī paśyatīty arthaḥ ।। 
।।

ita ūrddhvam adhyāyaparisamāpteḥ jñānasvarūpaṃ tatsahakārisādhanaṃ pratipādyate 

tadbuddhayas tadātmānas tanniṣṭhās tatparāyaṇāḥ । gacchanty apunarāvṛttiṃ jñānanirdhūtakalmaṣāḥ ।।
tadbuddhaya iti । tasmin brahmaṇi buddhir yeṣāṃ te tadbuddhayaḥ ।
tad brahmātmā yeṣāṃ te tadātmanaḥ । tasmin niṣṭhā tātparyaṃ yeṣāṃ te tanniṣṭhāḥ । tatparāyaṇaṃ gatir yeṣāṃ te tatparāyaṇāḥ । tadātmānas te

tanniṣṭhās tatparāyaṇā gacchanty apunarāvṛttiṃ mokṣaṃ jñānena nirdhūtaṃ kalmaṣaṃ yeṣāṃ te tathoktāḥ ।।

kīdṛśaṃ tajjñānam ity ucyate 

vidyāvinayasampanne brāhmaṇe gavi hastini । śuni caiva śvapāke ca paṇḍitāḥ samadarśinaḥ ।।

vidyeti । vidyā ca vinayaś ca vidyāvinayau । vinayaḥ saṃyamaḥ । tābhyāṃ sampanne adhyayanādisaṃskāravatīty arthaḥ । brāhmaṇavat pūjyatamatvād gograhaṇam । madhyamapratipattyarthaṃ hastigrahaṇam । śvaśvapākagrahaṇam atyantāspṛśyāvajñeyabhūtapratipattyartham । paṇḍitāḥ samadarśinas teṣu brahmāvasthitaṃ samaṃ taddarśino bhavanti । sarvabhūteṣv ākāśavad brahmasvarūpam anugataṃ paśyantīty arthaḥ ।।

evaṃ samgyagdarśināṃ ko lābha ity āha 

ihaiva tair jitaḥ sargo yeṣāṃ sāmye sthitaṃ manaḥ । nirdoṣaṃ hi samaṃ brahma tasmād brahmaṇi te sthitāḥ ।।

iheti । ihaiva dehasthitaiḥ sargaḥ punarbhavo jito nāśito yeṣāṃ sāmye brahmasvarūpe sthitaṃ manas tair ity arthaḥ । nirdoṣaṃ hi samaṃ brahma । buddhyā dṛśyamānaṃ sarvaṃ brahmaiva sampadyate yathā lavaṇakṣetre patitaṃ vastu lavaṇam eva sampadyate । tasmin brahmaṇi te sthitā yasmāt tasmāt tair jita iti pūrveṇa sambandhaḥ ।।

yaś ca brahmaṇi sthitas tasya tadanuguṇaṃ sādhanam upadiśyate 

na prahṛṣyet priyaṃ prāpya nodvijet prāpya cāpriyam । sthirabuddhir asaṃmūḍho brahmavid brahmaṇi sthitaḥ ।।

na preti । priyam iṣṭaṃ prāpya na prahṛṣyaṃ prakarṣeṇa hṛṣṭir na kartavyā । nodvijet prāpya cāpriyam । udvegaś cittavyathā । sthirā niścalā nirvicikitsā buddhir yasya sa sthirabuddhiḥ । asammūḍho viviktacittavṛttiḥ ।।

kiṃ ca 

bāhyasparśeṣv asaktātmā vindaty ātmani yat sukham । sa brahmayogayuktātmā sukham avyayam aśnute ।।

brahmeti ।।

kathaṃ punar ātmasukhasyaivākṣayatvam । nanu bāhyasparśasukham apy akṣayam eva । neti brūmo yasmāt 

ye hi saṃsparśajā bhogā duḥkhayonaya eva te । ādyantavantaḥ kaunteya na teṣu ramate budhaḥ ।।

ya iti । ye hi saṃsparśajā bhogā viṣayasaṃsarganibandhanā duḥkhasya yonayas te । yoniḥ kāraṇaṃ yasmāt । ādimanto antavantaś ca kādācitkāḥ kṣaṇikāḥ । na teṣu ramate budho doṣadarśī ।।

kaś ca yogī sukhī ca । tad ucyate 

śaknotīhaiva yaḥ soḍhuṃ prāk śarīravimocanāt । kāmakrodhodbhavaṃ vegaṃ sa yuktaḥ sa sukhī naraḥ ।।

śaknotīti । ihaiva dehe soḍhuṃ niyantuṃ yaḥ śaknoti na
lakṣaṇamātraṃ kiṃ tu prāk śarīravimocanād ādehapātāt । kāmodbhavaṃ krodhodbhavaṃ vegam । aprāptaprāptīcchā kāmaḥ । tena preritā cittavṛttiḥ kāmavego anuraktacittavṛttinirodhaḥ kāmodveganirodho netravaktravikāraliṅgaḥ । krodhas tadutthaveganirodhaś ca । tāv etau vegau niruṇaddhi yaḥ sa yuktaḥ sa sukhī naraḥ ।।

yaś caivaṃ kāmakrodhau jitvātmani vartate sa mukta evam ucyate ।

tad āha 

antaḥsukho antarārāmas tathāntarjyotir eva yaḥ । sa pārtha paramaṃ yogaṃ brahmabhūto adhigacchati ।।
antar iti । antarātmani sukhaṃ yasyāsāv antaḥsukhaḥ ।
antarātmany ārāmaḥ krīḍā yasyāsāv antarārāmaḥ । tathāntarātmā jyotir yasyāsav antarjyotir na vāyvādityādijyotiḥ । saḥ । he pārtha paramaṃ yogam । yujyata iti yogaḥ । taṃ paramātmānaṃ brahmabhūto adhigacchati ।।

kiṃ ca

labhante brahmanirvāṇam ṛṣayaḥ kṣīṇakalmaṣāḥ । chinnadvaidhā yatātmānaḥ sarvabhūtahite ratāḥ ।।

labhanta iti । labhante brahmaṇi nirvṛttim । athavā brahmaiva nirvāṇaṃ paramaṃ sukham ṛṣayo darśanavantaḥ । kṣīnaṃ kalmaṣaṃ yeṣāṃ te

tathoktāḥ । chinnaṃ dvaidhaṃ saṃśayo yais te chinnadvaidhāḥ ।
yatātmāno niyatāntaḥkaraṇāḥ । sarvabhūtānāṃ hite ratā ahiṃsakā ity arthaḥ ।।

sa eva śāntyupāyaḥ punaḥ kathyate । bahuśaḥ śravaṇāt sthirasaṃskāraṃ cittaṃ bhavatīti 

kāmakrodhaviyuktānāṃ yatīnāṃ yatacetasām । abhito brahmanirvāṇaṃ vartate viditātmanām ।।

kāmeti । yatīnāṃ parivrājakānām । pradarśanārtham etat । gṛhasthādīnām athavā yatīnāṃ yatnavatām । tasyaiva nirvacanaṃ yatacetasām iti । abhito nikaṭe samīpakāla ity arthaḥ । nirvāṇaṃ niratiśayānandarūpam । abhita ubhayata ity eke । jīvatāṃ mṛtānāṃ ceti । tad asat । jīvatāṃ cen nirvāṇaṃ siddhaṃ mṛtānāṃ daṇḍāpūpikayā siddham iti na vaktavyaṃ mṛtānām iti ।। 

muktyupāyaprasaṅgena yogo api muktyupāyatvād antaraṅgatvāc ca prastūyate । ṣaṣṭhe tasya vistaro bhaviṣyati 

sparśān kṛtvā bahir bāhyāṃś cakṣuś caivāntare bhruvoḥ । prāṇāpānau samau kṛtvā nāsābhyantaracāriṇau ।।

sparśān iti । bāhyān viṣayān bahir eva kṛtvā yadā manasāntarātmani nopasarpanti tadā viṣayā bahir eva bhavanti ।

bhruvo antare madhye cakṣuḥ kṛtvety adhikriyate । prāṇāpānāv ucchvāsaniḥśvāsau nāsābhyantaracāriṇau samau kṛtvā । nocchvāsam adhikaṃ karoti na niḥśvāsam । yathāsvabhāvapravṛttau kṛtvety arthaḥ ।।

vastūttareṇa samāpyate 

yatendriyamanobuddhir munir mokṣaparāyaṇaḥ । vigatecchābhayakrodho yaḥ sadā mukta eva saḥ ।।

yateti । niyatānīndriyāṇi mano buddhiś ca yasya sa vaśī । mananān muniḥ । mokṣaḥ param ayanaṃ gatir yasyāsau mokṣaparāyaṇaḥ । vigatecchā bhayaṃ ca krodhaś ca yasyāsau vigatecchābhayakrodhaḥ । icchā kāmaḥ । ya evaṃ sadā vartate mukta eva saḥ । nāsty atra vicāraṇā ।।

muktyupāyo darśitaḥ । jñeyas tu sākṣād darśayitavyo yaṃ jñātvā mucyetety āha 

bhoktāraṃ yajñatapasāṃ sarvalokamaheśvaram । suhṛdaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ jñātvā māṃ śāntim ṛcchati ।।

bhoktāram iti । yajñānāṃ tapasāṃ ca phalam । tasya bhoktā । bhoktaiḥ samarpitāni phalāni dṛṣṭvā tṛṣyati tuṣyatīty arthaḥ । na punas tasyāptakāmasyānyādṛśo bhogo asti yathā nivedya samarpaṇe devatā prīyate । sarveṣāṃ lokānāṃ mahāntaram īśvaram । suhṛdaṃ pratyupakārānapekṣayo apakāriṇaṃ jñātvā māṃ śāntiṃ mokṣam ṛcchati

gacchati । dehasambandhābhimānaśūnyasya subrahmarūpeṇāvasthitasyahagavato vacanam । ṛṣīṇām apīmāni vacanāni paramārthesatye avasthitānām । yathā tad vai tathā paśyann ṛṣir vāmadevaḥ
pratipede ahaṃ manur abhavaṃ sūryaś ca iti । ata eva sarvakarmāṇi manasā ity upapannam ।। 

iti śrībhagavadbhāskarakṛte gītābhāṣye pañcamo adhyāyaḥ ।।

atha ṣaṣṭho adhyāyaḥ ।

anantarātīte granthe kevalajñānasaṅkīrtanāt tāvanmātrād eva muktiḥ syād ataḥ karmatyāgaḥ kartavya iti sāṅkhyadarśanākulitacetasaḥ saukaryāc ca mumukṣor buddhiḥ syāt tāṃ nirākartum āha 

śrībhagavān uvāca 

anāśritaḥ karmaphalaṃ kāryaṃ karma karoti yaḥ । sa sannyāsī sa yogī ca na niragnir na cākriyaḥ ।।
