anāśrita iti । anāśritaḥ karmaphalābhisandhivarjitaḥ kāryaṃ nityaṃ karma svāśrayam avihitaṃ karoti yaḥ sa sannyāsī sa yogī ca । sa sannyāsī mayi sarvāṇi karmāṇi ity uktalakṣaṇo yogī ca brahmārpaṇam iti । na niragnir nirastāgniḥ । akriyas tyaktakarmā । naivaṃvidhaḥ sannyāsī yogī ca yaḥ । iha vidyayā saha sambandho nakartuḥ । sāṅkhyānāṃ prasiddhas tyaktakarmā caturthāśramī so atra pratiṣidhyate । yo hi buddhipūrvaṃ kartavyaṃ na karoti nāsāv āśrāmī । prāyaścittī hi saḥ । tena saha vidyayā saha sambandho na kartavyaḥ । atraikaveṇupāṇayaḥ karmatyāginaṃ mūrdhni padaṃ nihitam upalabhya

tad anyathā kartuṃ prayatamānā bahvasambaddhaṃ garjanti । gṛhasthasya stutyarthaṃ sannyāsitvaṃ yogitvaṃ cocyate । na punar niragner akriyasya ca nirākaraṇaṃ kriyata iti । tad asat । anyanirākaraṇaparatvād asya vākyasya । nityaṃ karma kurvataḥ sannyāsitvaṃ yogitvaṃ ca । pūrvair eva ca vacanaiḥ prāptasya niragner akriyasya ca pratiṣedhārthaṃ nānyo asya vākyasyārtho asti । yathā 

saṅkṣepāpavistarāv etau jñātvā ca pāramārthikau । ajasram āste tac cittaḥ sa paraṃ yāti netaraḥ ।। iti ।

yathā cābruvan pūrve vedapāragāḥ 

sa dharma iti vijñāyate yo netareṣāṃ sahasraśaḥ ।

ity uktavedapāragapratiṣedho avagamyate । na ca stutir ekasmād atra vaktavyā । karmayogitvaṃ gṛhasthādīnāṃ yathāśrutam evāsti । tatra sannyāsitvaṃ nāma yadi karmatyāgitvam ucyate tato nindā syān na tu stutiḥ । atha phalatyāgitvaṃ tad apy asty eva । kiṃ tatra stutikalpanayā । pūrvatra bahuśaḥ phalasaṅkalparahitatvam upadiṣṭam mā phaleṣu tyaktvā karmaphalāsaṅgam iti । yasya hi bhagavān pramāṇabhūtas taduktatvād eva pratipadyate । kiṃ stutyā । atha apramāṇaṃ tathā stutir api vyarthā । na cātra stutiparatvaṃ vākyasya pratīyate

yathābhūtārthapratipādakatvāc chāstrasya । tasmād bālaiḥ
svaceṣṭitaṃ vihāya bhagavad upadiṣṭena mahāmahāmārgeṇa gantavyam । yo hi svātmānaṃ vañcayitvā kaṣṭāṃ gatiṃ prāpayati nāsau pareṣāṃ hitāyopadiśati । tathā coktam 

ātmānaṃ yo abhisandhatte pareṣāṃ sa hitaḥ katham । iti ।

nanu sannyāsī sa yogī ca ity ekaḥ puruṣaḥ katham ucyate । virodhāt । yadi sannyāso kathaṃ karmayogī । sannyāsitvaṃ yogitvaṃ ca na yugapad sambhavati । kiṃ ca niragnir akriyaś ca sannyāsī prasiddhaḥ । kriyāvān karmayogī । tasmād anyaḥ sannyāsī । karmayogī cānya iti parābhiprāyam āśaṅkyāvirodhaṃ darśayati 

yaṃ sannyāsam iti prāhur yogaṃ taṃ viddhi pāṇḍava । na hy asannyastasaṅkalpo yogī bhavati kaścana ।।
yam iti । sannyāsam iti yaugiko atra sannyāsaśabdo mayā prayuktaḥ ।
paramātmani kṛtānāṃ karmaṇāṃ samyak tyāgo niḥkṣepaḥ samarpaṇaṃ sannyāsaḥ । sarvasarvāśramāṇām aviśiṣṭo na rūḍhiśabdaḥ prayuktaḥ । yathā vaidyaśabdaś cikitsake rūḍho yaugikas tu sarvatra vartate । vidyāyāṃ bhavo vaidya iti yo yo vidyāvān sa sarvo abhidhīyate ।

yad uktaṃ sannyāsitvaṃ yogitvaṃ ca yugapan na sambhavati iti । nāsau doṣo hetusadbhāvāt । tad āha na hy asannyastasaṅkalpo niḥkṣiptaḥ karmasaṅkalpo yenāsau sannyastasaṅkalpaḥ । tadviparīto na yogī bhavati kaścana । anekajanmapravṛttabhedavijñānavāsitacetasāṃ na sahasābhedavijñānam upapadyate । ahaṃ brahmāsmi iti । tasmāt sarvamā kta? yas tatprasādād advaitajñānaṃ pratipadyate । tasmād etad vai puruṣasyāvasthābhedamātraṃ phalam ।

punar ekam eva ma ktir ity abhipretyoktam yaṃ sannyāsam ityādi 
praśāntamanasam iti paryantaṃ sannyāsam ityādi praśāntamanasam

iti paryantaṃ ye prāṇinaḥ uktāḥ santi tān ātmavaśaṃ kuryād
ity arthaḥ ।।

yadi yogasukhaṃ syāt tato viṣayasukhaparityāgo yujyate । anyathā ko nāma parityajed ity āha 

praśāntamanasaṃ hy enaṃ yoginaṃ sukham uttamam । upaiti śāntarajasaṃ brahmabhūtam akalmaṣam ।।

praśānteti । praśāntamanasaṃ hy enaṃ yasmād yoginam uttamaṃ viṣayasukhād upaiti । śāntarajasaṃ rajoviṣayeṣu pravṛttir brahmabhūtam bhū prāptāv ātmanepadīti smaraṇād bhūtaśabdaḥ prāptyarthaḥ । brahmaprāptam akalmaṣam ।।

prakaraṇarthopasaṃhārārthaḥ ślokaḥ 

evaṃ yuñjan sadātmānaṃ yogī vigatakalmaṣaḥ । mukhena brahmasaṃśleṣam atyantam upagacchati ।।

evam iti । evam uktaprakāreṇātmānaṃ yuñjan yogī vigatasamastakalmaṣaḥ sukhenākleśena brahmasaṃśleṣanimittam atyantasukham aśnute ।।

yadātyantaparipakvo yogo bhavati tadā kathaṃ paśyatīty ucyate 

sarvabhūtastham ātmānaṃ sarvāṇi bhūtāny ātmani ।
paśyate yogayuktātmā sarvatra samadarśanaḥ ।।
sarvabhūteti । ahaṅkāraparicchinnam avidyānibandhanam aupādhikaṃ
rūpaṃ vihāya sarvabhūtastham ātmānaṃ sarvāṇi bhūtāni । ātmani paramātmani । ātmaparayor abhedavivakṣayā nirdeśaḥ । 
paśyate yogena yukta ātmā yasyāsau ।
sarvatra samadarśano brahmadṛṣṭir ity arthaḥ ।।

sarvatra paramātmānam 

yo māṃ paśyati sarvatra sarvaṃ ca mayi paśyati । tasyāhaṃ na praṇaśyāmi sa ca me na praṇaśyati ।।
yo mām iti । yo māṃ paśyati sarvatra tasyāhaṃ na praṇaśyāmi ।
na tirobhavāmi । sa ca me na tirobhavati । matsvarūpa evāsau bhavatīti ।।

phalakathanam etat kriyate । kiṃ ca 

sarvabhūtasthitaṃ yo māṃ bhajaty ekatvam āsthitaḥ ।
sarvathā vartamāno api sa yogī mayi vartate ।।

sarvabhūteti arvabhūtasthitaṃ yo mām ekatvam āsthito bhajate । sarvathā vartamāno api vā mayi madvikāre vākprapañce cetasā vartamāno mayy evāsau ca vartate । brahmātmanā dṛśyamānaṃ sarvaṃ brahmaiva sampadyate yathodakātmanā dṛśyamānaḥ phenataraṅgādis tatraivāntarbhavati tadvat ।

anye tu yatheṣṭaceṣṭham apīti vadanti । tad ayuktam । nahīdṛśasya yatheṣṭaceṣṭatā bhavati ।।

yoginaḥ sarvabhāveṣu maitrībhāva upadiśyate 

ātmaupamyena sarvatra samaṃ paśyati yo arjuna । sukhaṃ vā yadi vā duḥkhaṃ sa yogī paramo mataḥ ।।

ātmaupamyeti । upamāyā bhāva aupamyam । tenātmaupamyenātmasādṛśyenety arthaḥ । sarvatra bhūteṣu sukhaṃ vā paśyati । samam । yathā mama sukhaṃ priyaṃ tathānyeṣām । yathā me duḥkham apriyaṃ tathā pareṣām iti । sa yogī paramo mataḥ ।।
sarvatrādvaitadarśanalakṣaṇo yoga uktaḥ । tasya jñānam asambhavam

arjuna uvāca 

yo ayaṃ yogas tvayā proktaḥ sāmyena madhusūdana । etasyāhaṃ na paśyāmi cañcalatvāt sthitiṃ sthirām ।।

yo ayam iti । yo ayam yogas tvayā prokto manasaś cañcalatvāt sthirāṃ sthitiṃ tasya na paśyāmi ।।

yasmāt 

cañcalaṃ hi manaḥ kṛṣṇa pramāthi balavad dṛḍham । tasyāhaṃ nigrahaṃ manye vāyor iva suduṣkaram ।।

cañcalam iti । cañcalaṃ hi manaḥ kṛṣṇa aticañcalam itas tato dhāvamānam । pramathituṃ śīlam asyeti pramāthi । balavad vegavad dṛḍhaṃ bhedavāsanayā ghanīkṛtam । tasyāhaṃ nigrahaṃ nirodham ātmany avasthānam । vāyor iva suduṣkaraṃ manye ।।

bhagavān uvāca 

asaṃśayaṃ mahābāho mano durnigrahaṃ calam । abhyāsena tu kaunteya vairāgyeṇa ca gṛhyate ।।

asaṃśayam iti । nigraham avasthānam । asaṃśayam yathāvad avasitaṃ tathā । kiṃ tv abhyāsena । paramātmani punaḥ punaś cittapraveśanam abhyāsaḥ । śāstreṇa sarvaṃ brahmeti sāmānyena vijñāya hṛdayakamalanilaye paramātmānaṃ cintayataś cittaṃ dṛḍhabhūmikaṃ

bhavati । evam abhyāsena gṛhyate vairāgyeṇa ca । na prapañcaviṣayaṃ vaitṛṣṇyaṃ vairāgyam । yatprapañcaviṣayaphalaṃ tatsarvam aśāśvatam iti doṣadarśanād vaitṛṣṇyam utpadyate ।।

etāvān iha niścayaḥ asayatātmanā yogo duṣprāpa iti me matiḥ । vaśyātmanā tu yatatā śakyo avāptum upāyataḥ ।।
asaṃyateti । asaṃyatātmanā avaśīkṛta ātmā mano yasya tenaogo duṣprāpo na śakyate prāptum । vaśyātmanā tu yatatā yatnaṃ
kurvatā śakyo avāptum anantaroktopāyena ।।

yadā tu yogo apraptaḥ kenacid daurbalyena tadā tasya kā gatir iti praṣṭum uvāca 

ayatiḥ śraddhayopeto yogāc calitamānasaḥ ।
lipsamānaḥ satāṃ mārgaṃ pramūḍho brahmaṇaḥ pathi ।।

anekacitto vibhrānto mohasyeva vaśaṃ gataḥ । aprāpya yogasaṃsiddhiṃ kāṃ gatiṃ kṛṣṇa gacchati ।।
ayatir iti । anekacitto vibhrānto mohasyeva vaśaṃ gata iti ca ।
ayatir yatnarahitaḥ śraddhayā copeto yogād yogasakāśāc calitamānaso anivṛttamanāḥ । aprāpya yogasaṃsiddhiṃ muktyabhāve kāṃ gatiṃ kṛṣṇa gacchati । nīlotpaladalacchaviḥ kṛṣṇo yugānurūpavarṇo vā ।।

praśnam eva sopapattikaṃ kartum āha 

kaccid ubhayavibhraṣṭaḥ śāradābhram iva naśyati । apratiṣṭho mahābāho vimūḍho brahmaṇaḥ pathi ।।

kaccid iti । kaccid iti praśnārtho nipātitaḥ । ubhayasmād bhraṣṭaḥ । karma tāvan na phalārthaṃ kṛtam īśvare samarpitatvāt । na ca jñānaṃ muktisamam utpannam । tasmād ubhayabhraṣṭaḥ । kiṃ śāradābhram iva vṛṣṭirahitaṃ naśyati kiṃ vā neti । apratiṣṭho na vidyate pratiṣṭhā yasya । brahmaṇaḥ pathi brahmaprāptimārge vimūḍho naśyati ।।

etan me saṃśayaṃ kṛṣṇa cchettum arhasy aśeṣataḥ । tvadanyaḥ saṃśayasyāsya chettā na hy upapadyate ।।

etad iti । etaṃ me saṃśayaṃ kṛṣṇa cchettum apanetum arhasi । kasmāt । tvadanyaḥ saṃśayasyāsya cchettā jagati nopapadyate ।।

uttaraṃ bhagavān uvāca 

pārtha naiveha nāmutra vināśas tasya vidyate । na hi kalyāṇakṛt tāto gacchati kaścid durgatim ।।

pārtheti । he pārtha iha loke paratra vā na tasya nāśo asti । kasmāt । na hi kalyāṇakṛt puṇyakṛd durgatiṃ kaścit tāto gacchati । tanoti putram iti yady api tātaḥ pitocyate tathāpy anyatrāpi dṛśyate pūjārtham ।।

prāpya puṇyakṛtāṃ lokān uṣitvā śāśvatīḥ samāḥ ।
śucīnāṃ śrīmatāṃ gehe yogabhraṣṭo abhijāyate ।।

atha vā yoginām eva jāyate dhīmatāṃ kule । etad dhi durlabhataraṃ loke janma yadīdṛśam ।।

prāpyeti । atheti ca । yad uktavān phaloddeśena na karma kṛtam īśvaroddeśena kṛtatvād iti । ata eva tasya puṇyakṛl lokaprāptiḥ । na hi mām uddiśya kṛtam aphalāya bhavati । bhogāyāpavargāya vā tat sampadyate ।

puṇyakṛtām iti viśeṣaṇād ye tyaktakarmāṇaḥ kevalāj jñānān muktim icchanti teṣāṃ durgatir eveti darśayati । nāpi abhijñānasya bhogaḥ phalaṃ kalpayituṃ śakyam avidyānivṛttidvāreṇa tasya muktyarthatvāt । na ca karmābhāvo bhogahetuḥ sarveṣāṃ prasaṅgāt । tad etad bhāgavatam uttaraṃ karmayoginām upapadyate nānyeṣām । śāśvatīḥ bahvīḥ samāḥ saṃvatsarān śucīnām ācāravatāṃ śrīmatām aiśvaryavatāṃ gehe jāyate । adhikāratas tasyāpekṣayā pakṣāntaram ucyate । athavā yoginām eva yogābhyāsaratānāṃ daridrāṇāṃ kule vaṃśe jāyate । dhīmatām utpadyate । dhīmatām etad dhi durlabhataram īdṛśaṃ janma ।।

sa tu jātaḥ 

tatra taṃ buddhisaṃyogaṃ labhate pūrvadaihikam । tato bhūyo api yatati saṃsiddhau kurunandana ।।

tatreti । tatra taṃ buddhisaṃyogam ātmaviṣayayā buddhyā saṃyogaṃ
labhate । pūrvadaihikaṃ pūrvajanmani bhavam । tato yatati bhūyo api tato adhikataraṃ yatate । saṃsiddhau vimuktinimittam । he kurunandana ।।

।।

kathaṃ punar asau pūrvadaihikaṃ buddhisaṃyogaṃ labhate tad āha 

pūrvābhyāsena tenaiva hriyate hy avaśo api san । jijñāsur api yogasya śabdabrahmātivartate ।।

pūrvābhyāseti । pūrvajanmasañcitaḥ saṃskāras tena hriyate prāpyate buddhipūrvasaṃyogaṃ pratyavaśo api san । kiṃ ca । jijñāsur api yogasya jñātum icchur api śabdabrahma vedoktaṃ kevalaṃ karmātivartate । yogajijñāsāpi kevalāt karmaṇo gurutarety abhiprāyaḥ ।।

kiṃ ca 

prayatnād yatamānas tu yogī saṃśuddhakilbiṣaḥ । anekajanmasaṃsiddhas tato yāti parāṃ gatim ।।

prayatnād iti । prayatnād yatamānas tu yogī prakṛṣṭena yogena yatnena yogārthaṃ yatamāno yogī saṃśuddhakilbiṣaḥ yogena yātīti smaranti yogaśāstravidaḥ । kiṃ punaḥ kṣudrapāpāni । na hy ekasminn eva janmani yogī mucyate । anekajanmajanitayogena saṃsiddho bhavati । tato yāti parāṃ gatim ।।

yogamāhātmyaṃ darśayann adhyāyam upasaṃharati 

tapasvibhyo adhiko yogī jñānibhyo apy adhiko mataḥ । karmibhyaś cādhiko yogī tasmād yogī bhavārjuna ।।
tapeti । kṛcchracandrāyaṇopavāsaparebhyaḥ kevalakarmiṇo api
karmagrahaṇena tadviṣayasya jñānasyākṣiptatvāt pūrvatrātmajñānaṃ vivakṣitam । tasmād yogī bhavārjuna । gṛhasthasyārjunasya yogopadeśāt sannyāsinām eva ṣaṣṭhe yogopadeśaḥ kṛta iti yair vyākhyāyate teṣām upasaṃhāravirodhaḥ ।।

yoginām api sarveṣāṃ madgatenāntarātmanā । śraddhāvān bhajate yo māṃ sa me yuktatamo mataḥ ।।
yoginām iti । ādityaṃ rudram anyāṃ vā devatāṃ ye yuñjate
teṣāṃ yoginām api sarveṣāṃ madgatenānantarātmanā māṃ gatena madāsaktacetasā śraddhāvān āstikyabuddhir bhajate yo māṃ sa me yuktatamo mata iti ।।
iti śrībhagavadbhāskarakṛte gītābhāṣye ṣaṣṭho adhyāyaḥ ।।
atha saptamo adhyāyaḥ ।ṣaṣthe adhyāye samādhir uktaḥ । yatra samādhīyate cittaṃ
tad īśvarākhyaṃ brahma savistaraṃ vaktavyam ity adhyāya ārabhyate । na hy ajñātasvarūpasyopāsanaṃ śakyaṃ kartum iti ।

bhagavān uvāca 

mayy āsaktamanāḥ pārtha yogaṃ yuñjan madāśritaḥ । asaṃśayaṃ samagraṃ māṃ yathā jñāsyasi tac chruṇu ।।
mayīti । mayi parameśvare svābhāvikasnehārdracetā yogaṃ
yuñjānaḥ kurvāṇa ity arthaḥ । mām āśrito madāśrito ananyaśaraṇaḥ । 
saṃśayarahitaṃ samagraṃ kṛtsnaṃ māṃ yathā yena prakāreṇa
jñāsyasi
pratipatsyase tac chruṇu ।।

vistaraprakāraṃ darśayati 

jñānaṃ te ahaṃ savijñānam idaṃ vakṣyāmy aśeṣataḥ । yaj jñātvā na punar anyaj jñātavyam avaśiṣyate ।।

jñānam iti । jñānam īśvarasvarūpabodhanam । tadvijñānasahitaṃ vakṣyāmi । viśeṣajñānam so aham ityādi । idam iti pūrvoktaṃ parāmṛśyate । vakṣyāmi । kārtsyena । yaj jñānaṃ jñātvā neha loke jñātavyaṃ punar avaśiṣyate ।।

durlabhaṃ ca matsvarūpajñānam । katham 

manuṣyāṇāṃ sahasreṣu kaścid yatati siddhaye । yatatām api siddhānāṃ kaścin māṃ vitti tattvataḥ ।।

manuṣyeti । manuṣyāṇāṃ sahasreṣu madhye kaścid yatati siddhaye yatnaṃ karoti । yatatām api teṣāṃ siddhānāṃ siddhyarthaṃ pravṛttānām ity arthaḥ । kaścin māṃ vetti tattvataḥ yāthātathyena ।।

śrotāram abhimukhīkṛtyedānīṃ savistaram ātmānaṃ kathayati 

bhūmir āpo analo vāyuḥ khaṃ mano buddhir eva ca । ahaṅkāra itīyaṃ me bhinnā prakṛtir aṣṭadhā ।।

bhūmir iti । bhūmir āpo analo vāyuḥ kham iti pañcāpi bhūtamātrā nirdiśyante sthūlaśarīrārambhiṇyaḥ । mano buddhir ity antaḥkaraṇaṃ nirdiśyate । manograhaṇena bāhyam api karaṇaṃ gṛhyate buddhīndriyakarmendriyalakṣaṇam । ahaṅkāra ity anātmany ātmābhimāna ātmani cānātmābhimānaḥ । sa ubhayavidho viparītapratyayaḥ saṃsārahetur yam avidyety ācakṣate । me madīyāṣṭadhā bhinnā prakṛtiḥ sthāvarajaṅgamalakṣaṇasya bhūtajātasya ।।

imām acetanāṃ prakṛtiṃ pṛthakkṛtya cetanāṃ nirdeṣṭum āha 

apareyam itas tv anyāṃ prakṛtiṃ viddhi me parām । jīvabhūtāṃ mahābāho yayedaṃ dhāryate jagat ।।

apareti । apareyam aṣṭadhā bhinnā prakṛtir aparā bhogyarūpā

paratantrā । aparāṃ pradhānabhūtāṃ prakṛtim ito anyāṃmatsambandhinīṃ viddhi । jīvabhūtāṃ jīvatvaṃ prāptāṃ
bhoktṛrūpeṇāvasthitām ।
yayā prakṛtyedaṃ dhāryate jagadantar anupraviṣṭam ।
tathā ca śrutiḥ anena jīvenātmanānupraviśya nāmarūpe
vyākaravāṇi iti ।।

dvābhyāṃ prakṛtibhyāṃ bhūtāni jāyanta ity āha 

etadyonīni bhūtāni sarvāṇīty upadhāraya । ahaṃ kṛtsnasya jagataḥ prabhavaḥ pralayas tathā ।।
etad iti । ete dve prakṛtī yonī yeṣāṃ bhūtānāṃ tāny etadyonīni ।
tatra yācetanā prakṛtiḥ sā kāryakāraṇarūpeṇa pariṇamate । yā tu cetanā sā svakarmopārjitaphalabhoktṛrūpeṇāvatiṣṭhate । tāny etāni jīvāviṣṭāni bhūtāni sarvāṇīty upadhāraya । te ca matsambandhinyau । katham acetanā matto jātāś cetanāḥ punar madasambhūtāḥ । yata evam ato ahaṃ kṛtsnasya jagataḥ prabhavaḥ pralayas tathā । prabhavanty asmād iti prabhavaḥ । pralīyante asminn iti pralayaḥ । kathaṃ punar gamyate samastasya jagato mūlakāraṇaṃ brahma iti । śruteḥ sad eva saumyedam agra āsīt iti । tadaikṣata sa ātmā iti । sadātmaśabdābhyāaṃ parāmarśāc cetanaṃ kāraṇaṃ niścīyate । na hy anumānena kevalenātyantātīndriyaṃ jagatkāraṇaṃ kaścit samarthayituṃ śaktaḥ । asiddhānaikāntikaviruddhadoṣaduṣṭatvāt ।

tatra sāṅkhyāḥ pradhānaṃ jagatkāraṇaṃ varṇayanti । naiyāyikavaiśeṣikāḥ paramāṇūn । tatra vādinaḥ parasparaviruddhaṃ jalpanto nādyāpy antaṃ gatāḥ । śrutivirodhāc cānumānam ābhāsībhavati ।

yat punar anumānaṃ śrutyanusāri tadanugrāhakatvenopanyasyate tadāśrīyate । yena sarvajñaḥ sarvaśaktiś cetano jagatkartā sādhyate । tārkikānumānena tu yasya yatra kartṛtvaṃ tatparijñānavatas tacchaktiyuktasya kartṛtvopapatteḥ । rathaprāsādādikartṛvad iti । 
anena cāsarvajñasyāsarvaśakter anīśvarasya siddheḥ
prakṛtavastvasiddher
anāśrayaṇam iti ।।

yata evam 

mattaḥ parataraṃ nānyat kiñcid asti dhanañjaya । mayi sarvam idaṃ protaṃ sūtre maṇigaṇā iva ।।

matta iti । mattaḥ parataraṃ nānyad aham eva sarvasmāj jagataḥ parataro mūlakāraṇatvāt । kathaṃ punar asya kāraṇatvam । śaktipariṇāmāt । tathā ca śrutiḥ tadātmānaṃ svayam akuruta yathorṇanābhiḥ sṛjate gṛhṇate ca । pracyutasvarūpasyāpy acintyaśaktitvāt pariṇāmo bhavatīti । yathākāśo vāyurūpeṇa pariṇamate na svarūpavināśo vāyoś ca pañcavṛttirūpeṇādhyātmam ।

yathā ca tantubhyaḥ paṭo jāyate tantusvarūpapracyutiḥ । vicitraśaktayo hi bhāvāḥ । tathā coktaṃ purāṇe 

acintyāḥ khalu ye bhāvā na tāṃs tarkeṇa sādhayet । prakṛtibhyaḥ paraṃ yat tu tad acintyasya lakṣaṇam ।। iti ।

tathā ca mantraḥ 

na tasya kāryaṃ karaṇaṃ ca vidyate na tatsamaś cābhyadhikaś ca vidyate । parāsya śaktir vividhaiva śrūyate svābhāvikī jñānabalakriyā ca ।। iti ।

mayi kāraṇe sarvam idaṃ kāryaṃ proktaṃ grathitam anusyūtam ity
arthaḥ ।
yathā kārpāsasūtre maṇigaṇā yathā ca mṛdi śarāvādaya iti ।।

mamaitāḥ śaktayo yā abādiṣu rasādirūpā jagataḥ saṃsthitihetavas tā darśayati 

raso aham apsu kaunteya prabhāsmi śaśisūryayoḥ । praṇavaḥ sarvavedeṣu śabdaḥ khe pauruṣaṃ nṛṣu ।।

rasa iti । rasaḥ sāro yena śarīrapuṣṭir bhavati । iha prakaraṇe jagatsthitihetūnāṃ saṅkīrtanam । vibhūtiprakaraṇe tu kāraṇam akāraṇaṃ vā yad utkṛṣṭaṃ sattvaṃ tadupadiśyate । cintanīyaṃ yad utkṛṣṭaṃ sattvaṃ tad upadiśyate । cintanīyatvenety apunaruktatā । me

rasarūpaprotā āpa iti kecid yojayanti । tad asat । yathāśrutānvayabhaṅgaprasaṅgāt । sthitinimittānāṃ ca dharmāṇām iha vaktum iṣṭatvāt । prabhāsmi । prakāśaḥ śaktiḥ । praṇava oṅkāraḥ । so api dhyānajapādāv upayogād utkarṣahetuḥ । śabdo asmy ākāśe । śabdena hi sarvalokavyavahāraḥ pravartate । puruṣasyedaṃ pauruṣaṃ puṃstvaṃ prajananakāraṇam ।।

puṇyaṃ pṛthivyāṃ gandho asmi tejaś cāsmi vibhāvasau । jīvanaṃ sarvabhūteṣu tapaś cāsmi tapasviṣu ।।

kiṃ ca 

bījaṃ māṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ viddhi pārtha sanātanam । buddhir buddhimatām asmi tejas tejasvinām aham ।।

bījam iti । bījaṃ mūlakāraṇaṃ māṃ viddhi jānīhi । sanātanaṃ nityam । buddhir asmi buddhimatāṃ bṛhaspatibhārgavādīnām । tejaḥ prabhāvo asmi tejasvināṃ rājñām ।।

balaṃ balavatāṃ cāhaṃ kāmarāgavivarjitam । dharmāviruddho bhūteṣu kāmo asmi bharatarṣabha ।।

balam iti । balaṃ balavatāṃ cāham । tad viśinaṣṭi kāmarāgavivarjitam । kāmena rāgeṇa ca rahitam । tatsamutthaṃ tu yad balaṃ

pratyavāyanimittam । svābhāvikaṃ tu yad balaṃ tad utkarṣakāraṇam । yathā vainateyādīnām । dharmeṇāviruddhaḥ kāmo bhūteṣu so aham asmi yathā svadāreṣu ।।

kiṃ ca 

ye caiva sāttvikā bhāvās tāmasā rājasāś ca ye । matta eveti tān viddhi na tv ahaṃ teṣu te mayi ।।

ye caiva sāttvikā bhāvā iti । sattvanivṛttāḥ । sāttvikā devādayo rājasā asurā manuṣyāś ca tāmasāḥ sarpādayo matta eva iti tān viddhi । na tv ahaṃ teṣu । nāhaṃ janāśritaḥ । te tu punar mayi vartante । madadhīnavṛttaya ity arthaḥ ।।

athedānīṃ guṇānāṃ svabhāvaḥ kaścid kathyate 

tribhir guṇamayair bhāvair ebhiḥ sarvam idaṃ jagat । mohitaṃ nābijānāti mām ebhyaḥ param avyayam ।।
tribhir iti । tribhir guṇamayair bhāvaiḥ kṛtsnam idaṃ jagan mohitam ।nābhijānāti mām ebhyo guṇebhyaḥ param avyayaṃ vyayarahitam ।।
tribhir etair guṇair mohitasya saṃsārakāntārottāro nāstīty āha 

daivī hy eṣā guṇamayī mama māyā duratyayā । mām eva ye prapadyante māyām etāṃ taranti te ।।

daivīti । devasyeyaṃ daivī । hiśabdo hetau । yasya devasya mama māyā nirmīyate na māyāvikāḥ । na jātam iti prakṛtir

īśvarād utpannā māyocyate । śrutiś ca nirvakti māyāṃ tu
prakṛtiṃ vidyān māyinaṃ tu maheśvaram iti । na sāṅkhyānām iva nityā । yatra māyāśabdaḥ prajñāvacanaḥ prayujyate tatreyaṃ vyutpattiḥ । mīyate paricchidyate prameyo artha iti prajñā māyā । yathā indro māyābhiḥ pururūpa īyate atīndriyaprajñābhir ity arthaḥ । duratyayā duḥkhenātyayo atikramo asyā iti duratyayā । yady evaṃ śāstropadeśānarthakyam । neti brūmaḥ । mām eva ye prapadyante te māyāṃ tarantīti na doṣaḥ ।।

nanu ye prapadyanta iti viśeṣaṇam anarthakam । nety ucyate । arthavad eva tat । katham 

na māṃ duṣkṛtino mūḍhāḥ prapadyante narādhamāḥ । māyayāpahṛtajñānā āsuraṃ bhāvam āśritāḥ ।।

na mām iti । māyayānantaroktayā prakṛtyāpahṛtajñānā āsuraṃ bhāvaṃ śāṭyānṛtādilakṣaṇam āśritāḥ ।।

ke punas te ye tvāṃ prapadyante 

caturvidhā bhajante māṃ janāḥ sukṛtino arjuna । ārto jijñāsur arthārthī jñānī ca bharatarṣabha ।।
caturvidhā iti । caturvidhāś catuṣprakārādhikāriṇo māṃ
bhajante । ārto vyasanāpannaḥ । jijñāsuḥ parameśvarasambodhane yatamānaḥ । arthārthī dravyākāṅkṣī । jñānī brahmavit ।।

kiṃ ca sarve tulyāḥ । kiñ caiṣāṃ kaścid adhika iti pṛcchāyāṃ prāptāyām āha 

teṣāṃ jñānī nityayukta ekabhaktir viśiṣyate । priyo hi jñānino atyartham ahaṃ sa ca mama priyaḥ ।।

teṣāṃ iti । teṣāṃ jñānī nityayuktaḥ । nirdhāraṇe ṣaṣṭhī । nityayuktaḥ satatābhyāsī । mayy ekasmin bhaktir yasyāsāv ekabhaktiḥ । sa viśiṣyate । priyo hi jñānino atyartham । viśvasya jagato antarātmā paramātmā । 
mamāpi cāyam evātmeti manyamāno naisargikasnehapratibaddhabuddhir
atitarāṃ bhūyo bhūyo anurajyate ।
sa ca mama priya iti ।।

yady api rāgadveṣāv īśvarasya na staḥ । tathāpi śāstrārthayāthātmyaveditvād aikātmyaprāpteḥ priya ity ucyate । itarebhya ārtādayaḥ parameśvaram āśrayanto anyebhyo mahākālabhaktebhyaḥ prakṛṣṭatarā iti darśayitum āha 

udārāḥ sarva evaite jñānī tv ātmaiva me mataḥ । āsthitaḥ sa hi yuktātmā mām evānuttamāṃ gatim ।।

udārā iti । udārāḥ sarva evaite utkṛṣṭāḥ । jñānī tu nirupacāram ātmaiva me mataḥ । katham । āsthitaḥ sa hi yuktātmā mām evānuttamāṃ gatim । na vidyate anyottamā yasyā gates tām anuttamām ।।

kim ekasminn eva janmani jñānītthaṃ tvā tvāṃ bhajate

kiṃ vānekasminn iti । yady ekasminn eva tadārtādīnām api jñānitvaprasaṅgaḥ । tatra tāratamyaṃ nopapadyata iti paramatam āśaṅkyāha 

bahūnāṃ janmanām ante jñānavān māṃ prapadyate । vāsudevaḥ sarvam iti sa mahātmā sudurlabhaḥ ।।

bahūnām iti । yata ete ārtādayaḥ teṣām api bhagavati janmāntaravāsanāsti । yato nārāyaṇam eva te bhajante nānyāṃ devatām । jñānī punar ekabhaktiḥ prayojanāntaranirapekṣaḥ sannyāsakarmayogābhyāṃ sampanno bahūnāṃ janmanām ante māṃ prapadyate । kathaṃ prapadyate । vāsudevaḥ sarvam iti । vasanti tasmin sarvabhūtāni । vasati vāntaryāmitvena sarvabhūteṣv iti vāsuḥ । devanād dyotanād devaḥ । vāsuś cāsau devaś ceti vāsudevaḥ paramātmā । ātmaivedaṃ sarvam sad eva saumyedam agra āsīt idaṃ sarvaṃ yad ayam ātmā iti śruteḥ । kāraṇātmanā prapañcātmanā cāvasthita iti pratipadyate । sa mahātmā sudurlabhaḥ । santi hi dvaitadarśino api bhaktāḥ ।।

kasmāt punaś caturvidhā eva bhajante na sarve 

kāmais tais tair hṛtajñānāḥ prapadyante anyadevatāḥ । taṃ taṃ niyamam āśritya prakṛtyā niyatāḥ svayā ।।

kāmair iti । kāmais taiḥ putrapaśvādibhir hṛtajñānāḥ । rudrādityadurgāgāṇapatiprabhṛtayo yā anyā devatāḥ tāḥ ye bhajante taṃ tam upavāsādiniyamam āśritya prakṛtyā pūrvajanmavāsanayā svayā niyatāḥ । devatāntarabhaktānāṃ ca tadvāsitacetasāṃ ca tato nivṛttir nāsti ।।

katham 

yo yo yāṃ yāṃ tanuṃ bhaktaḥ śraddayārcitum icchati । tasya tasyācalāṃ śraddhāṃ tām eva vidadhāmy aham ।।

ya iti । yo yo yāṃ yāṃ tanuṃ bhaktaḥ । tanuṃ devatāmūrtim ity arthaḥ । tasya tasyācalāṃ dṛḍhāṃ śraddhāṃ tām eva vidadhāmy aham । tatkarmānusāreṇa । karmaiva phalotpattau nimittam । īśvaras tu karmānuvidhāyī niyantṛtvenāvatiṣṭhate ।।

sa tayā śraddhayā yuktas tasyārādhanam īhate । labhate ca tataḥ kāmān mayaiva vihitān hi tān ।।

sa iti । sa tayā śraddhayā yuktas tasya devatāviśeṣasyārādhanaṃ pūjanam īhate ceṣṭate nirvartayati tato labhate ca kāmān abhipretārthān mayaiva vihitāṃs tān । hiśabdo hetau । yasmād īśvaraḥ sarvatra phaladātā karmānurūpeṇa । tathā 
ca śrutiḥ eṣa sarveśvara eṣa bhūtādhipatir eṣa bhūtapāla
eṣāṃ lokānām asambhedāya iti ।
rahasi kṛtānāṃ prakāśakṛtānāṃ ca karmaṇāṃ
phalaparipākavibhāgajño hi saḥ ।।

devatāntaropāsanāt phalaṃ cel labheta tad apy astu । ko doṣa iti ced āha 

antavat tu phalaṃ teṣāṃ tad bhavaty alpamedhasām । devān devayajo yānti madbhaktāḥ śāśvataṃ padam ।।

anteti । devān devayajo yānti prāpnuvanti । madbhaktāḥ śāsvataṃ padam ।।

kiṃ punaḥ kāraṇam । kecid devatāntaraṃ bhajante na tvām iti tad ucyate 

avyaktaṃ vyaktim āpannaṃ manyante mām abuddhayaḥ । paraṃ bhāvam ajānanto mamāvyayam anuttamam ।।

avyaktam iti । svabhāvato avyaktam atisūkṣmaṃ santaṃ vyaktiṃ prakaṭabhāvam āpannaṃ manyante mām abuddhayo alpabuddhayaḥ । ayam api nārāyaṇākhyo viṣṇur mahādevādivad devatāviśeṣa eva nātrādhikyaṃ kiñcid astīti । 
paraṃ bhāvam ajānantaḥ samastasya jagato mūlakāraṇam īśvarāṇāṃ
brahmarudrendrādīnām apy adhīśvaro ayam ity ajānanto na māṃ
bhajante ।।

kasyacid evāham anekasmin janmani bhaktim udvahataḥ svarūpaṃ vivṛṇomi na sarvasya 

nāhaṃ prakāśaḥ sarvasya yogam āyāsam āvṛtaḥ । mūḍho ayaṃ nābhijānāti loko mām ajam avyayam ।।

nāham iti । nāhaṃ prakāśaḥ sarvasya । katham । yogamāyayā sañcchanna aiśvaryayogaḥ sa eva । māyāsaṃvaraṇahetutvāt । tasmān mūḍho ayaṃ nābhijānāti mām ajam avyayam ।।

ahaṃ tu sarvajñaḥ katham 

vedāhaṃ samatītāni vartamānāni cārjuna । bhaviṣyanti ca bhūtāni māṃ tu veda na kaścana ।।

vedeti । vedāhaṃ trikālaviṣayāṇi bhūtāni jānāmi । māṃ tu veda na kaścana । ayaṃ mūḍho loka iti । yaḥ punar jñānī sa jānāti vāsudevaḥ sarvam iti ।।

kenāyaṃ loko mūḍhatvam āpannas tad ucyate 

icchādveṣasamutthena dvandvamohena bhārata । sarvabhūtāni sammohaṃ yānti sarge parantapa ।।

iccheti । icchā rāgaḥ । rāgadveṣasamutthena dvandvamohena । dvandvāni śītoṣṇasukhaduḥkhādīni tatsambandho moho dvandvamohaḥ । upakāriṣu parārtheṣu rāgāt sukhaṃ tatsambandhī mohas tannibandhanā ca pravṛttir apakāriṣu dveṣo duḥkhaṃ tannibandhanā ca nivṛttir iti । evaṃ pravṛttinibaddhāni bhūtāni sarge śarīragrahaṇeṣu sammohaṃ yānti । yadi punar dvandvaśabdena rāgadveṣayoḥ parāmarśaḥ kriyate tadā dvandvagrahaṇam anarthakam icchādveṣasamutthena mohenety etāvad vaktavyaṃ syāt ।।

tatra tu 

yeṣāṃ tv antaṃ gataṃ pāpaṃ janānāṃ puṇyakarmaṇām । te dvandvamohanirmuktā bhajante māṃ dṛḍhavratāḥ ।।
yeṣām iti । yeṣāṃ tv antaṃ gataṃ pāpaṃ kṣīṇaṃ pāpaṃ
puṇyakarmopacayāt te rāgadveṣasamutthadvandvamohavinirmuktā bhajante māṃ dṛḍhavratāḥ ।।

evam 

jarāmaraṇamokṣāya mām āśritya yatanti ye । te brahma tadviduḥ kṛcchram adhyātmaṃ karma cākhilam ।।

jareti । ye jarāmaraṇamokṣāya mām āśritya yatanti prayatante te brahma tadviduḥ । kṛcchram adhyātmaṃ karma cākhilam । vastutrayam etad arjunapraśnād anantaram uttaraṃ vakṣyāmaḥ ।।

aparam api vastucatuṣṭayam 

sādhibhūtādhidaivaṃ māṃ sādhiyajñaṃ ca ye viduḥ । prayāṇakāle api ca māṃ te vidur yuktacetasaḥ ।।
sādhibhūteti ।।
iti śrīmadbhagavadbhāskarakṛte gītābhāṣye saptamo adhyāyaḥ ।।

athāṣṭamo adhyāyaḥ ।

te brahma tad viduḥ iti ye bhagavatopakṣiptāḥ padārthās tāṃs tattvato jñātum arjunaḥ pṛcchati ।

arjunaḥ uvāca 

kiṃ tad brahma kim adhyātmaṃ kiṃ karma puruṣottama ।
adhibhūtaṃ ca kiṃ proktam adhidaivaṃ kim ucyate ।।

adhiyajñaḥ kathaṃ ko atra dehe asmin madhusūdana । prayāṇakāle ca kathaṃ jñeyo asi niyatātmabhiḥ ।।

kiṃ tad iti । ka iti svarūpapraśnatātparyam ।

katham iti prakārapraśnaḥ । kena prakāreṇāsau dehe asmin bhavatīti । prayāṇakāle maraṇakāle kena prakāreṇa jñeyo asi niyatacittaiḥ ।।

।।

bhagavān uvāca 

akṣaraṃ brahma paramaṃ svabhāvo adhyātmam ucyate । bhūtabhāvodbhavakaro visargaḥ karmasañjñitaḥ ।।

akṣaram iti । na kṣaratīty akṣaraṃ paramaṃ brahma । etad vai tad akṣaraṃ gargi brāhmaṇā abhivadanti iti śruteḥ । svabhāvo adhyātmam ucyate । akṣaraśabdavācyasya paramātmana ātmīyo bhāvo aṃśo jīvo adhyātmam ātmānaṃ deham adhikṛtya bhoktṛtvena vartata iti । bhūtānāṃ jīvānāṃ bhāvo bhāvanā karma । tasya pralayakāle stimitasyāvasthitasyodbhavo vyaktiḥ phaladānayogyatāpādanam ।

taṃ karotīti bhūtabhāvodbhavakaro visargo visṛṣṭir hiraṇyagarbhādeḥ । tathā ca mantraḥ hiraṇyagarbhaṃ janayāmāsa pūrvaṃ mano buddhyā śubhayā saṃyunaktu iti । so ayam īśvarasyāntaryāmiṇo vyāpāraḥ karmasañjñitaḥ ।

apareṣāṃ vyākhyā yajamānasya vyāpāraś carupuroḍāśādīnāṃ devatoddeśena tyāgo visargaḥ । sa eva buddhidvāreṇa bhūtāny eva 
bhāvās teṣām udbhavaṃ karotīti bhūtabhāvodbhavakaraḥ
karmasañjñita
iti ।।

adhibhūtaṃ kṣaro bhāvaḥ puruṣaś cādhidaivatam । adhiyajño aham evātra dehe dehabhṛtāṃvara ।।

adhīti । adhibhūtaṃ kṣaro bhāvaḥ । kṣarati vinaśyatīti śarīre viṣayalakṣaṇaḥ । cetano bhogyavargo jāyamāno aniruddhyamānaḥ puruṣaś cādhidaivatam । yo asāv ādityamaṇḍale hiraṇyagarbhaḥ sarvadevatāmayaḥ । kṛtsnaṃ vairājaṃ śarīram āpūryāvasthitaḥ puruṣo adhiyajño aham eva । atra yajñānām adhidevatāham eva । yajño vai viṣṇuḥ iti śatapathaśruteḥ । deho adhikaraṇatvena vyapadiśyate na mama idaṃ devatāyā iti mānasas tyāgo yāga ucyate । ye ca dravyayajñā jñānayajñāḥ svādhyāyayajñas teṣām aham evādhidevatety abhiprāyaḥ ।

anyeṣāṃ vyākhyā dehasmin vaiśvānaravidhyaṅgabhūtāhutisādhanabhūta iti । viśiṣṭāhutisādhanopalakṣaṇārthe dehaśabdo yajñaśabdaś ca viśiṣṭayajñalakṣaṇapara iti । tad ayuktam । 
yato yajñaviśeṣavyākhyānād yajñasāmānyavyākhyānaṃ yuktataram ।
visargaśabdena sargavyākhyānaṃ yuktam ।।

antakāle ca mām eva smaran tyaktvā kalevaram । yaḥ prayāti sa madbhāvaṃ yāti nāsty atra saṃśayaḥ ।।

anteti । vayaso ante tyaktvā kalevaraṃ śarīraṃ yaḥ prayāti sa madbhāvaṃ yāti । na vidyate asminn arthe saṃśayaḥ ।।

na kevalaṃ mām eva smaran māṃ pratipadyate । kiṃ tarhi 

yaṃ yaṃ vāpi smaran bhāvaṃ tyajaty ante kalevaram । taṃ tam evaiti kaunteya sadā tadbhāvabhāvitaḥ ।।

yam iti । yaṃ yaṃ bhāvaṃ devatāviśeṣam anyad vā vastu smarann ante dehaṃ tyajati taṃ tam evaiti kaunteya sadā tadbhāvanayā bhāvito vāsitāntaḥkaraṇaḥ ।।

yata evam 

tasmāt sarveṣu kāleṣu mām anusmara yuddhya ca । mayy arpitamanobuddhir mām evaiṣyasy asaṃśayam ।।

tasmād iti । tasmāt sarveṣu kāleṣu madanusmaraṇaṃ kuru । yuddhaṃ ca svadharmaṃ kurv ity arthaḥ । mayi samarpitaṃ mano buddhiś ca yasya te sa tvaṃ mayy arpitamanobuddhiḥ । manovṛttiviśeṣo vṛttimatī buddhiḥ । ekam evāntaḥkaraṇaṃ paramārthataḥ । vyavahārasiddhyarthas tu bhedavyapadeśaḥ । mām evaiṣyasy asaṃśayam । nāsminn arthe saṃśayo asti । na caitad āśaṅkitavyam 

antakāle anyathāpi smṛtir bhavatīti । īśvaro hi sarvajñaḥ karmānusārī cittavṛtter niyantā ।।

anantaroktam arthaṃ viśiṣya darśayitum āha 

abhyāsayogayuktena cetasānanyavṛttinā । paramaṃ puruṣaṃ divyaṃ yāti pārthānucintayan ।।

abhyāseti । abhyāsaḥ samānapratyayaprabandho vijātīyapratyayāvṛttikīlaḥ so ayam abhyāsayogaḥ । tadyuktena cetasānanyavṛttinā paramaṃ puruṣaṃ divyaṃ yāti pratipadyate cetasā tam evānucintayan ।।

tam eva paramaṃ puruṣaṃ punar api viśinaṣṭi 

kaviṃ purāṇam anuśāsitāram aṇor aṇīyāṃsam anusmared yaḥ । sarvasya dhātāram acintyarūpam ādityavarṇaṃ tamasaḥ parastāt ।।

kavim iti । kaviṃ sarvajñam anuśāsitāraṃ niyantāram । tathā hi śrutiḥ etasya vākṣarasya praśāsane gargi sūryācandramasau vidhṛtau tiṣṭhataḥ iti । aṇor aṇīyāṃsaṃ sūkṣmād api sūkṣmataram । sūkṣmatvam ihāvayavopacayābhāvo vivakṣitaḥ । nabhaso api sakāśād atisūkṣmaḥ । paramakāraṇatvāt sarvakarmaphalasya dhātāraṃ vidhātāram acintyarūpam । nahīdaṃ tad iti cintanīyam । asya rūpaṃ na vidyate । asthūlam anaṇv ahrasvam adīrgham alohitam iti rūpapratiṣedhāt । tathāpy upāsakānām anugrahārthaṃ rūpaṃ nirdiśyate । ādityavarṇaṃ jyotirmayam ānandaikasvabhāvaṃ tamaso 
jñānāndhakārāt parastād avasthitam ajñānatimirāpanudaṃ
svayaṃprakāśam anusmared yaḥ sa ity uttaragītāyāṃ
vākyārthaṃ samāpyate ।।

kasmin punaḥ kāle anusmaret 

prayāṇakāle manasācalena bhaktyā yukto yogabalena caiva । bhruvor madhye prāṇam āveśya samyak sa taṃ paraṃ puruṣam upaiti divyam ।।

prayāṇeti । antakāle niścalena manasā bhaktyā tadanusmaraṇāhlāditahṛdayena yogabalena ca 
yogajanitasaṃskārapātisthair
yeṇa bhruvor madhye prāṇam āveśya suṣumṇayā nāḍyā
niṣkramyety arthaḥ ।।

prāptavyaṃ padam anūdya tatprāptyupāyaṃ kathayiṣyann āha 

yad akṣaraṃ vedavido vadanti viśanti yad yatayo vītarāgāḥ । yad icchanto brahmacaryaṃ caranti tat te padaṃ saṅgraheṇābhidhāsye ।।

yad iti । edad vai tadakṣaraṃ gargi atha parā yayā tadakṣaṛam adhigamyate iti । viśanti pratipadyante । yatayo yatnavanto yad icchanto brahmacaryaṃ maithunanivṛttim caranti । gṛhasthasyāpi sarvatra vā pratiṣiddhavarjam ity anujñātagamanānivṛttasyāvaśyakaṛtukālagāmino brahmacaryam asty eva । tat te padaṃ tat padaprāptyupāyaṃ saṅgraheṇa saṅkṣepeṇa kathayiṣyāmi ।।

sarvadvārāṇi saṃyamya mano hṛdi niruddhya ca । mūrdhnyādhāyātmanaḥ prāṇam āsthito yogadhāraṇām ।।

sarveti । sarvāṇīndriyadvārāṇi saṃyamya mano hṛdayakamalanilaye parameśvare sanniruddhya tālumūlavinirgatayā brahmanāḍyā

suṣumṇākhyayorddvam udgamayyātmanaḥ prāṇaṃ mūrdhnyādhāyāsthito yogadhāraṇām । yogadhāraṇāṃ gṛhītvety arthaḥ ।।

om ity ekākṣaraṃ brahma vyāharan mām anusmaran । yaḥ prayāti tyajan dehaṃ sa yāti paramāṃ gatim ।।

om iti । śabdabrahmaikākṣaram iti viśeṣaṇaṃ saṃhitādibrahmanivṛttyartham । vyāharann uccārayan । māṃ paramātmānam ākāśavat sarvavyāpinaṃ sarvajñam ānandam amṛtam । tyajaṃ dehaṃ yaḥ prayāti sa yāti paramāṃ gatim । antakāle ca mām evaiti iti yat sāmānyenoktaṃ tad idānīṃ viśeṣitam ।

kecid atra kramamuktyabhiprāyam idaṃ na sadyomuktipradarśanārtham iti vadanti । etad vai satyakāma paraṃ cāparaṃ ca brahma yad oṅkāraḥ iti śruteḥ । oṅkārālambanopāsanaphalam idaṃ kathyata iti । tadapavyākhyānam । paravidyādhikārāt । yad akṣaraṃ vedavido vadanti

iti pratijñānāt kathaṃ kālāntaramuktirūpaṃ varṇyate ।।

na cāhaṃ durlabhaḥ satatābhiyuktasya 

ananyacetāḥ satataṃ yo māṃ smarati nityaśaḥ । tasyāhaṃ sulabhaḥ pārtha nityayuktasya yoginaḥ ।।

ananyeti । yasyānyatra ceto nāsty asāv ananyacetāḥ । satataṃ sarvadā nairantaryeṇa । nityaśa iti yāvajjīvam । tenaitad darśitaṃ 
vākyārthajñānamātreṇa kṛtārthatā ।
satatopāsanayā jñānaṃ paripakvaṃ muktikṣamaṃ sambhavatīti ।
tasyāhaṃ sulabhaḥ sukhena labhyo nityayuktasyeti nigamanam ।।

tatpadaprāptāv upāya uktaḥ । tatprāptau satyāṃ kaḥ puruṣārthaviśeṣa iti 

mām upetya punar janma duḥkhalayam aśāśvatam । nāpnuvanti mahātmānaḥ saṃsiddhiṃ paramāṃ gatāḥ ।।

mām iti । māṃ prāpya punar janma duḥkhasyālayaṃ sthānaṃ na prāpnuvanti । sthānāntaraprāptau punarāvṛttiḥ । matprāptir evānāvṛttihetur iti darśayati ।।

ā brahmabhuvanāl lokāḥ punarāvartino arjuna । mām upetya tu kaunteya punarjanma na vidyate ।।

ābrabmeti । ā brahmabhuvanād । brahmaṇo hiraṇyagarbhasya bhuvanaṃ nivāso brahmalokas tena saha । abhividhāv ākāro brahmalokasahitāḥ prāṇina ucyante । nanu ca yo ha vai tat paramaṃ brahma veda brahmaiva bhavati । tasya tāvad eva ciraṃ yāvan na vimokṣye atha sampatsye ityādhiśrutiprāmāṇyād viduṣaḥ prārabdhakarmakṣaye śarīrapātānantaraṃ mokṣāvadhāraṇāt kathaṃ brahmavidāṃ nivṛttakalmaṣāṇāṃ punar āvartanam । tathā yāvad adhikāram avasthitir adhikāriṇām iti śārīrakasūtrād adhikāre lokānugrahārthe vyāpāre ye avasthitās teṣāṃ prājāpatyādāv adhikāre īśvarānuśāsanād yāvad adhikāram avasthitir bhavati । tatra ca jñānaśeṣam abhyasyatāṃ prārabdhaphalakarmakṣaye muktiḥ । yo yo devānāṃ pratyabuddhyata sa sa

tad abhavat iti brahmasvarūpāpatteḥ । na ha vai devān pāpaṃ gacchati iti punarjanmapratiṣedhāc ca । etad anupapannam । atrocyate । prārabdhakarmaphalabhogakṣaye sarveṣāṃ muktir uktā । tac cārabdhaphalaṃ karma keṣāñcid ekaśarīrabhogyam । anyeṣām anekaśarīrabhogyam । ekajanmakṛtasyāpi karmaṇo anekaśarīrabhogyatāpi smaryate । yathāvāntaratamanāmnaḥ purāṇarṣeḥ kalidvāparayoḥ sandhau viṣṇuśāsanād vyāsapadaprāptiḥ । evaṃ muktiphalāniyamas tattadavasthāprāpter iti śārīrake api karmaphalatāratamyavaśena mukter aniyamadarśanād avirodho atra । mām upetya he kaunteya punar janma śarīragrahaṇaṃ na vidyate ।।

kasya hetor itareṣāṃ lokānām āvṛttiḥ । kālaparicchinnatvāt । parasya kāraṇaprāptasya pracyutir nāsti kāryalokeṣu hi vartamānasya । teṣāṃ vināśitvād āvṛttir avaśyaṃ bhāvinī tad etad āha 

sahasrayugaparyantam ahar yad brahmaṇo viduḥ । rātriṃ yugasahasrāntāṃ te ahorātravido janāḥ ।।

sahasreti । tathā coktam 

daivikānāṃ yugānān tu sahasraṃ parisaṅkhyayā । brāhmam ekam ahar jñeyaṃ tāvatī rātrir eva ca ।। iti ।

sahasrayugaparyantam ahar brahmaṇo jāgaritāvasthā । caturdaśam anvantarāvacchinnaḥ kālaḥ । tāvatī rātrir avāntarapralayo brahmaṇaḥ svapnāvasthā । tad evam ahorātrau saṃvatsarakalpanayā varṣaśasam āyur

brahmaṇaḥ । tato brahmā mucyate । mahāpralayo bhavati । pṛthivyādīny api bhūtāni tadā pralīyante ।।

tatrāhani rātrau ca yo vyāpāro bhūtānāṃ sa kathyate 

avyaktād vyaktayaḥ sarvāḥ prabhavanty aharāgame । rātryāgame pralīyante tatraivāvyaktasañjñake ।।

avyakteti । avyaktam avyākṛtam ucyate pañcānāṃ bhūtānāṃ sūkṣmāvasthā । karmāvidyāsahitāś ca jīvāḥ । antaryāmīśvaro adhiṣṭhātā । tad etad vyākṛtam ucyate । tathā ca śrutiḥ tad dhedaṃ tarhy avyākṛtam āsīt iti । vyaktaṃ yac ca 
carācarāṇi bhūtāni mahābhūtāni ca prabhavaty aharāgame ।
rātryāgame tu pralīyante ।
tatra vā vyākṛte avāntarapralaye carācarāṇāṃ bhūtānāṃ pralayo
mahāpralaye tu mahābhūtānām apīti viśeṣaḥ ।।

kṛtakarmavināśo akṛtakarmaphalasya cāgama iti doṣadvayaṃ pariharann āha

bhūtagrāmaḥ sa evāyaṃ bhūtvā bhūtvā pralīyate । rātryāgame avaśaḥ pārtha prabhavaty aharāgame ।।

bhūteti । saṃsārasyānāditvāt pūrvakalpakṛtānāṃ karmaṇāṃ stimitaṃ nāmāvasthānaṃ na vināśaḥ । tannibandhano ayaṃ punaḥ suranaratiryakprabhedena vicitraḥ sarga iti । sa evāyam iti । samānanāmākṛtitvād abhedo vyapadiśyate । tannāmanas tadākṛtayaś ca jāyante । vyaktīnām anyatve api yathā ta eva śālayo bhujyante tadvat । śeṣaṃ gatārtham ।।

yad etad vyaktaṃ varṇitaṃ tasmāt 

paras tasmāt tu bhāvo anyo vyakto avyaktāt sanātanaḥ । yaḥ sa sarveṣu bhūteṣu naśyatsu na vinaśyati ।।

para iti । paras tatkāṣṭhā । sarvajño avyaktaḥ karaṇāgocaratvāt । tasmād avyaktāt pūrvoktād acetanād ayaṃ cetanaḥ paramātmā sanātano nityaḥ paraḥ । katham । yaḥ sa sarveṣu naśyatsu na vinaśyati । so ayam īśvaraḥ pratipattavyaḥ ।।

avyakto akṣara ity uktas tam āhuḥ paramāṃ gatiṃ । yaṃ prāpya na nivartante taddhāma paramaṃ mama ।।

avyakteti । yo ayam avyaktaḥ paramātmākṣara ity ukto vede tato akṣarāt sambhavatīha viśvam iti tam āhuḥ śrutayaḥ । paramāṃ gatiṃ kathaṃ prāpya na nivartante । taddhāma sthānaṃ paramaṃ mama ।।

sa punaḥ kenopāyena labhyata ity āha 

puruṣaḥ sa paraḥ pārtha bhaktyā labhyas tv ananyayā । yasyāntaḥsthāni bhūtāni yena sarvam idaṃ tatam ।।

puruṣa iti । bhaktyā ananyayā tatparayā stutinamaskāradhyānadhāraṇādibhis tam eva bhajate । na devatāntaram । tasya lakṣaṇam ucayate pratipattisaukaryārtham । yasyāntaḥsthāni hi bhūtāni । kāraṇe hi kāryam antarbhavati mṛdīva śarāvam । yogena cedaṃ sarvaṃ tataṃ vyāptam ।।

īśvarasatattvaṃ nirdhāritam । tatprāptyupāyaś ca prayāṇakāle manasā ity ārabhyoktaḥ । puruṣaṃ prāptānāṃ cānāvṛttir uktā ।

athedānīṃ yena mārgeṇa gatānām anāgamo anāvṛtir yena cāvṛttir iti vibhāgena darśayann āha 

yatra kāle tv anāvṛttim āvṛttiṃ caiva yoginaḥ । prayātā yānti taṃ kālaṃ vakṣyāmi bharatarṣabha ।।

yatreti । kālagrahaṇaṃ mārgopalakṣaṇārtham । karmayogino 
jñānayoginaś
ca devayānapitṛyānamārgam arcirādilakṣitaṃ prathamaṃ darśayati
prādhānyāt ।।

agnir jyotir ahaḥ śuklaḥ ṣaṇmāsā uttarāyaṇam । tatra prayātā gacchanti brahma brahmavido janāḥ ।।

agnir iti । agnir jyotir ity arcirdevatā lakṣyate । tathā śuklapakṣadevatottarāyaṇadevatety ātivāhinyo devatā iti sthitaṃ śārīrake । tena tu prayātā gacchanti brahma paramātmānam । brahmaśabdasya tatra mukhyatattvaṃ na kāryaloko gṛhyate parabrahmaprakaraṇāc ca ।

tatra yat kaiścid uktam arcirādimārgagāmiṇāṃ hiraṇyagarbhalokaprāptir iti tad asat । ihānāvṛttir ucyate brahmaprāpteḥ svatantravṛttiḥ । tathā coktam ā brahmabhuvanāl lokāḥ iti ।।

idānīṃ kevalakarmiṇāṃ pitṛyānaḥ na punaḥ punarāvṛttilakṣaṇo mārgo nirdiśyate prasaṅgāt kathaṃ cānabhijñā nāma parābhaveyur iti darśanārtham 

dhūmo rātris tathā kṛṣṇaḥ ṣaṇmāsā dakṣiṇāyanam । tatra cāndramasaṃ jyotir yogī prāpya nivartate ।।

dhūma iti । dhūmo rātris tathā kṛṣṇa ity atrāpi devatā eva lakṣyante । nātrottarāyaṇaṃ dakṣiṇāyanaṃ rātrirahar veti vivakṣitam । yatra kvacana mṛtānāṃ samuccayakāriṇām arcirādir eva । itareṣām api dhūmādir eva । bhīṣmasyottarāyaṇapratīkṣā 
tatra maraṇaṃ praśastam iti protsāhanārthā na niyamārthā ।
śeṣaṃ gatārtham ।।

śukrakṛṣṇe gatī hy ete jagataḥ śāśvate mate । ekayā yāty anāvṛttim anyayāvartate punaḥ ।।

śukleti । ete ca gatī śuklakṛṣṇe jagataḥ । śāśvate mate 
vedoktatvāt ekayā yāty anāvṛttim anyayāvartate punar iti ।
arthasya punar vacanaṃ nigamanam ।।

mārgadvayābhijñaḥ kevalaṃ karma nārabhate samuccayārtham eva yatate niḥśreyasārthatvād iti darśayitum āha 

naite sṛtī pārtha jānan yogī muhyati kaścana । tasmāt sarveṣu kāleṣu yogayukto bhavārjuna ।।
naita iti ।।
tad etad adhyāyoktaṃ jñānam anyanindayā stūyate । śraddhālavaḥ katham atrābhiyuktā bhaveyur iti ।

vedeṣu yajñeṣu tapaḥsu caiva dāneṣu yatpuṇyaphalaṃ pradiṣṭam । atyeti tat sarvam idaṃ viditvā yogī paraṃ sthānam upaiti cādyam ।।

vedeṣv iti । vedeṣu caturṣv api yat puṇyaphalaṃ yajñeṣv agniṣṭomādiṣu tapaḥsu cāndrāyaṇādiṣu gobhūmihiraṇyadāneṣu tat sarvam idam atyeti । katham । idaṃ jñānaṃ viditvā yogī paraṃ sthānam upaiti cādyam । sarvasthānānām ādyaṃ pārameśvaraṃ padam iti ।।

iti bhagavadbhāskarakṛte gītābhāṣye aṣṭamo adhyāyaḥ ।।

atha navamo adhyāyaḥ ।

devayānena gatānām apunarāvṛttir uktā mām upetya punarjanma na vidyate iti । yat prāpyāpunarāvṛttis tasya brahmaṇo viśiṣṭaśaktiyuktasya satattvaṃ punar api kathayiṣyann āha । atyantātīndriyatvāt punaḥ punaḥ kathitam api na cetasi sthitipadaṃ labhate keṣāñcid eva puṇyakṛtāṃ cetasi sthirībhavatīti bhagavān yatate ।

bhagavān uvāca 

idaṃ tu te guhyatamaṃ pravakṣyāmy anasūyave । jñānaṃ vijñānasahitaṃ yaj jñātvā mokṣyase aśubhāt ।।

idaṃ tv iti । idaṃ tu te guhyatamam । tuśabdo atiśayārthaḥ । anasūyave paraguṇeṣu doṣāviṣkaraṇam asūyā । tadrahitāya । jñānaṃ pravakṣyāmi । vijñānasahitam । yaj jñānaṃ jñātvā mokṣyase aśubhāt saṃsārabandhāt ।

keṣāñcid eva puṇyakṛtām arcirādinā vartmanā kramamuktir uktā । idānīṃ sadyomuktir ucyata ity āhuḥ । tad asat । arcirādinaiva saṃsāramaṇḍalam atikramya liṅgaśarīraviyogān muktir nātraiva śarīre mucyate । tasmād ihaiva muktir ity apasiddhāntaḥ ।।

taj jñānaṃ stūyate śraddhājananārtham 

rājavidyā rājaguhyaṃ pavitram idam uttamam । pratyakṣāvagamaṃ dharmyaṃ susukhaṃ kartum avyayam ।।

rājeti । rājñām aśvapatijanakādīnām । teṣāṃ ca gopyaṃ pavitraṃ pāvanaṃ pratyakṣaṃ spaṣṭo avagamo yasya tad idaṃ pratyakṣāvagamam । naitatparokṣam ity arthaḥ । yathā mahāmerujñānam । dharmād anapetaṃ dharmyam । kartuṃ susukhaṃ sukaram ity arthaḥ । akṣayaphalahetutvād avyayam ।।

ye punaḥ 

aśraddadhānāḥ puruṣā dharmasyāsya parantapa । aprāpya māṃ nirvartante mṛtyusaṃsāravartmani ।।

aśraddadheti । aśraddadhānāḥ puruṣā dharmasyāsya vakṣyamāṇasya jñānarūpasya te mām aprāpya nivartante mṛtyugraste saṃsāravartmani ।।

idānīṃ tatjñānaṃ kathayati 

mayā tatam idaṃ sarvaṃ jagad avyaktamūrtinā । matsthāni sarvabhūtāni na cāhaṃ teṣv avasthitaḥ ।।
mayeti । mayā tatam idaṃ sarvam avyaktamūrtinātīndriyeṇa
sūkṣmeṇātmanā । mayi tiṣṭhantīti matsthāni । na cāhaṃ teṣv avasthitaḥ । svamahimni sthitatvāt ।।

mama yogam aiśvaraṃ paśya 

na ca matsthāni bhūtāni paśya me yogam aiśvaram । bhūtabhṛn na ca bhūtastho mamātmā bhūtabhāvanaḥ ।।

na ceti । bhūtāni bibhartīti bhūtabhṛt । na ca bhūteṣu । yathā śarīrī jīvaḥ । śarīrākārapariṇatāni bhūtāni bibharti teṣu cāvasthito na caivam aham । bhūtāni bhāvayatīti bhūtabhāvanaḥ ।।

matsthāni na ca matsthāni iti viruddhaṃ paśyaṃ dṛṣṭāntam āha 

yathākāśasthito nityaṃ vāyuḥ sarvatrago mahān । tathā sarvāṇi bhūtāni matsthānīty upadhāraya ।।

yatheti । yathākāśe vyāpaketi sūkṣmo vāyuḥ sthitaḥ sarvatrago lokatrayavyāpī tathā bhūtāni matsthānīty upadhāraya । na saṃśleṣasambandhena । kiṃ tarhi । vyāpake mayi viṣayabhūte alpaparimāṇāni bhūtāni parivartanta iti sthityavasthā darśitā ।।

adhunā pralayāvasthocyate 

sarvabhūtāni kaunteya prakṛtiṃ yānti māmikām । kalpakṣaye punas tāni kalpādau visṛjāmy aham ।।

sarveti । sarvabhūtāni kaunteya madīyāṃ prakṛtiṃ yānti । kadā kalpakṣaye । kalpādau ca punas tāni visṛjāmi ।।

katham 

prakṛtiṃ svām avaṣṭabhya visṛjāmi punaḥ punaḥ ।
bhūtagrāmam imaṃ kṛtsnam avaśaṃ prakṛter vaśāt ।।

prakṛtim iti । prakṛtiṃ svām avaṣṭabhyāvalambya bhūtagrāmaṃ bhūtasamūhaṃ visṛjāmi । avaśaṃ paratantraṃ prakṛter vaśāt । yathākarma prāṇināṃ prakṛtiḥ pariṇamate atas tadvaśāt sṛjāmi ।

kā punar iyaṃ prakṛtiḥ । pañcānāṃ bhūtānāṃ sūkṣmāvasthā vīryabhūtā । atreyaṃ vedāntaprakriyā paraṃ brahma niścalam ākāśakalpaṃ prathamam avasthitam । tatas tasya roṣād vikṛtaḥ sṛṣṭīcchāviśiṣṭo antaryāmīśvaraśabdavācyo bhavati । tato bhūtasūkṣmam avyākṛtam ākāśam utpadyate । tataḥ sūkṣmātmāyaṃ hiraṇyagarbha ity ācakṣate । tataḥ sthūlāni viyadādīni mahābhūtāni krameṇotpadyante । tato aṇḍaṃ tato virāṭ prajāpatiḥ । 
tasmin vairāje sthūlaśarīre sarve lokāḥ sarve devāḥ sarvāṇi ca
sthāvarajaṅgamāni bhūtānīti vastubhūte ayaṃ prakṛtir na
māyāmātram avastubhūtam ।।

na cāvidyā nāma kācid anātmany ātmabuddhiḥ । jīvasya pratipuruṣaṃ parabrahmasvarūpaṃ tadagrahaṃ ca muktvā kadācid āśaṅkyeta viṣamāṃ sṛṣṭiṃ kurvato doṣāya tat syād ity āha 

na ca māṃ tāni karmāṇi nibadhnanti dhanañjaya । udāsīnavad āsīnam asaktaṃ teṣu karmasu ।।

na ceti । na ca māṃ nibadhnanti karmāṇi । kasmāt । udāsīnavad āsīnatvāt । teṣu karmasu asaktatvāt । anyo api yaḥ phalāsaktas tam api karmāṇi na nibadhnanti nyāyatulyatvāt ।।

nanu ca prakṛtir nityā svatantrā bhūtasṛṣṭau pravartata iti sāṅkhyā vadanti । tad asat । tad ucyate 

mayādhyakṣeṇa prakṛtiḥ sūyate sacarācaram । hetunānena kaunteya jagad viparivartate ।।

mayeti । mayādhyakṣeṇa matta utpannā satī mayādhyakṣeṇādhiṣṭhātrā pravartitā sūyate janayati । na hy acetanā prakṛtis triguṇātmikā sāṅkhyaparikalpitā satī pravartitum arhati prāṇināṃ vicitrakarmavipākāparijñānāt । kathaṃ suranaratiryakprabhedabhinnaṃ bhuvanaṃ nirmīyate rathādīnām acetanānāṃ svataḥ pravṛttyadarśanāc ca cetanādhiṣṭhitāḥ pravartanta iti yuktam । ato matpravartitā prakṛtiḥ । anena prasavahetunā jagad viparivartate ।।

prakṛter adhyakṣam api santam 

avajānanti māṃ mūḍhā mānuṣīṃ tanum āśritam । paraṃ bhāvam ajānanto mama bhūtamaheśvaram ।।

aveti । avajānanti māṃ mūḍhāḥ prādurbhāveṣu mānuṣīṃ 
tanum āśritaṃ vāsudevo nāma kṣatriyo manuṣyo ayam ity anādaraṃ
kurvanti
paraṃ bhāvam ajānanto bhūtamaheśvaraṃ mama ।।

te ca 

moghāśā moghakarmāṇo moghajñānā vicetasaḥ । āsurīṃ rākṣasīṃ caiva prakṛtiṃ mohinīṃ śritāḥ ।।

mogheti । moghāśā moghakarmāṇo vṛthāsaṅkalpāḥ । karmāṇi ca 
teṣām
agnihotrādīni vṛtaiva jñānaṃ cānātmaviṣayatvāt ।
vicetaso avivekinaḥ rākṣasīṃ tāmasīṃ prakṛtim āsthitāḥ ।।

ye tu 

mahātmānas tu māṃ pārtha daivīṃ prakṛtim āsthitāḥ । bhajante ananyamanaso jñātvā bhūtādim avyayam ।।

maheti । mahātmānas tu lokottaraprajñā daivīṃ prakṛtiṃ sattvaguṇasambhūtā cittavṛttim āśritā bhajante sevante bhūtānām ādiṃ māṃ jñātvā ।।

kena prakāreṇa bhajante 

satataṃ kīrtayantaś ca yatantaś ca dṛḍhavratāḥ । namasyantaś ca māṃ bhaktyā nityayuktā upāsate ।।

satatatam iti । satataṃ matsvarūpakathane pravṛttacetaso yatantaś ca 
matprāptyupāyeṣu yatnavanto dṛḍhavratāḥ dṛḍhaṃ sthiraṃ
vrataṃ niyamaḥ karmety anarthāntaraṃ tad yeṣāṃ te dṛḍhavratāḥ ।
bhaktyā cādareṇa māṃ namasyantaḥ pādapatanādinā vyāpāreṇa
nityayuktāḥ santa upāsate ।।

anye tu paripakvajñānāḥ 

jñānayajñena cāpy anye yajante mām upāsate । ekatvena pṛthaktvena bahudhā viśvatomukham ।।

jñāneti । jñānam eva yajño jñānayajñaḥ । yajantaḥ pūjayanto mām upāsate । sātatyena parameśvare cittadhāraṇam upāsanam । te caikatvenātmānam idaṃ sarvaṃ vāsudevaḥ sarvam ity anayā buddhyā samastabhedaprapañcaṃ paramakāraṇaparamātmani cetaḥ pravilāpya tadātmanāvatiṣṭhante । te caite brahmavidaḥ śreṣṭhāḥ । anye punar evam asaktāḥ pṛthaktvenopāsate । bahudhā bahubhiḥ prakārair āditye candramasy agnau paramātmānaṃ cintayanti । viśvatomukhaṃ sarvato mukhāni

dvārāṇi yasya taṃ viśvatomukham । yad evālambanatvenopādīyate vakṣyamāṇaṃ tad eva tatprāptyupāyatāṃ pratipadyate ।।

tad idānīṃ prapañcayati 

ahaṃ kratur ahaṃ yajñaḥ svadhāham aham auṣadham । mantro aham aham evājyam aham agnir ahaṃ hutam ।।

ahaṃ kratur iti । ahaṃ kratuḥ paśusomeṣṭilakṣaṇo yajñaḥ smārtaḥ pañcamahāyajñādiḥ । svadhā yat tu pitṝn uddiśya kriyate । aham auṣadhaṃ vrīhyādīnām । idaṃ kim । tad annam । mantro yājyāpuro'nuvākādiḥ । aham evājyaṃ homasādhanam । aham agnir āhavanīyo yatra hūyate । hutaṃ ca havanakriyāham eva ।।

pitāham asya jagato mātā dhātā pitāmahaḥ । vedyaṃ pavitram oṅkāra ṛk sāma yajur eva ca ।।

piteti । pitotpādayitā pālayitā vā । mātā dhātrī dhātā vidhātā । karmaphalānām । pitāmahaḥ pituḥ pitā cāham eva । yad vedyaṃ jñeyaṃ vastu tad aham । yac ca pavitraṃ pāvanaṃ prāyaścittādi । oṅkāraḥ praṇavaḥ । vedatrayaṃ cāham eva ।।

gatir bhartā prabhuḥ sākṣī nivāsaḥ śaraṇaṃ suhṛt । prabhavaḥ pralayasthānaṃ nidhānaṃ bījam avyayam ।।

gatir iti । gamyata iti gatir gantavyo aham । bhartā poṣṭā । prabhuḥ svāmī । draṣṭā pratyakṣaparokṣakṛtānāṃ karmaṇām । nivāsaḥ prāṇinām । nivasanty asminn iti nivāsaḥ । śaraṇam ārtānām । suhṛd upakārī pratyupakārānapekṣayā । prabhavo jagataḥ pralayaḥ sthānaṃ

sthitihetuḥ । nidhīyate asmiñ chreya iti nidhānam । bījam utpattikāraṇam । avyayaṃ vyayarahitam । vrīhyādibījaṃ vyayi ।।

kiṃ ca 

tapāmy ahaṃ ahaṃ varṣa nigṛhṇāmy utsṛjāmi ca । amṛtaṃ caiva mṛtyuś ca sad asac cāham arjuna ।।

tapāmīti । ādityātmanā sthitvā nidāghasamaye tapāmi kaiścid raśmibhiḥ । prāvṛṭkāle varṣam utsṛjāmi । kaiścit kiraṇair nigṛhṇāmy anyartāv aham evāmṛtaṃ jīvanam । mṛtyuś ca vināśaḥ sad asac cāham arjuna । sad iti sthūlaṃ vyavahārayogyaṃ vastu vyapadiśyate । asad iti sūkṣmam avyaktam avyavahāryam । evaṃ madvyatiriktaṃ kim api nāsti । santaḥ samyagdarśina ekatvenākāmā viśvatomukham avasthitaṃ mām upāsate । 
apare akāmāḥ kratvādyekaikapratipattyā bahudhā
pṛthaktvenopāsata
iti saṅkṣepārthaḥ ।।

ye punar jñānayajñenopāsate pṛthaktvenaikatvena vā kevalakarmiṇaḥ phalalubdhāḥ 

traividyā māṃ somapāḥ pūtapāpā yajñair iṣṭvā svargatiṃ prārthayante । te puṇyam āsādya surendralokam aśnanti divyān divi devabhogān ।।

traividyeti । tisro vidyā yeṣāṃ te traividyāḥ । svārthe taddhitaḥ । vedatrayavihitakarmāṇa ity arthaḥ । somapās tata eva pūtapāpāḥ saṃśodhitakalmaṣā yajñair iṣṭvā mām evendrādirūpeṇāvasthitaṃ vastuto na punas te jānanti svargatiṃ svargagamanam । te puṇyaṃ puṇyakarmasādhyaṃ śatakratoḥ sthānaṃ bhuñjanti divyān anubhavanti bhogān ।।

te ca 

te taṃ bhuktvā svargalokaṃ viśālaṃ kṣīṇe puṇye martyalokaṃ viśanti । evaṃ trayīdharmam anuprapannā gatāgataṃ kāmakāmā labhante ।।
te tam iti । bhukteṣu bhogeṣu punaḥ kṣīṇapuṇyāḥ puṇyakṣaye
martyalokaṃ praviśanti । evam ity uktaparāmarśaḥ । hiśabdo hetau । 
trayīdharmaṃ vedatrayavihitaṃ karma prapannā jāyante mriyante ।
kāmān bhogān kāmayamānāḥ ।।

ye tu 

ananyāṃś cintayanto māṃ ye janāḥ paryupāsate । teṣāṃ nityābhiyuktānāṃ yogakṣemaṃ vahāmy aham ।।

ananyāṃś cintayanto mām iti । na vidyate anya upāsyo yeṣāṃ te ananyāḥ । teṣāṃ nityābhiyuktānām aham eva yogakṣemaṃ vahāmi । aprāptaprāptir yogaḥ । kṣemaḥ prāptasya parirakṣaṇam । tad ubhayam ।।

kiṃ ca 

ye apy anyadevatābhaktā yajante śraddhayānvitāḥ । te apy mām eva kaunteya yajanty avidhipūrvakam ।।

ye apīti । ye apy anyadevatābhaktā yajante śraddhayānvitāḥ । yajante pūjayanti ca । te api mām eva vastuto yajanti । kiṃ tv avidhipūrvakam । muktimārgavidhirahitam ity arthaḥ । na punaḥ kalpasūtroktaṃ vidhipūrvakam । vidhiṃ te na jānanti ।।

kutaḥ punar evam 

ahaṃ hi sarvayajñānāṃ bhoktā ca prabhur eva ca । na tu mām abhijānanti tattvenātaś cyavanti te ।।
ahaṃ hīti । ahaṃ hi sarvayajñānām tena tenendrādyātmanāvasthito
bhoktā ca prabhur eva ca । te punar na tu mām abhijānanti tattvena tathāvasthitam । ataś cyavanti te । punarāvṛttiṃ bhajanta ity arthaḥ ।।

etad eva darśayati 

yānti devavratā devān pitṝn yānti pitṛvratāḥ । bhūtāni yānti bhūtejyā yānti madyājino api mām ।।

yāntīti । yānti devavratāḥ । devānāṃ karma vratam yeṣāṃ te । yathā kratur asmiṃl loke puruṣo bhavati tathetaḥ pretya bhavati

iti śruteḥ । taṃ yathā yaś copāsate iti ca brāhmaṇam । nigadavyākhyā । ata eva । sarve māṃ yājinaḥ vāsudevā bhavanti ।।

sāphalyam anena paṭha sādhyatvāt ārādhanīyaḥ ।

katham 

patraṃ puṇyaṃ phalaṃ toyaṃ yo me bhaktyā prayacchati । tad ahaṃ bhaktyupahṛtam aśnāmi prayatātmanaḥ ।।

patraṃ puṣpam iti । vilvādipatram । puṣpaṃ karavīrādi । badarāmrādi phalam । kṛtārthaṃ me janmeti snehārdrahṛdayo yo me prayacchati tad aham upahṛtaṃ gṛhītvāśnāmi tṛpyāmi śraddhābuddheḥ ।।

yata evam ataḥ 

yat karoṣi yad aśnāsi yaj juhoṣi dadāsi yat । yat tapasyasi kaunteya tat kuruṣva madarpaṇam ।।

yad iti । yat karoṣi snānādi । yad aśnāsi bhojanakāle । prāṇāhutiḥ homo nirdiśyate । yaj juhoṣi bāhye agnau dadāsi hiraṇyādi । yat tapasyasy upavāsādi karoṣi । tat sarvaṃ madarpaṇaṃ kuru ।।

śruṇu tataḥ phalam 

śubhāśubhaphalair evaṃ mokṣyase karmabandhanaiḥ । sannyāsayogayuktātmā vimukto mām upaiṣyasi ।।

śubheti । śubhāśubhāni phalāni yeṣāṃ karmabandhanānām । karmāṇy eva bandhanāni । tair vimucyase । vimuktaś ca sannyāsayogayuktātmā । sannyāsaḥ kṛtānāṃ karmaṇāṃ brahmaṇi samarpaṇam । tad eva

kartṛkarmaphalaṃ cety abhedabhāvanā yogaḥ । tābhyāṃ yukta ātmā yasyāsau sannyāsayogayuktātmā mām upeṣyasi ।।

nanu yas tvayi samarpaṇaṃ karoti sa eva cet tvām upaiti rāgādimāṃs tarhi bhavān yathā loke rājā bhajamānasyopakaroti netarasyety āśaṅkyāha 

samohaṃ sarvabhūteṣu na me dveṣyo asti na priyaḥ । ye bhajanti tu māṃ bhaktyā mayi te teṣu cāpy aham ।।

samoham iti । samohaṃ sarvabhūteṣu na me rāgadveṣau । yo bhaktyā māṃ bhajate tasyānugrahaṃ kartuṃ mama svabhāvaḥ yathāgniḥ samyag bhajamānasya śītādyapanodaṃ karoti netarasya । ato ye bhajanti tu bhaktyā sevante mām āśrayante teṣv ahaṃ varte । nātra rāgadveṣau kāraṇam । api tu prāṇikarmānurūpaphalapradarśanenāgnivadanugṛhṇāmīty abhiprāyaḥ ।।

idānīṃ vṛttādinirākaraṇenāpi bhagavadāśrayaṇastutyartham arthavādakathanaṃ kriyate । vṛttam apy atra tantram ity āha 

api cet sudurācāro bhajate mām ananyabhāk । sādhur eva sa mantavyaḥ samyag vyavasito hi saḥ ।।
apīti । suṣṭhu bhṛśaṃ ced durācāraḥ so api sādhur eva
mantavyaḥ । kasmāt । samyag vyavasitaḥ suniścitabuddhiḥ sanmārgam āsthito yataḥ । hiśabdo hetau ।।

ayaṃ punaḥ 

kṣipraṃ bhavati dharmātmā śaśvac chāntiṃ nigacchati । kaunteya pratijānīhi na madbhaktaḥ praṇaśyati ।।

kṣipram iti । ṭi pāpakṣayāt । śaśvad iti kriyāviśeṣaṇam nirgacchatīty arthaḥ । tad etad vastu pratijānīhi । na me bhaktaḥ praṇaśyatīti ।।

idānīṃ ye bhajanti tu māṃ bhaktyā iti yad bhagavatsevanaṃ prakrāntaṃ tatra śraddhābhaktibhyāṃ bhagavadvyapāśrayaṇaprarovanārtham apy arthavādam āha 

māṃ hi pārtha vyapāśritya ye api syuḥ pāpayonayaḥ । striyo vaiśyās tathā śūdrās te api yānti parāṃ gatim ।।

mām iti । he pārtha māṃ vyapāśritya viśeṣeṇa śaraṇatvenāśritya ye api pāpayonayo bhavanti । pāpād yonir janma yeṣāṃ te pāpayonayaḥ kutsitajanmānaḥ stryādayo ye atyantam apavarge anadhikṛtās te api svakarmānuṣṭhānalakṣaṇena madājñāsampādanena pāpakṣayāt paramāṃ prakṛṣṭām uttamāṃ svargalakṣaṇāṃ gatiṃ yānti prāpnuvantīti sambhāvyate । matsamparko hi śuddhikāraṇam analasamparka iva lauhasya । svakarmaṇā māṃ sevasveti । svakarmaṇaivārādhanasya vidhānāt 
pratyutthānātmakaṃ karma śūdrasyāpi svabhāvajam iti pratyutthānena
paricaryātmakena svakarmaṇā tam evārthasiddhiṃ vindati mānava iti ।
tadanuṣṭhānenaiva puruṣārthasiddher vidhāsyamānatvāt ।।

arthavādatātparyam upasaṃharann āha 

kiṃ punar brāhmaṇāḥ puṇyā bhaktā rājarṣayas tathā । anityam asukhaṃ lokam imaṃ prapya bhajasva mām ।।

kim iti । bhagavaccharaṇagatā anadhikṛtāḥ stryādayo apy utkṛṣṭāṃ gatiṃ gacchanti । kiṃ punar ye śuddhayonayo adhikṛtā brāhmaṇarājarṣayaś ca te na yāsyantīti । apiśabdena sambhāvanārthenātiśayoktyā brāhmaṇādīnāṃ jñānaprarocanānena kriyate na tu yathāśruto artho vidhīyate । yathā api parvataṃ śirasā bhindyāt api droṇapākaṃ bhuñjīta ity anena vākyena puruṣaśaktiśraddhānaṃ kriyate na tu parvatabhedaḥ pratipādyata aśakyatvāt । na hi parvataṃ bhindyād ity asyānyaparatvāt svārthātātparyāt tatra pravṛttiḥ । na hi vidhivihitasyārthasya stutyā droṇapākasya pratiṣiddhasya duṣṭasya nindayā nivṛttiḥ । na tu viṣabhakṣaṇalakṣaṇaṃ svārthaṃ pratipādyate । ataś ca jaiminir arthavādalakṣaṇasūtraṃ praṇītavān vidhinā tv ekavākyatvāt stutyarthena vidhīnāṃ syur iti । arthavādāḥ kila vidhyekavākyatayā vidhiśeṣatvena niṣedhaśeṣatvena ca tatstutyarthās tannindārthā vā bhaveyur ity arthaḥ । arthavādavākyānāṃ padārthatvāt svārthe ca tātparyābhāvād anyaparatvāc ceti । tathā ca bhaṭṭapādair evoktam 

vyākhyeyād guṇavādena yo arthavādād atatparāt । arthe adhigantum iṣyeta kathaṃ syāt tasya satyatā ।। iti ।

tathā ca śrutau paśuyāge vapāhomaḥ kartavya iti । asya vidher avaśyānuṣṭhānāyārthavādavākyam prajāpatir vapām udakhidata

ityādi । tasyāyam arthaḥ evaṃ nāma yajamānenāvaśyaṃ vapāhomaḥ kartavya iti । yad uktaṃ paśvantarābhāve prajāpatinā svātmana eva vāpam utkhidya vapāhomo anuṣṭhita iti paśuyāgavidher avaśyakartavyatve vapotkhananam adhyāropitaṃ prarocanārtham । loke apy anabhipretaduṣṭapuruṣagṛhabhojananivṛttyarthaṃ kaścid bravīti varaṃ viṣaṃ bhakṣya mā cāsya gṛhe bhuṅkthā iti anenāpi laukikenārthavādavākyena na viṣabhakṣaṇalakṣaṇaḥ svārtho vidhīyata api tu atiśayoktyā tad gehabhojananivṛttiḥ kriyate । niṣiddha ।
